shuxue \n \n shuxue shi liyong fuhao yuyan yanjiu shuliang 、 jiegou 、 bianhua yiji kongjian deng gainian de yi men xueke ， cong mouzhong jiaodu kan shuyu xingshi kexue de yi zhong 。shuxue touguo chouxianghua he luoji tuili de shiyong ， you jishu 、 jisuan 、 liangdu he dui wuti xingzhuang ji yundong de guancha er chansheng 。shuxuejiamen tuozhan zhexie gainian ， weile gongshihua xin de caixiang yiji cong xuanding de gongli ji dingyi zhong jianli qi yanjin tuidao chu de dingli 。\n \n jichu shuxue de zhishi yu yunyong zongshi geren yu tuanti shenghuo zhong bukehuoque de yi huan 。dui shuxue jiben gainian de wanshan ， zao zai gu aiji 、 meisuo bu da miya ji gu yindu nei de gudai shuxue wenben bian ke guanjian ， er zai gu xila nali you gengwei yanjin de chuli 。cong nashi kaishi ， shuxue de fazhan bian chixubuduan di xiaofu jinzhan ， zhi 16shiji de wenyi fuxing shiqi ， yinwei xin de kexue faxian he shuxue gexin liangzhe de jiaohu ， zhishi shuxue de jiasu fazhan ， zhizhi jinri 。shuxue bing chengwei xuduo guojia ji diqu de jiaoyu fanchou zhong de yibufen 。\n \n jinri ， shuxue shiyong zai butong de lingyu zhong ， baokuo kexue 、 gongcheng 、 yixue 、 jingjixue he jinrongxue deng 。shuxue dui zhexie lingyu de yingyong tongchang bei chengwei yingyong shuxue ， youshi yi hui jiqi xin de shuxue faxian ， bing daozhi quanxin xueke de fazhan ， liru wulixue de shizhixing fazhan zhong jianli de mouxie lilun jifa shuxuejia duiyu mouxie wenti de butong jiaodu de sikao 。shuxuejia ye yanjiuchun shuxue ， jiushi shuxue benshen de shizhixing neirong ， er bu yi renhe shiji yingyong wei mubiao 。suiran xuduo yanjiu yichun shuxue kaishi ， dan qi guocheng zhong ye faxian xuduo yingyong zhi chu 。\n \n xifang yuyan zhong “ shuxue ” （ ） yi ci yuanziyu guxilayu de （ ） ， qi you “ xuexi ” 、 “ xuewen hui bei yonglai zhi\ " shuxue de \" 。qi zai yingyu zhong biaomian shang de fushu xingshi ， ji zai fayu zhong de biaomian fushu xingshi ' ， kesu zhi ladingwen de zhongxing fushu ' ， you xisai luoyi gengjinyibu ze xuyao xiezuo huo qita ke jilu shuzi de xitong ， ru fumu huo yu yinjiadi guonei yonglai chucun shuju de qipu 。lishi shang ceng you guo xuduo butong de jishu xitong 。\n \n zai zuichu you  zhexue \n \n zhexue （ ） shi yanjiu pubian de 、 genben de wenti de xueke ， baokuo cunzai 、 zhishi 、 jiazhi 、 lizhi 、 xinling 、 yuyan deng lingyu 。zhexue yu qita xueke de butong shi qi pipan de fangshi 、 tongchang shi xitonghua de fangfa ， bing yi lixing lunzheng wei jichu 。zai richang yongyu zhong ， qi ye ke bei yinshen wei geren huo tuanti de zui jiben xinyang 、 gainian huo taidu 。\n \n yingyu ciyu （ ） yuanyu guxilayu zhong de ， yisi wei 「 ai zhihui 」 ， youshi ye yiwei 「 zhihui de pengyou 」 ， gai ci you （ philos ， ai ） de paishengci （ Philein ， qu ai ） he （ Sophia ， zhihui ） zuhe er cheng 。yiban renwei ， gu xila sixiangjia bidagelasi zuixian zai zhuzuo zhong yinru “ zhexuejia ” he “ zhexue ” zhe liang ge shuyu 。\n \n “ zhe ” yi ci zai zhongguo qiyuan hen zao ， ru “ kongmen shi zhe ” ， “ gusheng xianzhe ” deng ci ， “ zhe ” huo “ zheren ” ， zhuanzhi naxie shanyu sibian ， xuewen jingshenzhe ， ji xifang jinshi “ zhexuejia ” ， “ sixiangjia ” zhi wei 。zai 《 yijing 》 dangzhong yijing kaishi taolun zhexue wenti ， xingershangxue de zhongwen mingcheng quzi 《 yijing·xici shang chuan 》 「 xinger shangzhe wei zhi dao ， xinger xiazhe weizhiqi 」 yi yu 。1874nian ， riben qimeng jia xizhou ， zai 《 bai yi xinlun 》 zhong shouxian yong hanwen 「 zhexue 」 lai fanyi \"philosophy \"yici 。\n \n yingguo zhexuejia luosu dui zhexue de dingyi shi ： \n\n hushi zai 《 zhongguo zhexueshi dagang 》 zhong cheng 「 fan yanjiuren shengqie yao de wenti ， cong genben shang zhuoxiang ， yao xun yige genben de jiejue ： zhezhong xuewen jiaozuo zhexue 」 。\n \n suiran zhexue yuanzi xifang de chuantong ， dan xuduo wenming zai lishi shangdou cunzai zhu yixie xiangsi de lunti 。dongya he nanya de zhexue bei chengzhiwei dongfang zhexue ， er beifei he zhongdong ze yinwei qi he ouzhou miqie de hudong ， yinci chang bei shiwei shi xifang zhexue de yi bufen 。\n \n dui zhexue de zhuti yi cunzai xuduo kanfa 。yixie ren renwei zhexue shi dui wenti benshen guocheng de shencha ； lingwai yixie ren ze renwei shizhishang cunzai zhu zhexue bixu qu huida de zhexue mingti 。\n \n \n gu xila zhexuejia touguo wen wenti lai jinxing zhexue shijian ， tamen suo ti de wenti dagai keyi guilei wei sanlei ， zhe sanlei wenti fenbie xingcheng le zhexue de jichu xueke —— fenbie shi xingershangxue 、 lunlixue 、 renshilun （ huo zhishilun ） 。\n \n youyisi de shi ， xiandai zhexue shang mengxian chu \" bu yaoqiu jingque liyou \" de zhexue lundiao ， ru \" benzhi jiqiao \" ( rending benzhi buke zhi) ， zhezhong xianxiang jiang buke zhilun ( shijie shang zhongjiu youren bu neng lijie de cunzai ) de zhongyaoxing tigao le 。\n \n zhexue keyi fenwei henduo butong de fenzhi ， zhuyao baokuo xingershangxue 、 zhishilun 、 lunlixue 、 luojixue he meixue 。\n \n \n henduo renlei shequn sikao guo zhexue wenti bingqie huxiang xuexi jianli baihuaqifang ， qizhong zui zhuming de baokuo fojiao chuangshiren shijia mounifu 、 qi na jiao chuangshiren fa tuomo na 、 aqiduo·chishe qinpoluo 、 bojutuo·jiazhanyan 、 fulanna·jiaye 、 shulunpai deng 。\n bolatuzhuyizhe baokuo kusa de nigula ， haiyou zhihou de maerxiliao·feiqinuo he ruowang·pike·dela·milanduola 。\n \n wenyi fuxing ye chongxin chansheng le dui fanya lishiduode de ba ziran kanzuo yige zhexue zhong zheyang de yundong yu dui shenmizhuyi 、 mofa 、 heermosizhuyi haiyou zhan xingxue deng xingqu zhongran xiang qihe ， tamen bei renwei yincang zhe shouhuo zhishi he zhangkong ziran fangfa de damen 。\n \n zhexie xin de zhexue yundong bansui zhe ouzhou zongjiao he zhengzhi de jubian tongshi chuxian ： zongjiao gaige he fengjianzhi de shuailuo 。suiran canyu zongjiao gaige de shenxuejiamen dui zhexue meiyou zhijie de xingqu ， tamen dapo le shenxue he zhishi quanwei de chuantong jichu 。tongshi hai bansui zhe xinyangzhuyi he huaiyizhuyi de fuxing ， tixian zai yilasimo ， mengtainie he deng sixiangjia shenshang 。tongshi ， minzu guojia zhengzhi shang zhubu de zhongyang jiquan de guocheng dedao le shisu zhengzhi zhexue de xiangying ， runikeluo·majiya weili （ chang bei miaoshu wei diyi ge xiandai zhengzhi sixiangjia ， huozheshi xiandai zhengzhi sixiang xingcheng de guanjiandian ） 、 tuomasi·moer 、 yilasimo 、 yousitusi·lipuxiusi 、 rang·bodan he huguo·gelaoxiusi deng de zhuzuo 。\n \n xianqin zhuzi zhihou de lianghan jingxue 、 weijin xuanxue deng dou shi zhongguo zhexue de yi bufen ， zi tangchao qi fojiao ye kaishi dui zhexue chansheng zhongyao yingxiang ； buguo zhongshiji zhongguo zhexue zui zhuyao de bufen shi songminglixue de fazhan 。\n \n songming lixue fandui handai hou kaishi yingxiang ruxue de daojiao he fojiao zhong de mixin he shenmi de yuansu ， shi yi gu changdao gengjia lixing he shisuhua ruxue de zhexue yundong 。jinguan lixue zaodao daojiao he fojiaotu de piping ， lixue reng jiejian le tamen liang ge de bufen shuyu he gainian 。raner he fojiao he daojiao ba xingershangxue kanzuo xinling fazhan 、 zongjiao qishi de cuihuaji bingqie shi buxiu de butong ， songming lixue ba xingershangxue dangzuo jianli yige lixing de lunli tixi de zhidao 。songming lixue de qiyuan keyi zhuisu dao tangchao ： hanyu he liao bei shiwei song dailixue de xianqu 。song dailixuejia zhoudunyi yidao jiaoxing er shangxue lilun wei kuangjia jianli le ta de lunli zhexue tixi ， ta bei kanzuo shi songminglixue de chuangshiren 。\n \n zai dongya de qita difang ， riben zhexue xingcheng yu bentu de shendao xinyang he fojiao 、 rujia yiji ling yixie zhongguo zhexue he yindu zhexue xuepai hunhe fazhan 。yu riben leisi ， zai zhongwujiao de qingxuhua neirong bei hunhe dao le cong zhongguo chuanru de lixue dangzhong 。\n \n zhu tiaomu ： jindai zhexue \n \n xifang zhexueshi shang de jindai zaoqi yiban zhi17 shiji he 18shiji ， qizhong 18shiji chang bei chengwei qimeng shidai 。xiandai zhexue butongyu qi qianshen ， ta he chuantong quanwei liru jiaohui 、 xueyuan 、 yalishiduode de guanxi gengjia duli ， chuxian le dui zhishi jichu he xingershangxue tixi jianshe de xin xingqu ； he baituo le ziran zhexue de jindai wulixue de chuxian 。cong 17shiji kaishi ， jindai zhexue jiu yi renshi lunwei yanjiu zhongdian 。youyu jingyanlun （ jingyanzhuyi ） yu weililun （ lixingzhuyi ） de zhenglun ， shi wuzhi yu jingshen de guanxi zuowei renshilun de shouyao wenti tuxian chulai 。\n dangshi qita de zhengzhi zhexue de shisu jichu \n 。zhezhong chaoliu zui zao bei xianming di tixian zai fulanxisi·peigen de bei chengwei yonglai kuozhan zhishi de xin de 、 jingyanzhuyi de chengxu ， bing henkuai zai ziran lai weiren fuwu 。\n \n jinxiandai zhengzhi zhexue de bizutuomasi·huobusi zuizao jiang zhe taofang falun xitong de yingyong zai zhengzhi zhexue shang ， baokuo \" shehui qiyue \" de jindai lilun 。zaoqi jindai zhexue de xueshu jingdian yiban baokuo dikaer 、 sibinnuosha 、 laibunici 、 luoke 、 beikelai 、 xiumo he kangde 。tongshi qi de qita sixiangjia ye dui zhexue zuochu le gongxian ， liru jialilve 、 piaier·gasangdi 、 bulaizi·pasika 、 malebo langshi 、 aisake·niudun 、 、 mengdesijiu 、 、 tuomasi·lide 、 rang·leilang·dalangbeier he yadang·simi ， er rang - yake·lusuo shi fanqimeng yundong de kaichuangxing renwu 。zaoqi jindai zhexue de dazhi jieshu tongchang bei queding wei yimannuer·kangde de shitu xianding xingershangxue fanwei 、 zhengming kexue zhishi bingyong daode he ziyou laidiao he zhengge jingyuan zhexue yiji zai ta nage shidai liuxing de jiaoyu yu zhexue tixi jiayi fengci 。qi renwei “ wo sigu wo zai ” shi renshilun de wuke huaiyi zhi chufadian 。di kaer shi gelie jingshen he wuzhi de eryuan lunzhe ， weile liqing erzhe guanxi ， ta jianding renwei zai shangdi nali ， jingshen he wuzhi shi tongyi de 。qi lilun bei chengwei di kaerzhuyi \n 。sibin nuosha shi dikaer zhihou ， you shuxing \n 。laibunici zuowei weili lunzhe jianding di weihu dikaer de xueshuo bing fanbo yuehan·luoke de lilun 。yu dikaer butong de shi ， ta renwei wanwu de shiti shi “ danzi ” ， qie huxiang meiyou guanxi ， ershi youyu “ qianding hexie ” cai gongcun yiti ， ji cunzai yushen zhizhong 。“ qianding hexie ” tiaohe le di kaerzhier yuanlun he sibinnuosha zhi shiti shuangchongxing 。\nluoke fazhan le jingyanlun ， ta bu rentong dikaer de “ tianfu guannian ” ， tichu baiban shuo ， ta qiangdiao renmen cong ganjue zhong chouxiang chu pubian de gainian ， renwei ganjue zhong de gebie dongxi cai shi diyi wei de 。buguo ta jiben rentong dikaer de eryuan lun 。beikelai fazhan le luoke de zhexue lilun ， tichu le “ cunzai jiushi bei ganzhi ” 。ta renwei chule ganzhi de zhuti he bei ganzhi de zhijue zhiwai ， shenme ye meiyou 。ta feichang bu zantong wuzhi de chouxiang gainian ， renwei qi ji wu keguan shizai ， ye bu neng cunzai yu renxin 。dawei·xiumo de lilun bi beikelai de gengjinyibu ， ta bujinjin renwei wuzhi shiti bu cunzai ， geng renwei jingshen shiti bu cunzai 。zhi chengren zhijue de cunzai 。ta hai yi ziji de buke zhilun he huaiyilun renwei bu cunzai tongyixing he pubianxing de dongxi ， rending duoyangxing he gebiexing cai shi zui gao yuanli 。\n \n jingyan lun yu weililun de zhenglun ye baohan le weiwuzhuyi yu weixinzhuyi de zhenglun 。zai 18 shiji shi ， faguo de lamei teli gongkai xuanbu weiwuzhuyi shi weiyi de ， er baikequanshu de zhubiandeni·dideluo ye jujue chengren shen de cunzai 。\n \n lingwai fuertai ， mengdesijiu he qita baikequan shupai de xuezhe dou you sheji zhengzhi he bukeyuyue ， ren de siwei shi ren ganguan de jieguo 。buguo tamen rengran shi jingyanzhuyizhe ， zai yinguoxing shang ， tamen renwei zhiyou biranxing cai shi weiyi de ， zhejiu chengwei weixinzhuyi de yanjiu hexin jiushi guiding lixing neng zuo shenme yiji bu neng zuo shenme 。\n \n kangde tongyi xiumo de lilun bing renwei ， cunzai yixie yuanze ， shide xinling dui jingyan he renshi jiayi zuzhi ， er xiangying de jiegou ： \n\n \n ta hai wei daode zhexue dianding le xin jichu ， qie ta fuyu le ziyou gainian de xin yiyi 。yinwei qi yingxiang zai xiandai yijiu shangcun ， qi lilun bei renmen chengwei kangdezhuyi 。\nfeixite benlai chengren sibinnuosha de jixie de yinguo juedinglun ， dan houlai shoudao kangde de yingxiang ， kaishi renwei yinguo jueding lunzhi shi biaomian ， qishi zhiwei ziwo bushi biranxing de nupu ershi duli ziyou de zhuti 。jiuci ， ta jianli le zhuguan de siwei yu keguan de cunzai zhi tongyi shuo 。\n \n xielin shi cong feixite lilun chufa de ， dan shenshou sibinnuosha he wenxue shang langmanzhuyi de yingxiang ， chuangli le ziji de xueshuo 。ji ta renwei ziran he jingshen 、 cunzai he siwei ， keti he zhuti ， biaomian xiangfan ， shize tongyi ， shi tongyige “ juedui ” de butong fazhan jieduan ， zhege “ juedui ” ji shi wanshiwanwu de genyuan 。ta renwei yishu cai shi zui zhiguan de lixing 。\n heigeer jiqi lilun de chuxian jiang xifang zhexue de tuishang yige xin gaodu ， ta chuangli le xifang zhexueshi shang zui pangda de keguan weixinzhuyi tixi ， bing xitong di chanshu le bianzhengfa 。ta de lilun he xueshuo dui jinxiandai zhexue chansheng le hen shenyuan de yingxiang ， bing bei chengwei heigeerzhuyi 。\n \n cong heigeer de sixiang tixi zhong fazhan er cheng de duozhong zhexue yundong 。qi zhongdian jiushi yi lishi he luoji weizhu ， lishi fangmian ， ta cong butong jiaodu lijie “ fanshi heli de jiushi xianshi de ” ； luoji fangmian ， ta you faxian qizhong suo shuo de “ zhenli ji zhengti ” 。\n \n heigeer renwei zhexue de zhongdian shi fangqi fenlie ， dadao tongyi 。ta ba yiqian de shidai shuocheng shi siwei yu cunzai 、 lixiang yu xianshi fenlie ， ziyou yu biran ， geren yu shehui 、 wuxian yu youxian 、 tongyixing yu duoyangxing fenlie zhi shidai 。\n \n ta cong kangde de “ xinling de helixing yiji zai jingyan zhong de jiji zuoyong ” de gainian chufa ， dan fandui kangde de “ chaoyue jingyan shijie he ‘wu zishen ’ de shijie ” ， bing renwei xinling he shijie yiyang juyou xiangtong jichu lixing jiegou 。ta suo renwei de pubianxing bushi tuoli teshu de chouxiang pubian ， ershi baohan teshu zainei zhi pubian ， ji wei juti pubian ； ta suo renwei de tongyi ye fei tuoli maodun 、 duili de chouxiang tongyi ， ershi baohan tamen zainei de tongyi ， ji wei duili tongyi 。shangshu zonghe zaiyiqi ji shi ta de lilun ： zui zhenshi de wusuobubao de zhengti ji shi “ juedui jingshen ” ， you shi duili de tongyi 。\n \n ta renwei ， weile dadao zhege “ juedui jingshen ” ， xuyao jingguo san ge jieduan ， cong luoji 、 ziran dao jingshen ， ji shi cong siwei dao cunzai ， zai dao liangzhe tongyi de guocheng ， conger wancheng ta de tongyilun 。\n \n jiuci ， shehui he lishi de xianxiang ， bian bei fuyu yi zhong zai zhexueshi shang haishi zhanxin de xianhe diwei 。ta hai jiang lunli xuehua guidao zhege lingyu ， conger zai lunlixue lilun he dui sixiang de lijie zhong tichu zhongyao de luxian 。\n \n cong 19shiji zhongye kaishi ， xifang zhexue jiu jinru xiandai zhexue jieduan 。yinwei zai 19 shiji zhongqi ， ouzhou de gongye geming jijin wancheng 。\n \n xiandai zhexue ， tebieshi 19 shiji zhonghouqi de zhexue liupai ， youshu benhua de yizhizhuyi ， xin kangdezhuyi ， suo fazhan chu de 「 fenxi zhexue 」 chengwei fengge jiongyi de liang da xifang zhexue dianfan 。\n \n 20 shiji de xifang zhexue shang zhuliu you liang tiao ： \n\n xiandai zhexue zhuyao baohan yixia ji ： \n\n weixinzhuyi de gezhong bianti zai 18 shiji wanqi zhi 20 shiji zaoqi de zhexuejie xiangdang liuxing 。kangde zhuzhang de xianyan weixinzhuyi renwei renmen dui shiwu de lijie shi you jiexian de ， yinwei zai keguan panduan tiaojian xia henduo shiqing shi ban bu dao de 。ta zai 1781nian faxing de zuopin 《 chuncui lixing pipan 》 shitu tiaohe 18 shiji liang da zhuyao de zhexue paibie ： jingyanzhuyi he lixingzhuyi ， bingqie jianli yige yanjiu xingershangxue de xin jichu 。\n \n deguo weixinzhuyi zui zhuming de zuopin shi heigeer yu 1807nian chuban de 《 jingshen xianxiangxue 》 。heigeer chengren ziji de linian bushi xin de ， buguo ta de mubiao shi wancheng zhiqian de zhexuejiamen de bu wanzheng de tixi 。heigeer renwei zhexue de zhongdian shi fangqi fenlie ， dadao tongyi 。ta ba yiqian de shidai shuocheng shi siwei yu cunzai 、 lixiang yu xianshi fenlie ， ziyou yu biran 、 geren yu shehui 、 wuxian yu youxian 、 tongyixing yu duoyangxing fenlie zhi shidai 。ta cong kangde de “ xinling de helixing yiji zai jingyan zhong de jiji zuoyong ” de gainian chufa ， dan fandui kangde de “ chaoyue jingyan shijie he ‘wu zishen ’ de shijie ” ， bing renwei xinling he shijie yiyang juyou xiangtong jichu lixing jiegou 。ta suo renwei de pubianxing bushi tuoli teshu de chouxiang pubian ， ershi baohan teshu zainei zhi pubian ， ji wei juti pubian ； ta suo renwei de tongyi ye fei tuoli maodun 、 duili de chouxiang tongyi ， ershi baohan tamen zainei de tongyi ， ji wei duili tongyi 。shangshu zonghe zaiyiqi ji shi ta de lilun ： zui zhenshi de wusuobubao de zhengti ji shi “ juedui jingshen ” ， you shi duili de tongyi 。heigeer renwei xuyao jingguo san ge jieduan lai dadao zhege “ juedui jingshen ” ， cong luoji 、 ziran dao jingshen ， ji shi cong siwei dao cunzai ， zai dao liangzhe tongyi de guocheng ， conger wancheng ta de tongyilun 。ta hai jiang lunli xuehua guidao zhege lingyu ， conger zai lunlixue lilun he dui sixiang de lijie zhong tichu zhongyao de luxian 。\n makesizhuyi zhexue shi makesi he engesi jianli de yi bianzheng weiwuzhuyi wei hexin de zhexue tixi 。qi renwei shijian shi jianyan zhexue zhi zhenlixing de zuizhong biaozhun ， zhexue ying bansui zhe shehui 、 kexue jishu he wenhua de fazhan er buduan fazhan 。qi zhuyao sixiang tixi zai 19shiji 70niandai zhuyao you engesi chuangli ， 20 shiji 20niandai zai sulian xingcheng wanzheng tixi —— bianzheng weiwuzhuyi he lishi weiwuzhuyi ， zhege tixi zai houlai de shehuizhuyi guojia tuidong xia deyi fazhan 。makesizhuyi zhexue xuancheng ziji de lilun tixi juyou kexuexing ， renwei zhexue keyi chengwei kexue de yibufen 。tongshi makesizhuyi zhexue renwei zhexue hai juyou yishi xingtai de xingzhi 。\n \n lingwai makesizhuyi zai zhengzhi shang ye zhi gezhong butong de gongchanzhuyi yundong ， ru you liening suo chuangli er bei sidalin xiugai de sulian makesizhuyi ， chengwei makesi lieningzhuyi ， wei eguo geming yiji houlai jianli de gezhong gongchandang zhi jiaoyi 。ta de pangxi baokuo fansidalin de tuoluociji jiqi zhuisuizhe de makesizhuyi 、 maozedong de makesi lieningzhuyi deng 。\n shiyongzhuyi chansheng yu 19 shiji 70niandai de xiandai zhexue paibie ， zai 20shiji de meiguo chengwei yi zhong zhuliu sichao 。dui falv 、 zhengzhi 、 jiaoyu 、 shehui 、 zongjiao he yishu de yanjiu chansheng le hen da de yingxiang 。shiyongzhuyi ye shitu zai lixingzhuyi ji jingyanzhuyi zhaochu yi tiao zhongjian daolu lai ， shi 「 jingyanzhuyi sixiang fangfa yu renlei de bijiao juyou zongjiaoxing xuyao de shidang de tiaohezhe 。 」\n\n xianxiangxue shi you deguo zhexuejia husaier zai 1900nian tichu de lilun ， qiangdiao dui zhijie zhiguan he jingyan ganzhi de qufen ， renwei zhexue （ huo zhishao shi xianxiangxue ） de zhuyao renwu shi liqing erzhe zhijian de guanlian ， bingqie zai zhiguan zhong huode dui benzhi de renshi 。xianxiangxue shi dui jingyan jiegou yu yishi jiegou de zhexuexing yanjiu 。zuowei yige zhexue yundong ， xianxiang xueyu ershi shiji zaoqi you aidemengde·husaier chuangli ， zhihou bei ta zai deguo de geting gen daxue he munihei daxue zhong de yi pai zhuisuizhe fazhan zhuangda 。zai ci zhihou xianxiangxue chuanbo dao faguo 、 meiguo yiji qita diqu ， bing yuan chaochu le husaier zaoqi zhuzuo de yujing 。qita zhuyao zhexuejia baokuo haide ge( Martin Heidegger ) , meiluo— pangdi( Maurice Merleau -Ponty ) , yiji lieweinasi(Emmanuel Lévinas) 。\n \n cunzai zhuyi shi yige zhexue de feilixingzhuyi sichao ， gai shuyu bei yong zai shijiu shiji wanqi dao ershishiji de yixie zhexuejia de gongzuo shang ， jinguan tamen de xueshuo xiangcha juda ， dan tamen dou xiangxin zhexue sikao kaishi yu renlei zhuti —— er bujinjin shi siwei zhuti ， erqie baokuo xingwei 、 ganzhi 、 renlei geti 。cunzai zhuyi qiangdiao geren 、 dulizizhu he zhuguan jingyan ， renwei ren cunzai de yiyi shi wufa jingyou lixing sikao er dedao daan 。zai cunzai zhuyi zhong ， geti de chufadian de tezheng shi bei chengwei “ cunzai de taidu ” ， huo yi zhong miandui xianran shi yige wu yiyi de huo huangmiu de shijie de mishi he hunluan de ganjue 。henduo cunzai zhuyizhe hai renwei chuantong de tixi he zhexue xueshu wulunshi neirong he fengge dou guoyu chouxiang bing yuanli renlei jingyan 。\n \n 19 shiji zhexuejia keerkaiguoer he nicai bei  wenxue \n \n wenxue （ ） ， zai zui guangfan de yiyi shang ， shi renhe danyi de shumian zuopin 。\n \n geng yange di shuo ， wenxue xiezuo bei renwei shi yi zhong yishu xingshi ， huo bei renwei juyou \"littera \" ： \"letter \" huo \" handwriting \" ）bei yonglai zhidai suoyou de shumian jilu ， jinguan dangdai dingyi jiang shuyu kuozhan dao baokuo koutou huo changge de wenben （ koutou wenxue ） 。wenxue keyi genju shi xugou zuopin hai shifei xugou zuopin jinxing fenlei ， ye keyi genju shi yunwen haishi sanwen jinxing fenlei ； keyi genju changpian xiaoshuo 、 zhongpian xiaoshuo 、 duanpian xiaoshuo deng zhuyao xingshi jinyibu qufen ； zuopin wangwang genju lishi shiqi huozhe zunshou mouxie meixue tezheng huo qiwang （ yishu leixing ） jinxing fenlei 。\n \n yi yuyan wenzi wei gongju xingxianghua di fanying xianshi de yishu ， baokuo yunwen 、 sanwen 、 juben 、 xiaoshuo deng ， shi wenhua de zhongyao biaoxian xingshi ， yi butong de liupai biaoxian neixin qinggan he zaixian yiding  lishi \n \n lishi （ xiandai hanyu cihui ， gudian wenyanwen chengzhiweishi ） ， zhi renlei shehui guoqu de shijian he xingdong ， yiji dui zhexie shijian xingwei you xitong de jilu 、 quanshi he yanjiu shijian de jilu he yanjiu ， you cheng lishixue ” ， huo jiancheng “ shixue ” 。lishuyu lishixue huo yuqi miqie xiangguan de xueke you niandaixue 、 bianzuanxue 、 jia puxue 、 gu wenzixue 、 jiliang  jisuanji kexue \n \n jisuanji kexue （ ， youshi suoxie wei ） shi xitongxing yanjiu xinxi yu jisuan de lilun jichu yiji tamen zai jisuanji xitong zhong ruhe yu yingyong de shiyong jishu de xueke 。ta tongchang bei xingrong wei dui naxie chuangzao 、 miaoshu yiji zhuanhuan xinxi de suanfa chuli de xitong yanjiu 。jisuanji kexue baohan henduo fenzhi lingyu ； youxie qiangdiao teding jieguo de jisuan ， biru jisuanji tu xingxue ； er youxie shi tantao jisuan wenti de xingzhi ， biru jisuan fuzaxing lilun ； haiyou yixie lingyu zhuanzhuyu zenyang shixian jisuan ， biru chengshi yuyan lilun shi yanjiu haoyong ， yiji suishi suidi weiren suo yong 。\n \n youshi gongzhong huiwu yiwei jisuanji kexue jiushi jiejue jisuanji wenti de shiye （ biru xinxi jishu ） ， huozhe zhishi yu shiyong jisuanji de jingyan  xiju \n\n xiju shi yanyuan jiang mouge gushi huo qingjing ， yi duihua 、 gechang huo dongzuo deng fangshi suo biaoyan chulai de yishu 。xiju you si ge yuansu ， baokuo le 「 yanyuan 」 、 「 gushi （ qingjing ） 」 、 「 wutai （ biaoyan changdi ） 」 he 「 guanzhong 」 。「 yanyuan 」 shi si zhe dangzhong zui zhongyao de yuansu ， ta shi juese de daiyanren ， bixu jubei banyan de nengli ， xiju yu qita yishulei zui da de butong zhi chu bian zaiyu banyan le ， touguo yanyuan de banyan ， juben zhong de juese cai deyi shenzhang ， ruguo paoqi le yanyuan de banyan ， name suo yanchu de bian bu zai shi xiju 。\n \n jishi zai donghua 、 muouxi 、 piyingxi deng meiyou yanyuan xianshen de xiju zhong ， yanyuan buguo shi yincang zai guanzhong de shijue zhiwai de difang yanchu 。\n \n xiju de biaoyan xingshi duozhongduoyang ， changjian de baokuo huaju 、 geju 、 wuju 、 yinyueju 、 muouxi deng 。youyu wenhua beijing de chabie ， butong wenhua suo chansheng xiju xingshi wangwang yongyou dute de chuantong he chengshi ， biru xifang xiju 、 zhongguo xiqu 、 yindu fanju 、 riben nengle 、 gewuji deng 。\n \n xiju de qiyuan shibukekao ， muqian you duozhong jiashuo 。bijiao zhuliu de kanfa you er ： yi wei yuanshi zongjiao de wushu yishi 。biru zai shanggu hanyu zhong ， “ wu ” 、 “ wu ” 、 “ wu ” san zi keneng tongyuan （ shanggu hanyu niyin fenbie wei ： /* ma / ， /* maʔ / ， /* maʔ / ） 。qi you keneng shi dui yi zhong qiqiu zhandou shengli de wushu huodong de hecheng ， ji xiju de yuanshi xingtai 。ling yi wei laodong huo qingzhu fengshou shi de jixing gewu biaoyan ， zhezhong shuofa zhuyao yiju shi gu xila xiju bei renwei qiyuanyu jiushen jisi 。\n \n xiandai de xiju guannian qiangdiao wutai shangxia suoyou yanchu yuansu tongyi biaoxian yi shixian zonghe de yishu xiaoguo 。yanchu yuansu baokuo yanyuan 、 wutai 、 daoju 、 dengguang 、 yinxiao 、 fuzhuang 、 huazhuang ， yiji juben 、 daoyan deng de yiqie zongcheng ， ye baokuo taishang yanchu yu taixia hudong de guanxi （ yiban chengwei “ guanyan guanxi ” ） 。\n \n wenxue shang de xiju gainian shi zhiwei xiju biaoyan suo chuangzuo de jiaoben ， huo chengzhiwei juben 。\n \n zhongwen xiju yi ci de ziyuan laiziyu 「 nanxi beiju 」 de hecheng ， xizhi de shi xiwen ， yihou cai chuxian de yongfa 。\n \n shijie geguo yuwen zhong yu 「 xiju 」 yi ci jiangjin de cihui nangkuo de fanwei buyi ， liru zai yindu wen zhong de \"lila\ " yi ci chule shi xiju zhiwai ， ye baohan wudao 、 yundong jingsai deng yiyi 。danshi jihu shijie geguo yuwen zhong yu 「 xiju 」 xiangguan de cihui ， jihu jubei yu 「 youxi 」 leisi de yiyi ， liru zai yingwen zhongjiang yi bu juzuo chengwei shi \"play \" （ tongchang zhiyou juben you duibai de xiju ） 。zhongwen zhong 「 xiju 」 de 「 xi 」 ， ye daiyou 「 youxi 」 de yiyi 。\n \n shijie shang san zhong gulao xiju wenhua ， baokuo xila de beiju he xiju 、 yindu de fanju ji zhongguo de xiqu 。\n \n xifang xiju de shuguang ， pubian renwei shi gu xila beiju ， er gu xila beiju ze shi yuanyu guxila yadian chengbang ， zai gongyuanqian 5 shiji ， zai shendai  dianying \n\n dianying shi yi zhong biaoyan yishu 、 shijue yishu ji tingjue yishu ， liyong jiaojuan 、 luyingdai huo shuwei meiti jiang yingxiang he shengyin buzhuo qilai ， zai jiashang houqi de bianji gongzuo er cheng 。dianying zhong kanqilai lianxu de huamian ， shi you yizhenzhen dandu de zhaopian goucheng de ， zhiyu guanyu dianying zhong yundong de ganzhi ， shi yinwei renmen yinwei shijue shang de feixian xiang （ Phi phenomenon ） ， shide dui yilianchuan jingtai tupian que hui zaocheng yidong de cuojue 。chuantong dui dianying zhong yundong ganzhi de lijie shi yinwei shijue zanliu ， shide tuxiang likai hou ， reng neng zai yanjing baoliu 「 shixiang 」 yue shifenzhiyi miao 。yinci danao ganjue dao tuxiang shi 「 yundong 」 de 。dan zai 1916nian chuban de deguo xinlixuejia （ Hugo Münsterberg ） de 《 dianying ： yi ci xinlixue yanjiu 》 zhong disan zhang 《 shendugan he yundonggan 》 zhong ， yuguo·mingsiteboge zhengming le waiguan yundong juebu shi yingxiang zhiliu （ ji shijue zanliu ） de jieguo ， ershi （ dan bujinjin shi ） dui yundong de lianxu jieduan de ganzhi 。\n \n dianying zhizuo benshen shi yishu ye shi 。dianying keyi you dianying sheyingji paishe zhenshi yingxiang zai zhizuo er cheng ， ye keyi liyong chuantong de donghua jiqiao huizhi tuhua zai paishe tuhua er cheng ， shenzhi keyi liyong diannao chengxiang ji jisuanji donghua zhizuo dianying ， ye keyi zai dianying zhong liyong shangshu suoyou de jishu ji qita shijue xiaoguo 。dianying jishu fazhan chuqi you gezhong butong de fangying sudu ， dan xianshi dianying dou duo yi mei miao ershisi getu xiang zuo fangying biaozhun 。\n \n luyisi·pulinsi yu 1888nian 10yue 14ri ， shiyong gaijinban de danjingtou sheyingji （ ji MkII ）paishe le dianying 《 langdehai huayuan changjing 》 。ta zai lizi de hansilai tequ dianyinghui xuyao sannian de shijian ， tou yi nian jiaoben fazhan ， dier nian shi qianqi zhizuo ji dianying zhizuo ， disan nian shi houqi zhizuo ji dianying faxing 。\n \n shi zhi rang yuetingren keyi 。dianying chule zai dianyingyuan gongren guankan wai ， fang zai suixuan shixun shang ， huoshi touguo guangbo lianmai fangshi zuocheng dianshi jiemu 。\n \n qita faxing de fangshi baokuo geren goumai huoshi chuzu dianying de VHS 、 DVD huo languang guangdie ， shi zai hulianwang shang xiazai 。\n \n \n \n 
 yinyue \n\n yinyue ， guangyi eryan ， jiushi zhi renhe yi shengyin zucheng de yishu 。yingwen Music yi ci yuanyu guxilayu de μο υσ ικ ή （ mousike ） ， yijimousi （ muse ） nvshen de yishu 。er zhongwen de yinyue erzi ， xushen 《 shuowen jiezi 》 jieshi wei 「 yin ， sheng ye 。shengyu xin ， you jieyu wai ， wei zhi yin 。 」renwei yinyue he shengyin de qubie ， zaiyu yinyue xuyao touguo renxin qu xiangxiang he chuangzao 。yinyue ke fenwei chuangzuo 、 yanzou 、 lingting san ge guocheng ， zai butong wenhua he shehui ， duiyu yinyue de guocheng jiqi zhongyaoxing dou you butong de lijie 。liru zai xifei guyue li ， meige ren jie shi canyuzhe ， renmen bu hui qufen zuoquzhe 、 yanzouzhe he lingtingzhe de shenfen 。\n \n zhiyu hewei shengyin 、 zaoyin he yinyue de qubie ， meiyou gongren de biaozhun 。yinwei yinyue he shuxue 、 wuli xiangguan ， ouzhou zigu xila shidai kaishi ， youren lunshu yueli 。zai xifang yueli zhong ， yinyue de zhuyao yuansu you yingao （ huo shengyin de pinlv ） 、 jiezou he yinse 。butong de yingao chongdie xingcheng hesheng ， yingao yiju jiezou jinxing chengwei xuanlv ， changyong de yingao xingcheng yinjie he diaoxing ， guilvxing de qiangpai he ruopai xingcheng jiepai ， paizi de kuaiman goucheng sudu 。dan jindai you bushao yinyuejia bu rentong chuantong de lijie ， liru ershishiji meiguo zuoqujia yuehan·kaiji renwei renhe shengyin he jingmo jie shi yinyue 。yinyue keyi fenwei butong zhonglei ， dan mei zhong zhonglei de qubie changchang shi hanhu he ju zhengyi de 。\n \n yinyue keyi yong yuepu miaoshu ， yiju yuepu yanzou ， dan ye you bushao yinyue leixing ru minge huo jueshiyue shi yinyueshi 。lingwai zi shijiushiji mo kaishi you minzu yinyuexue ， yanjiu gedi butong de yinyue wenhua 。\n \n yinyue de yaosu baokuo ： \n\n mei shou butong de yinyue dou shi zhuyao you butong de jiezou he xuanlv lai qufen de ， zhe liang zhong yaosu jueding le yinyue de gexing 。you liang ge yishang de yueqi huo liang ge yishang de ren gongtong yanzou （ yanchang ） de yinyue ， keyi you hesheng xietiao zucheng fudiao yinyue 。mei zhong yueqi he meige rensheng dou you ziji dute de yinse ， butong yinse de yueqi zuhe xingcheng dute de xiaoguo ， anpai zhexie yueqi de zuhe jiaozuo peiqi 。yishang si zhong yaosu de butong zuhe zucheng le mei shou yinyue dute de xingge ， shi ren zai lingting butong yinyue shi neng ganshou dao huankuai 、 beishang 、 kangkai 、 zhenfen deng gezhong qingxu ， neng lijie shi ， yi zhong shengyin fuhao ， biaoda ren de suosi suoxiang 。shi renmen sixiang de zaiti zhiyi 。yinyue shi you mudi de ， shi you neihan de ， qizhong yinhan le zuozhe de shenghuo tiyan ， sixiang qinghuai  jingjixue \n \n jingjixue shi yi men dui chanpin he fuwu de shengchan 、 fenpei yiji xiaofei jinxing yanjiu de shehui kexue 。xifang yuyan zhong de “ jingjixue ” yi ci yuanyu guxila de 。\n \n jingjixue zhuzhong de shi yanjiu jingji xingweizhe zai yige jingji tixi xia de xingwei ， yiji tamen bici zhijian de hudong 。zai xiandai ， jingjixue de jiaocai tongchang jiang zhe men lingyu de yanjiu fenwei zongti jingjixue he geti jingjixue 。weiguan jingjixue jianshi yige shehui li jiben cengci de xingwei ， baokuo geti de xingweizhe （ liru geren 、 gongsi 、 maijia huo maijia ） yiji yu shichang de hudong 。er hongguan jingjixue ze fenxi zhengge jingjiti he qi yiti ， baokuo shiye 、 tonghuopengzhang 、 jingji chengzhang 、 caizheng he huobi zhengce deng 。\n \n qita de duizhao hai baokuo le shizheng jingjixue （ yanjiu 「 shi shenme 」 ） yiji guifan jingjixue （ yanjiu 「 yinggai shi shenme 」 ） 、 jingji lilun yu shiyong jingjixue 、 xingwei jingjixue yu lixing xuanze jingjixue 、 zhuliu jingjixue （ yanjiu lixing - geti - junheng deng ） yu feizhuliu jingjixue （ yanjiu tizhi - lishi - shehui jiegou deng ） 。\n \n jingjixue de fenxi ye bei yong zai qita gezhong lingyu shang ， zhuyao lingyu baokuo le shangye 、 jinrong 、 he zhengfu deng ， dan tongshi ye baokuo le ru jiankang 、 fanzui 、 jiaoyu 、 falv 、 zhengzhi 、 shehui jiagou 、 zongjiao 、 zhanzheng 、 he kexue dengdeng 。dao le 21 shiji chu ， jingjixue zai shehui kexue lingyu ge fangmian buduan kuozhang yingxiangli ， shide youxie xuezhe fengci di cheng qi wei 「 jingjixue diguozhuyi 」 。\n \n zai xiandai duiyu jingjixue de dingyi youshu zhong shuofa ， qizhong you xuduo shuofa yinwei fazhan zi butong de lingyu huo lilun er you jieranbutong de dingyi ， sugelan zhexuejia he jingjixuejia yadang·simi zai 1776nian jiang zhengzhi jingjixue dingyi wei 「 guomin caifu de xingzhi he yuanyin de yanjiu 」 ， ta shuo ： \n\n rang - badisite·saiyi zai 1803nian jiang jingjixue cong gonggong zhengce li duli chulai ， bing dingyi qi wei duiyu caifu zhi shengchan 、 fenpei 、 he xiaofei de xuewen 。lingyifangmian ， tuomasi·kalaier ze fengci de cheng jingjixue wei 「 youyu de kexue 」 （ Dismal science ） ， buguo zhe yi ci zui zao shi you maersasi zai 1798nian tichu 。yuehan·situerte·mier zai 1844nian tichu le yige yi shehui kexue dingyi jingjixue de jiaodu ：\n\n aerfuleide·maxieer ze zai ta 1890nian de 《 jingjixue yuanli 》 yi shu zhongjiang jingjixue fenxi de lingyu cong danchun caifu chuangzao kuozhan chuqu ， bingqie baohan buzhi shi shehui shang 、 tongshi ye shi geti shang de cengci ： \n \n luobinsi jueshi （ Lionel Robbins ） ze zai 1932nian tichu le bei renwei shi 「 dao xianzai yilai zui bei guangfan shiyong de jingjixue dingyi 」 ： \n \n luobinsi renwei ci dingyi zhuzhong de bushi yi jingjixue 「 yanjiu mou yixie xingwei 」 ， ershi yao yi fenxi de jiaodu qu 「 yanjiu xingwei shi ruhe bei ziyuan youxian de tiaojian suo gaibian 」 。yixie ren piping ci dingyi guodu guangfan ， erqie wufa jiang fenxi de fanwei juxian zai duiyu shichang de yanjiu shang 。raner ， zicong 1960niandai qi ， youyu lixing xuanze lilun he qi yinfa de saiju lilun buduan jiang jingjixue de yanjiu lingyu kuozhang ， zhege dingyi yijing huode guangfan jingjixue zhongshi xuqiu yu gongji ， ruhe yingxiang geren ， dacheng jiaoyi ， bing xingcheng shichang zhong de junheng jiage 。\n \n weiguan jingjixue guanzhu renmen de jueding he xingwei yingxiang wupin he fuwu de gongji he xuqiu 、 shui fuze jueding jiage 、 huozhe fanguolai ， jiage zenyang jueding wupin he fuwu de gongjiliang he xuqiuliang 。\n \n weiguan jingjixue de mudi zaiyu touguo fenxi tai zhongshi jingji xiaolv wenti ， yinwei na ke cong guifan jingjixue huode daan 。bujin ruci ， weiguan jingjixue hai fenxi shichang shiling ， jiujing shichang na chu wufa chansheng youxiaolv de jieguo zai shichang shang zhijie jiaoyi ， ershi touguo gongsi jinxing gongzuo he shengchan 。zui mingxian de gongsi shi qiye 、 hehuo 、 yiji xintuo 。yiju luonade·kesi de shuofa ， dang touguo gongsi shengchan de chengben diyu zixing shengchan shi ， geti bian hui xuanze touguo gongsi shengchan 。gongsi zonghe le laodong he ziben ， bingqie keyi dadao bi geren jiaoyi geng gao de guimo jingji （ yejiushishuo ， dang shengchan yige chanpin danwei de chengben suizhu shengchan shuliang de zengjia er jiangdi shi ） 。\n \n zai wanquan jingzheng de yanjiu moxing xia ， shengchanzhe zhongduo ， erqie duiyu shichang jiage dou meiyou juedingxing de yingxiang 。chanye zuzhi yanjiu de ze shi dang mouxie shengchanzhe dique yongyou juedingxing yingxiang shi gongsi zhijian de jingzheng xingwei ， ta baohan le duiyu shichang yiji gongsi zhijian de hudong 。changjian de duiyu shichang jiegou de fenxi chule wanquan jingzheng yiwai ， haiyou longduanxing jingzheng 、 yiji qita ru guazhan 、 shuangtou longduan deng qingxing 。\n \n guanli jingjixue shi yi geti jingjixue jiaodu yanjiu gongsi huo qita guanli danwei jinxing shangye juece de guocheng ， zhe men yanjiu xiangdang yilai shuju shang de tongji ， biru duiyu yunchouxue de yanjiu ， yiji qita tongji fangfa liru zai meiyou wanzheng zixun he queding xingxia de huigui fenxi 。qi yanjiu de tese shi duiyu shangye juece zui jiahua de zhuiqiu ， baokuo le ruhe jiangdi chengben 、 zuidahua liyi deng ， dangran ， zheshi jiashe zai qita qingkuang liru keji he shichang xuqiu bu bian de tiaojian xia 。\n \n buquedingxing zai jingjixue shang shi zhi duiyu weilai shouru huo sunshi wufa yuce de benzhi ， buguan zheshi bushi shuyu fengxian 。ruoshi meiyou le buquedingxing ， geti de jingji xingwei jiu hui wanquan tuoli gongzuo he shouru de buquedingxing ， jinrong he ziben shichang ye hui lunwei danchun de shichang jieduan meijie ， er tongxun chanye ze hui wanquan xiaoshi 。youyu buquedingxing de xingtai zhongduo ， zai jingjixue shang you xuduo butong fangshi yong lai daibiao buquedingxing yiji jingji juecezhe dui qi de yingdui 。\n \n saiju lilun shi yingyong shuxue de yi zhong ， ta yanjiu de shi butong juecezhe zhijian de zhanlve hudong ， zhe ye shi shuyu buquedingxing de yi zhong 。saiju lilun tigong le chanye zuzhi lilun de shuxue genji ， yongyi jiagou gongsi de gezhong xingwei ， juli laishuo ta keyi yonglai yanjiu guazhan （ hen shao maijia ） de chanye xingwei ， ye keyi taoyong zai gongzi tanpan 、 taojia 、 qiyue liding he qita gezhong juecezhe shuliang shao dao tamen hui dui bici chansheng kejian yingxiang de qingkuang shang 。saiju lilun shi yi zhong xingwei jingjixue feichang pinfan shiyong de fangfa ， ta jiashe le getimen zai zhishao you bufen liyi chongtu de tiaojian xia ， fenbie xuanze dui tamen zui youli de zhanlve 。touguo zhezhong fenxi ， ta keyi jiang geti xunqiu liyi zuidahua de judong yonglai yanjiu liru gongji yu xuqiu de moxing ， tongshi ye kaolv dao zixun de buquedingxing 。zhe men yanjiu zuizao zhuisu zhi 1944nian yuehan·feng·nuoyiman de lilun 。saiju lilun duiyu zhongduo lingyu dou chansheng yingxiang ， baokuo le hezi zhanlve 、 lunlixue 、 zhengzhixue 、 shenzhi shi yanhua shengwuxue 。\n \n fengxian yanwu ye hui zai yige fada de jingji li cushi zhuanmen guanli fengxian he tigong fengxian zixun de chanye ， liru baoxianye shichang 、 qihuo jiaoyi 、 jinrong shangpin 、 jinrong jingjixue 、 huo chuncui de jinrong shichang bian shi zhendui fengxian ersheng de chanye 。zhekuai lingyu tongshi ye yanjiu jinrong shichang he gongsi de ziben jiegou 、 jinrong shichang de xiaolv he jiankangxing 、 jinrong weiji 、 yiji zhengfu duici de guanzhi dengdeng 。\n \n you yixie shichang zuzhi ye hui yinwei buquedingxing er chansheng dixiaolv ， yiju qiaozhi·akeluofu de 「 ningmeng shichang 」 lilun ， zhezhong dixiaolv de dianxing lizi zhiyi shi ershouche shichang 。youyu xiaofeizhe bu queding yi taiche shifou shi you qianzai wenti ， tamen wangwang hui yadi le yi tai haode ershouche de jiage diyu qi shiji pinzhi 。zixun bu duichen shide maijia jishi you zhe fangmian de zixun ， ye meiyou dongji gaozhi maijia 。xiangtong de baoxianye zai zhe fangmian de wenti ze shi nixiang xuanze ， yejiushishuo naxie hen rongyi mao fengxian de ren （ ye yinci zui rongyi chushi ） ， wangwang shi naxie zui qingxiangyu toubao de ren ， ye yinci daozhi le daode fengxian ， shide baoxian fandao cushi geng maoxian de xingwei 。zhexie wenti dou keneng zaocheng baoxian chengben de shangsheng ， ye yinci quzhu le bufen yuanben keyi congci fuwu huoli de ren （ bu wanzheng shichang ） 。erqie ， ruoshi shitu jiejue danyi wenti ， liru qiangzhi suoyouren baoxian ， name rengran bu neng jiejue 、 faner hui chuangzao chu geng duo daode fengxian de wenti 。zixun jingjixue bian shi duiyu zhexie wenti de yanjiu ， zhe zai xuduo lingyu ru baoxian 、 qiyuefa 、 jizhi sheji 、 huobi jingjixue 、 yiji jianbao shang 。keyi yingyong de yanjiu chengguo baokuo le jiejue huo jianshao falv he shichang shang de fengxian de cuoshi ， birushuo chanpin baogu 、 zhengfu guiding de bufen baoxian 、 ziben chongzu huo pochanfa 、 yiji qita duiyu zixun toulu de guanli 。\n \n 「 shichang shiling 」 baokuo le xuduo butong de wenti ， xuduo zhexie wenti keneng yu jingjixue jiyou de jiashe huxiang chongtu 。jinguan jingjixuejia duiyu shichang shiling de dingyi yousuo chayi ， yixia de fenlei jingchang bei tichu ： \n\n zixun bu duichen he bu wanzheng shichang keneng hui daozhi jingji de dixiaolv ， dan zhe you keneng touguo shichang 、 falv 、 huo qita zhengce banfa jiayi xiuzheng 。\n \n ziran longduan huozhe chengwei 「 jishu shang longduan 」 shi yi zhong jingzheng shiling de jiduan lizi 。zhezhong wenti miaoshu le jiran shengchan yige chanpin shi shengchan yue duo danyi chengben yue di ， name yici tuiduan meige chanpin zuizhong yinggai zhiyou yige shengchanzhe cai shi zui you xiaolv de 。\n \n gonggong wupin yiju shichang shiling lilun shi yiban shichang shi suo quefa gongji de ， zhezhong shiling de zui zhuyao tese shi renmen keyi shiyong gonggong wupin er bubi zhijie fufei 。\n \n waibu xingzhi de ze shi shichang jiage suo meiyou fanying chulai de waibu shehui chengben huo liyi 。juli laishuo ， wuranhui zaocheng fumian de waibuxing ， er （ zhengfu fufei de ）jiaoyu ze hui chuangzao zhengmian waibuxing （ ru geng gao jishu laogong ） 。zhengfu jingchang xiang you zhizao fumian waibuxing keneng de jingji huodong keshui huo jinxing jinzhi ， bingqie xiang zhengmian waibuxing de shouyizhe keshui yi qitu jiaozheng shichang 。lingwai ， jiben de gongji yu xuqiu lilun jieshi le junheng de dacheng ， dan bingmeiyou jieshi dadao gongxu junheng suo xuyao huafei de shijian 。\n \n yixie ren ze zhuzhang zhanxing jiage zhengming shuliang er bushi jiage jueding le gongji yu xuqiu de duanqi gaibian ， zhe ye shi xuduo zongti jingjixue li duiyu jingqi xunhuan de biaozhun yanjiu 。yanjiuzhe tongchang jujiao yu taolun zhanxing jiage de chengyin yiji dadao changqi junheng de guocheng 。you yixie jingjixue lingyu zhuanzhuyu dui shichang shiling de yanjiu ， biru gonggong jingjixue bian shi yanjiu zhengfu yi tiaojie shichang shiling weiming dui shichang jinxing de ganyu 。jiejue shichang shiling de zhengce fangshi baokuo le genju chengben shouyi fenxi liding de zhengfu guanli ， huozhe tigong shichang youyin yi jinxing gaibian ， biru shouqu paifangshui 。\n \n jinguan ruci ， xuduo jingjixuejia de yanjiu ze tichu zhiyi shichang shiling de lilun 。liru gonggong xuanze xuepai bian tichu le yu shichang shiling xiangfan de lizi － zhengfu shiling ， renwei zhengzhi shang de jingji ganyu he teshu liyi cai shi daozhi shichang shiling de zhuyin 。er aodili jingji xuepai ze gengjinyibu ， zhuzhang di xiaolv de longduan zhiyou zai zhengfu zhudao zhixia cai hui xingcheng ， bingqie zhuzhang shichang de dixiaolv zhiyou touguo xunqiu lirun de qiyejia jingshen caineng xiaochu ， er zhengfu bing bu neng zuochu zhengmian yingxiang 。\n \n gonggong caizheng shi yanjiu zhengfu gongjia jiguan ruhe jinxing yusuan he shuishou de jingjixue lingyu ， yanjiu de baohan le shuizhi de zhiding （ naxie ren zai jiao naxie shui ） 、 zhengfu kaizhi huodong de chengben xiaoyi fenxi 、 jinrong zhengce 、 zhengfu duiyu jingji xiaolv he shouru fenpei de yingxiang 。gonggong xuanze lilun bian shi yi geti jingjixue jiaodu yanjiu gonggong chanye de xuepai ， fenxi gezi xunqiu liyi zuidahua de zhengzhi geti ， liru zhengke 、 xuanmin 、 guanliao 、 he liyi tuanti ， yiji tamen zai zhengzhi guocheng zhong de hudong 。\n \n dabufen de jingjixue dou shi shizheng weizhu de ， yi miaoshu he yuce jingji xianxiang wei zhongdian ， er guifan jingjixue ze yanjiu jingji 「 yinggai shi shenme 」 。fuli jingjixue bian shi guifan jingjixue de yi zhong ， yi geti jingjixue de jiaodu fenxi shouru fenpei de xiaolv ， bingqie yi shehui li geti de jingji xingwei lai hengliang shehui fuli 。\n \n zongti jingjixue jiang jingji kanzuo shi yige zhengti ， bingqie touguo yiban junheng lilun yong 「 cong shang er xia 」 de jiaodu jianshi jingji de zonghe yu hudong 。zhexie zonghe baokuo le duiyu yi guo jingjiti de zong touru yu shuchu 、 shiyelv 、 yiji tonghuopengzhang ， qita de xiao zonghe ze baokuo le xiaofei he touzi zonghe deng 。zongti jingjixue ye zhuanzhuyu yanjiu huobi zhengce he caizheng zhengce shang 。\n \n zicong 1960niandai yilai ， zongti jingjixue ye bei yinjin yixie geti jingjixue de huafen fangshi ， liru fenxi geti de lixing 、 xiaolv shichang jiashuo 、 yiji bu wanquan jingzheng deng ， zhexie fazhan jiejue le bufen duiyu zhexie lingyu de bu yizhixing zhiyi 。\n \n zongti jingjixue tongshi kaoliang yingxiang chengzhang he guojia shouru de yinsu ， zhexie yinsu baokuo le ziben leiji 、 keji jinbu 、 yiji laodongli de chengzhang deng 。\n \n 「 chengzhang jingjixue 」 yanjiu de shi zaojiu jingji chengzhang de yinsu ， yi ji yige guojia renjun shengchan shuchu zai changqi de tigao 。tongyang zhege yinsu ye bei yong lai jieshi geguo zhijian cunzai de renjun shengchan shuchu de chayi ， youqi weihe mouxie guojia chengzhang de bi qita guojia kuai 、 er weihe mouxie pinqiong guojia de chengzhanglv bi yi kaifa guojia gao 。\n \n xuduo bei guangfan yanjiu de yinsu baokuo le touzi de bili 、 renkou chengzhang 、 yiji keji biange 。zhexie yanjiu baokuo le lilun shang he guancha shang de xingshi （ rutong xin gudianzhuyi jingji zengzhang moxing ） yiji zengzhang hesuan 。\n \n duiyu jingji xiaotiao de yanjiu cushi le zongti jingjixue de dansheng 。zai 1930niandai de jingji da konghuang shi ， yuehan·meinade·kaiensi chuban le 《 jiuye 、 lixi he huobi tonglun 》 yi shu ， jiangou le kaiensizhuyi de zhuyao lilun 。kaiensi renwei zai jingji xiaotiao shi ， duiyu chanpin de zong xuqiu keneng you buzu de xianxiang ， daozhi gao shiyelv yiji keneng de channeng liushi 。ta yushi renwei yinggai zengjia zhengfu zai gonggong chanye de huodong ， baokuo le yi zhongyang yinhang shixing kuozhangxing de huobi zhengce he caizheng zhengce yi wending jingqi xunhuan 。ye yinci ， kaiensizhuyi de yida jielun wei ， zai mouxie qingkuang xia ， shichang benshen bingbu neng jiang chanchu he guyong tuidao chongfen jiuye de chengdu 。yuehan·xikesi de IS - LM moxing bian shi jieshi kaiensi lilun de jingdian lizi 。\n \n suizhu shijian fazhan ， duiyu jingqi xunhuan de renzhi ye zhujian zengjin bing kuozhang dao qita lingyu ， daduo shi zuowei dui kaiensi lilun de huiying 。xin gudian zonghe xuepai bian shi zonghe kaiensi jingjixue yu xin gudianzhuyi jingjixue ， renwei kaiensizhuyi suiran zai duanqi shang shi zhengque de ， dan xin gudianzhuyi ze zai zhongchangqi geng you jieshi shuofuli 。xinxing gudian jingji xuepai ze cong kaiensi jingqi xunhuan lilun zhong tuochu ， renwei shichang de xiaotiao shi yinwei bu wanquan zixun suo zaocheng de ， chi zhezhong lichang de baokuo le mierdun·fuliman duiyu xiaofei de hengchang suode jiashuo yiji xiao luobote·lukasi tichu de 「 lixing xuanze 」 lilun 。\n \n xiangjiaozhixia ， xinxing kaien sixuepai ze baoliu le dui lixing yuqi de jiashe ， dan jiang jingqi xunhuan guijiuyu shichang shiling shang 。xinxing kaien sixuepai renwei jiage he gongzi shi you 「 nianxing 」 de ， yi ji tamen bu hui suizhu jingji qingkuang de biandong er henkuai zuochu tiaozheng 。ye yinci ， xin gudianzhuyi xuepai renwei jiage he gongzi hui zidong tiaozheng yi dacheng chongfen jiuye ， er xinxing kaien sixuepai ze renwei chongfen jiuye zhiyou zai changqi shang cai hui zidong dacheng ， ye yinci duanqi nei bixu yao you zhengfu he zhongyang yinhang jieru 。\n \n lingyifangmian ， yu kaien sixuepai duili de aodili jingji xuepai ze renwei jingqi xunhuan shi youyu zhengfu touguo zhongyang yinhang shichu guo duo de jiedai zijin ， yiner daozhi ziben jiedai de guodu rongyi ， conger zhishi qiyejia de cuowu touzi he ziben de cuowu fenpei ， yiner xingcheng xinyong paomo 。tamen renwei jingqi xunhuan li de kuozhangqi shi duiyu ziben de lanyongqi ， er jinjieerlai de shuaituiqi cai shi jingji fusu de kaishi 。aodili xuepai de lilun bu bei kaien sixuepai huo xin gudianzhuyi xuepai suo zhongshi ， raner zai xuejie rengran you bufen zhichizhe 。\n \n yige jingji tili de shiye renshu keyi you shiyelv lai jisuan ， yi ji you duoshao laogong zai jiji de xunzhao gongzuo ， tuixiuzhe 、 zheng jieshou jiaoyuzhe 、 huo yinwei qita yinsu er fangqi xunzhao gongzuozhe bingbu baohan zai shiyezhe li 。shiye keyi yiju ji zhong xingtai lai fenlei ， gudianshi shiye zhi de shi dang gongzi tai gao yiner daozhi guzhu bu yuan guyong geng duo laogong shi ， gongzi tai gao de yuanyin keneng shi zuidi gongzi fagui 、 huoshi gonghui de huodong daozhi 。yiju gudianshi shiye shuofa ， mocaxing shiye ze shi dang shichang you yingdui de gongzuo cunzai ， dan zai peidui gongzuo de guocheng zhong laogong suo xuyao xunzhao he dengdai de shijian 。jiegouxing shiye ze baohan yixilie daozhi shiye de yuanyin ， biru laogong youde jineng yu shichang xuyao de jineng bu tongshi 。dang yige jingjiti de chanye zheng jinxing daguimo de zhuanbian shi ， yinwei xuduo laogong jiyou de jineng yu xinxing chanye butong ， xuduo jiegouxing shiye bian you keneng fasheng 。wulun jingjiti suo chu de qingkuang ， mouxie chengdu de shiye dou you keneng chixu cunzai ， buguo kaien sixuepai zhuzhang dang jingji tingzhi chengzhang shi ， yinwei zong xuqiu buzu suo chansheng de zhouqixing shiye jiu you keneng fasheng ， aokenfa ze bian shi duiyu shiyelv yu jingji chengzhang de guancha 。yuanshi de aokenfa ze zhichu 3% de jingji chanchu chengzhang bian hui jiangdi 1% de shiyelv 。\n \n zai daduoshu shichang jingji xia ， huobi shi yi zhong yongyi zuowei jiaoyi meijie de gongju 。jiashe zai meiyou tonghuopengzhang de qingkuang xia ， huobi biqi qita xingshi de jiaoyi meijie （ liru beike 、 yintiao 、 huangjin ） yao geng lai de you jiazhi wendingxing 、 keqie fenxing 、 jianbianxing 、 yiji geng liudong de gongji 。huobi baohan le dazhong chiyou de zhichao he jixu 、 yiji yinhang he zhengfu juyou de beiyong zijin 。huobi jiu haobi shi xiang yuyan yiban de shehui meijie ， qi jiazhi cunzaiyu yu taren hudong de gongneng shang ， ruoshi meiyou qita jiaoyi de duixiang ， name zai duo de qian ye dengtong feizhi 。\n \n zuowei yi zhong jiaoyi meijie ， huobi rang jiaoyi biande gengwei rongyi ， ta shi renmen keyi geng jiandan de gujia chanpin he fuwu ， tongshi ye cushi chuxu de chansheng 。yu huobi duibi de shi yi wuyiwu de jiaoyi fangshi ， meiyou le huobi ， bian yao yi geng kunnan de wuzhi peidui jiaoyi shuangfang de xuqiu （ biru pingguo jiaohuan shuben ） 。youyu huobi de tongyongxing ， ta shide jiaoyi de jiaoyi chengben deyi jiangdi ， ruciyilai shengchanzhe bian keyi qingyi jiang chanchu huanwei shichang tongyong de jiazhi ， er bu xu zhuanhuan bixu jinxing er ci jiaoyi de wupin 。\n \n dui yige jingjiti eryan ， huobi gongji yu zong shengchan de mianzhi he wujia shuizhun you miqie guanxi ， ye yinci ， guanli huobi gongji shi huobi zhengce de zhongyao keti 。\n \n kaien sixuepai renwei zhengfu yinggai touguo duiyu caizheng zhengce de caonong lai tiaozheng zong xuqiu ， tamen zhuzhang dangzong xuqiu diyu jingjiti cunzai de shengchan qianneng shi ， zhezhong meiyou shiyong dao de shengchan nengli bian xingcheng le chanchu langfei 。yiju zhezhong shuofa ， zhengfu touguo zengjia caizheng zhichu de fangshi （ touguo chizi zhichu 、 keshui 、 huoshi tonghuopengzhang ） lai guli zong xuqiu chengzhang ， ruciyilai bian yunyong dao meiyou bei shiyong de shengchan qianneng 。juli laishuo ， jishi zai meiyou shiji xuyao de qingkuang xia ， zhengfu ye keyi guyong shiye laogong lai xingjian gaosu gonglu ， ruciyilai bian hui fahui tamen de 「 shengchan qianneng 」 。er zhezhong zhichu ye you chengshu xiaoying ， yi ji wei yingfu kuozhangxing caizheng zhengce er chansheng de shangji goucheng le duochu de jingji huodong 。\n \n dangran ， zhezhong lilun shi genji zai meiyou kaolv dao jichu xiaoying de jiashe shang 。ruguo chanchu langfei bing bu cunzai ， na jingji tibian shi yi wanquan de channeng zai yunzuo ， zheshi ruguo zhengfu jieru zengjia caizheng zhichu ， bian hui jiya dao minjian chanye de jingji huodong ， ye yinci bu hui chansheng jingji zengzhang 。zhichi kuozhangxing caizhengzhe renwei jichu xiaoying zhiyou zai meiyou chanchu langfei shi cai hui chuxian ， er fandui de jingjixuejia renwei zhezhong xiaoying shi yongyuan cunzai de ， bingqie zhichu lijiatu dengjia lilun ， tamen zhuzhang zhengfu jiedai biran xuyao yi weilai de keshui zengjia lai changhuan ， er renhe yinwei zhengfu caizheng zhengce suo yinqi de xuqiu zengzhang ， duhui yinwei minjian wei yingfu weilai gaoshuilv de chuxu er bei xiaochu 。\n \n guoji jingjixue yanjiuguo yu guo zhijian de maoyi wanglai ， bingqie yanjiu guoji maoyi keyi dailai de maoyi lide ， zhongyao de zhengce yanjiu baokuo le guanshui yiji maoyi bilei duiyu jinchukou he jingji chengzhang de yingxiang 。guoji jinrongxue ze shi zhengti jingjixue li yi men zhuanmen yanjiu ziben ruhe zai geguo zhijian liudong de lingyu ， bingqie yanjiu huilv 。guoji maoyi de zengzhang 、 geguo fengong de zengqiang he mijihua shi quanqiuhua zhongyao de laiyuan 。\n \n fazhan jingjixue ze shi yanjiu zai fazhan chengdu xiangdui luohou de kaifa zhong guojia ， bingqie yanjiu chanye gaibian 、 pinqiong 、 he jingji chengzhang 。yu qita jingjixue lingyu butong de shi ， fazhan jingjixue jingchang jiehe shehui yu zhengzhi de yiti zuowei kaoliang 。\n \n jingji tixi shi jingjixue li yanjiu geguo jingji tixi chayi de lingyu ， yanjiu de zhongdian baokuo le geguo zai jingji luxian 、 fazhan celve 、 chanquan baohu 、 yiji jingji ziyuan fenpei deng zhibiao shang de chayi 。zhe men lingyu de yanjiu shi yi yige 「 jingji tixi 」 zuowei zui jiben de yanjiu danwei 。\n \n zai dangdai jingji tixi li ， jingji zuzhi de liang da butong luxian wei shehuizhuyi tizhi he zibenzhuyi tizhi ， yizhe shi yi guojia tongyu jingji 、 ling yi zhe ze shi yi ziyou shichang lai jinxing ， er zhe liangzhe zhijian de zhongjian luxian wei hunhe jingji 。yanjiu jingji tixi yu zhengzhi tizhi zhijian de hudong ， ye bei chengwei zhengzhi jingjixue ， 「 jingji tixi bijiao 」 zhi de ze shi hengliang butong jingji tixi zhijian de jingji xingwei he chengzhang chayi 。\n \n dangdai de jingjixue jingchang shiyong shuxue zuowei yanjiu shouduan zhiyi ， jingjixuejia shiyong de yanjiu gongju baokuo le weijifen 、 xianxing daishu 、 tongjixue 、 saiju lilun 、 yiji diannao kexue 。xueshujie de jingjixuejia yiban dou you shiyong zhexie gongju de jiben nengli ， shaoshu jingjixuejia ze zhuanzhu zai shuli jingjixue he qita shuxue de fangshi 。\n \n zhuliu jingjixue lilun yikao de shi xianyan de jingji moxing ， bing cong zhongyansheng zhongduo gainian 。zhexie jingji lunshu tongchang jiashe zai 「 qita qingkuang baochi bu bian 」 zhixia ， yanjiu jujiao de bianshu shi ruhe yinying gezhong tiaojian jinxing gaibian 。dang jinxing jingjixue lunshu shi ， jingjixuejia zhongshi de shi xunzhao keyi yi zuishao guancha zixun lai shizheng 、 zuiwei mingque biaoda 、 tongshi keyi yansheng chu qita yanjiu de lilun 。\n \n zai geti jingjixue xia ， zhuyao de yanjiu gainian wei gongji yu xuqiu 、 bianjizhuyi 、 lixing xuanze lilun 、 jihui chengben 、 yusuanxian 、 xiaoyong 、 yiji gongsi yanjiu 。er zongti jingjixue zaoqi ze jujiaoyu duiyu zongti bianyin de moxing jiangou ， raner suizhu shijian fazhan ， zhezhong luxian zhujian bei taotai ， querdaizhi de yanjiu ze geng zhuzhong yu yi geti jichu chufa de zongti yanjiu 。\n \n geti jingjixue de xuduo gainian dui zongti jingjixue de lingyu dou qi le zhongda yingxiang ， liru huobi zhengce shang ， huobizhuyi zhuzhang de huobi shuliang lun zhichu dui huobi de gongji kuozhang hui yinwei shichang de lixing yuqi er zaocheng tonghuopengzhang 。zai fazhan jingjixue zhong ， yi kaifa guojia yiban bei yuce hui you bijiao xiao fudu de jingji chengzhang ， yinwei ziben touzi de bianji huishou hui suizhu fazhan chengdu er kaishi xiajiang ， zhezhong qushi jiu zai yazhou si xiao long de fazhan shang bei guancha dao 。youshihou zhexie jingji jiashuo suo zhuzhang de zhishi yi zhong 「 dingxiang 」 huo 「 qushi 」 ， er fei juedui de shuju gaibian 。\n \n zai jin jishi nian ， saiju lilun yu shehui kexue lingyu de jisu kuozhang ye dui jingjixue chansheng juda yingxiang ， touguo liru nashenjun hengdian zuowei yanjiu jingji geti juece de jizhun ， jingjixuejia keyi zai bu yikao shiji shijie ziliao de qingkuang xia dui xuduo lingyu zuochu fenxi he yuce 。biaozhun de saiju lilun jingjixue lunshu tongchang xian sheji yige yu xianyou jingji wenti leisi de 「 saiju 」 ， jingjixuejia bing yi saiju li de danfang xingwei he duofang hudong lai yanjiu tamen ruhe zai butong guize xia jinxing liyi zuidahua 。\n \n jingji lilun jingchang bei yong guancha shang de fangfa jiayi yanzheng ， tongchang shi touguo jiliang jingjixue lai jianshi jingji shuju 。yiban shiti kexue changjian de fengbi shiyan zai jingjixue shang shi hen nan dacheng erqie hen shaojian de ， ye yinci ， jingjixuejia tongchang yilai guancha jiyou ziliao de fangshi lai ceshi tamen de lilun ， suiran zheyang guancha shiyan de jieguo meiyou fengbi shiyan lai de zhunque 、 ye bi yao rongyi bei zhiyi 。jinguan ruci ， shiyan jingjixue shi yi men zhujian zai chengzhang de lingyu ， erqie dui jiyou moxing de guancha ye zai zengjia 。\n \n tongjixue de yanjiu fangfa liru huigui fenxi ye hen changjian ， shiyongzhe yong ci fangfa lai guji guimo 、 jingji zhongyaoxing 、 yiji tongji xianzhuxing ， jie ci lai tichu jiashuo 、 bingqie kongzhi bianyin de yingxiang 。touguo zhezhong zuofa ， yige jiashuo you keneng yinci huode zhichi ， jinguan qi zhunquexing rengran zhishi jilv shang de 、 er bushi juedui de ， panduan yanjiu de biaozhun ze shi yikao qi kefou zhengxing yiji zhengwei jieguo 。youyu shiyan jieguo de buquedingxing ， zhexie guancha yanjiu bingbu yiding yao dui qi yanjiu wenti tichu juedingxing de jielun ， shenzhi ye bu yiding yao tichu zhuyao de faxian 。zai shiyong jingjixue lingyu shang ， yi xianxing guihua lai jinxing touru - chanchu moxing de yanjiu xiangdang changjian ， weile yanjiu mouzhong zhengce dui ge fangmian de yingxiang ， jingjixuejia chang jiang daliang ziliao jiaoyou diannao tongji fenxi 。\n \n zhuanye de tonghang pingshen he duiyu jieguo de chongxin shengcheng ye neng jinyibu quebao guancha shiyan bu hui chansheng you pianjian de 、 cuowu de 、 huo qingshuai gaihua de jieguo ， jinguan jingjixue xuduo yanjiu lingyu dou chang bei piping shi wufa chongsheng yanjiu jieguo de 。rutong chuncui de lilun ， duiyu tongji shiyan de shiyong ye hui shoudao pipan fenxi ， jinguan ruci ， zai guoqu 40nian jian ， danchun wei piping qita yanjiu jieguo de wenzhang zai ru meiguo jingji pinglun de qikan shang yizhi jianshao ， zhe bei renwei shi qikan shitu zengjia qi yinyong shuliang de yi zhong jieguo 。\n \n shiyan jingjixue ye zaojiu le xuduo yi fengbishi duizhao shiyan wei fangfa de yanjiu ， zhijie ceshi yiban bei shiwei zhenli de yixie jingjixue lilun ， zhe jiang chuantong shang jingjixue yu ziran kexue de qufen gei suoxiao le ， liru zuihou tongdie saiju de shiyan jieguo bian zhengshi le renmen hui jujue jieshou bu pingdeng de fenpei fangshi 。\n \n zai xingwei jingjixue shang ， xinlixuejia dannier·kaneiman yu amosi·tewosiji yiqi yinwei tamen duiyu zhanwang lilun he renzhi piancha de faxian er huode 2002nian de nuobeier jingjixue jiang ， zai shenjing jingjixue shang de guancha shiyan ye zhengshi le leisi jieguo 。lingwai yige lizi ze shi duizhao chuantong de sili pianhao jiashe yu yige keyi ceshi zisi 、 lita 、 yu hezuo qingxiang de moxing 。zhexie yanjiu de jinzhan shide yixie ren zhuzhang jingjixue ye shi 「 zhenzheng de kexue 」 de yibufen \n \n jingjixue zhe yi lingyu de zhuanyehua ， fanying zai zhege lingyu de yanjiusuo kecheng de chengzhang shang ， bingqie bei chengwei shi 「 jingjixue zi 1900 nian lai de zhongda gaibian 」 。daduoshu zhuyao de daxue he yuanxiao dou you yige zhuanjing de jingjiyuan suo bing banfa jingjixue de xuewei ， bulunshi zai tongshi jiaoyu 、 shangye huo qita zhuanye lingyu shang ， jingjixue kecheng wangwang shi bixiu de kecheng 。\n \n nuobeier jingjixue jiang zai meinian hui yiju qi zhuanjia pingshen banfa gei dui zhege lingyu you zhongda gongxian de jingjixuejia 。zai siren qiye ， jingjixuejia tongchang danren guwen de juese ， youqishi zai yinhangye he jinrongye 。jingjixuejia ye ti zhongduo zhengfu bumen fuwu ， liru guoku 、 zhongyang yinhang 、 he tongji zuzhi 。\n \n jingjixue shi shehui kexue de yi men ， tongshi ye yingxiang le zhongduo qita lingyu de xueshu fazhan ， liru jingji dilixue 、 jingjishi 、 gonggong xuanze lilun 、 jiating jingjixue 、 yiji zhidu jingjixue 。\n \n falv jingjixue shi yi zhong yi jingji lilun jiaodu qieru yanjiu faxue de fangshi ， baohan le yi jingjixue jieshi falv chansheng de jingji yingxiang 、 yanjiu falv shifou youzhu huo youhaiyu jingji xiaoyi 、 yiji yuce weilai jingjifa zouxiang 。luonade·kesi zai 1961nian de wenzhang li jiu ceng zhuzhang ， duiyu chanquan de lianghao baohu keyi kefu shichang de waibuxing 。\n \n zhengzhi jingjixue shi yi men jiehe jingjixue 、 faxue 、 yiji zhengzhixue de yanjiu ， zhendui zai tantao zhengzhi zhidu 、 zhengzhi huanjing 、 yiji jingji tizhi （ ru zibenzhuyi huo shehuizhuyi ） zhijian de hudong 。zhengzhi jingjixue yanjiu de baohan le ru longduan he xunzu xingwei yiji waibuxing yu zhengfu zhengce de guanxi 。lishixuejia youshi hui shiyong zhengzhi jingjixue yi ci lai miaoshu yanjiu zai lishi shang you teding liyi de geren huo tuanti shi ruhe liyong zhengzhi shouduan lai qude liyi 。\n \n jingjixue de shehui xuefen zhi ye touguo jingji shehuixue fazhan chulai ， zhuyao shi genji zai aimier·tuergan 、 makesi·weibo 、 geaoerge·qimeier deng ren de zuopin shang ， yongyi fenxi jingji fazhan he jingji xianxiang duiyu shehui chuantong de yingxiang 。zhongyao de zuopin baokuo le makesi·weibo de 《 xinjiao lunli yu zibenzhuyi jingshen 》 geaoerge·qimeier de 《 huobi zhexue 》 deng shu 。\n \n dui jingjixue de yanjiu zuizao keyi zhuisu zhi meisuo bu da miya 、 guxila 、 guluoma 、 zhongguo 、 bosi 、 yiji alabo wenming 。14 shiji zhiqian zhiming de xuezhe baokuo le yalisiduode 、 kaodi liye 、 tangmasi·akuina 、 yiben·heleidun deng ren 。shoudao yalisiduode xiezuo de qifa ， akui na dui qi houdai 14 zhi 17shiji de jingyuan zhexue you xuduo gongxian ， you jingyuan zhexue suo yansheng de salaman kaxuepai ye chengwei zhongshiji mo diyi ge you xitongxing di yi ziranfa yanjiu huobi 、 lixi 、 yiji jiazhi lilun deng jingji faze de jingjixuepai 。\n \n zai wenyi fuxing zhihou ， jingjixue de fazhan kaishi you zhongshangzhuyi he zhongnongzhuyi liang pai suo zhipei ， zhe liang ge xuepai dou dui ouzhou jingji minzuzhuyi he xiandai zibenzhuyi de fazhan you xiangdang yingxiang 。zhongshangzhuyi zai 16 zhi 18 shiji shengxing yu yixie shangren he zhengke zhijian ， zhuzhang yi guo zhi caifu shi kao zhulei jijin yin er lai de ， er meiyou tianranjin kuang yinkuang de guojia ze zhineng kaozhu chukou chanpin bingqie xianzhi jinkou jinyin yiwai huowu lai leiji caifu 。zhongshangzhuyi zhuzhang jinkou pianyi de yuanshi ziyuan yi yonglai shengchan chukou de huowu ， bingqie yi guanshui fangzhi laizi guowai chanpin de jingzheng 。\n \n zhongnongzhuyi ze shi yi qun 18shiji de faguo sixiangjia zucheng ， bing renwei jingjiti shi yige shouru he chanchu buduan xunhuan de quanquan ， tamen zhuzhang zhiyou nongye shengchan cai nenggou chanchu chaoguo chengben de jiazhi ， ye yinci nongye shi suoyou chanye de genji 。tamen fandui zhongshangzhuyi dui zhizaoye he chukou de zhongshi er hulve le nongye 。zhongnongzhuyizhe bingqie zhuzhang taotai haofei daliang chengben de shuijin shouqu zhidu ， gaiyi dizhu de suodeshui tidai zhi 。biqi zhongshangzhuyi ， zhongnongzhuyizhe geng zhichi ziyou fangren de zhengce ， renwei zhengfu bu gai ganyu jingji 。\n \nyadang·simi （ 1723 - 1790 ） bei renwei shi xiandai jingjixue de kaiduan ， ta duiyu dangshi de zhongshangzhuyi tichu zhongduo piping ， bing renwei zhongnongzhuyi jinguan 「 bing bu wanmei 」 dan rengran shi gengwei jiejin jingjixue zhenxiang de kuangjia 。\n \nyadang·simi zai 1776nian chuban de 《 guofulun 》 yi shu bei renwei shi 「 zaojiu le jingjixue dansheng de qishidian 」 ， zhe benshu jiang tudi 、 laodong 、 yiji ziben shiwei shi shengchan de sanda yaosu yiji shengchan yi guo caifu de laiyuan ， er paoqi le zhongnongzhuyi renwei zhiyou nongye huodong cai you shengchanxing de lilun 。\n \n simi taolun le fengong keyi dailai de jingji haochu ， baokuo le laodong channeng de shangsheng yiji maoyi lide ， wulunshi xiangcun huoshi dushi 、 huoshi butong guojia zhijian dou keyi jie ci huoli 。ta de lilun renwei fengong de chengdu shi you shichang de xuqiu suo jueding ， zhe ye chengwei le houdai jingjixuejia duiyu gongsi he chanye zuzhi de zhuyao lilun laiyuan 。yadang·simi tichu le bei guangfan renwei shi jingjixue li zui zhongyao de mingti ： yi ji zai jingzheng zhixia ， ziyuan de chiyouren （ wulunshi laodongli 、 tudi 、 haishi ziben ） hui xunqiu liyi zuidahua de tujing ， yushi zai junheng zhixia suoyou tongyi ziyuan de chiyouren duhui huode xiangtong de baochou （ paichu shiye deng yinsu wai ） 。\n \n simi renwei suoyou ge tihui liyong tamen chiyou de renhe ziben lai zengjin qi zishen de lirun he fuli er fei 「 shehui 」 de liyi ， zhe zai houlai bei chengwei shi 「 jingjixue shang zui zhongyao de yi duan hua 」 。simi bingqie zhuzhang geti xunqiu lirun de dongji shi shengchan guocheng zhong suo bukehuoque de ， tamen huode de lirun jiu daibiao le tamen suo shengchan chu de jiazhi 。ta zheyang shuodao ： \n\nyinci ， youyu meige geren duhui jinli ba ta de ziben yongyi zhichi bing guanli guonei de chanye ， zhexie chanye de shengchan yushi bian neng dadao zui da de jiazhi ； meige geren ye biran jieli de shi shehui de nianshouru jinliang kuoda 。queshi ， ta tongchang bingmeiyou dasuan yao cujin gonggong de liyi ， ye bu zhidao ta ziji cujin le zhezhong liyi zhihe zhong chengdu 。youyu ningyuan zhichi guonei de chanye er feiguowai de chanye ， ta zhishi pansuan zhu ta ziji de anquan ； ta guanli chanye de fangshi zaiyu shi qi shengchan de jiazhi nenggou zuidahua ， ta suo pansuan de ye zhishi ta ziji de liyi 。zai zhexie changjian de qingkuang xia ， jingguo yi shuang kan bujian de shou de yindao ， ta ye tongshi cujin le ta yuanxian wuyi dacheng de mubiao 。bingfei chuzi benyi bingbu daibiao jiu dui shehui youhai 。jieyou zhuiqiu ta geren de liyi ， wangwang ye shi ta gengwei youxiao di cujin le zhege shehui de liyi ， er chaochu ta yuanxian de yiliao zhiwai 。wo conglai meiyou tingshuo guo you duoshao haoshi shi you naxie yangzhuang zengjin gonggong liyi er ganyu maoyi de ren suo dacheng de 。\n \nyadang·simi tichu de kan bujian de shou de gainian yu ta duiyu jingji fazhan he jingji chengzhang de zhongshi you miqie guanxi ， ta renwei jingji shang de zengzhang shide shehui dazhong keyi jinxing geng duo geng you jiazhi de xiaofei ， zhe zai ta xinmu zhong cai shi 「 suoyou shengchan de weiyi mudi 」 。simi bingqie yi kan bujian de shoulai pinglun zhongduo de jingjixue lingyu ， baokuo le zhengfu duiyu jingzheng 、 maoyi de xianzhi ， yiji yinhang he lixi ， bing tichu ta renwei shi 「 ziyou de jiding tizhi 」 baokuo le guofang 、 gongping de sifa zhidu 、 yixie keyi zaofu quan shehui de gonggong gongcheng yiji tigong jiaoyu 、 daolu 、 shuiba dengdeng 。xiandai de jingjixue jiaokeshu chang ba yadang·simi de kan bujian de shou zuowei jieshi jingjixue de zui jiben gainian 。\n \n tongshi qi de tuomasi·maersasi ze liyong baochou dijian lai jieshi shenghuo shuiping ， ta yuyan renlei renkou hui yi jihe fangshi beizeng 、 dan liangshi shengchan que zhi hui jianjin de zengjia ， ruciyilai youxian de tudi bian hui daozhi baozeng de renkou laodongli channeng baochou dijian ， yushi bian hui daozhi shenghuo shuiping dafu tuibu de renkou guosheng chuxian 。maersasi bingqie zhiyi shichang jingji de tiaojie xingneng ， piping shichang benshen wufa dacheng wanquan jiuye ， bingqie cheng jingjiti qingxiangyu guodu cunkuan er daozhi xiaofei buzu ， zhe yi lilun houlai ye bei kaiensi jiayi liyong 。\n \nyadang·simi zhuzhong zai caifu de shengchan shang ， er dawei·lijiatu ze zhuzhong zai shouru de fenpei 。lijiatu renwei dizhu yu ziben he laogong zhijian biran hui you chongtu cunzai ， ta zhuzhang suizhu renkou de chengzhang he shengchan zengjia ， youxian de tudi biran hui shide zujin zhujian shangzhang ， yushi jiandi ziben huode de lirun 、 yiji laogong de gongzi 。lijiatu shi diyi ge tichu le bijiao youshi de jingjixuejia ， yiju ci lilun ， wulun yi guo shifou zai shengchan shang meige cengmian dou bi taguo youyue huo luohou ， bianji de shengchan chengben chayi shide tamen dou keyi cong guoji maoyi guocheng zhong huoli 。bijiao liyi dao jintian yizhi bei jingjixuejia renwei shi jieshi maoyi lide de zui jiben kuangjia 。\n \n dao le gudian jingjixue de moqi ， yixie ren kaishi dui qi jiashe tichu zhiyi ， biru yuehan·situerte·mierbian tichu shichang fenpei shouru de wenti ， ta renwei shichang banyan le liang ge zhuyao de juese ： ziyuan de fenpei yiji shouru de fenpei 。ta renwei shichang zai fenpei ziyuan shang keneng shi zui youxiao de ， dan bu yiding keyi zuihao de fenpei shouru ， yushi chansheng shehui jieru de xuyao 。\n \n jiazhi lilun shi gudian jingjixue zhongyao de yibufen ， yadang·simichang bei renwei shi tichu yige chanpin de jiaohuan jiazhi shi you qi laodongsuo jueding de ren ， buguo ， simi qishi zai zhe fangmian yousuo baoliu ， biru ta shuo ： 「 suoyou dongxi de zhenzheng jiazhi ， qujueyu qude zheyang dongxi de nandu 。 」simi renwei chule gongzi yiwai de yinsu ye yingxiang le chanpin de jiage 。jinguan ruci ， xuduo gudian jingjixuejia kaishi yi simi wei jichu tichu le laodong jiazhi lilun ， zhuzhang laodong shi jiazhi de zhuyao huo weiyi laiyuan 。\n \n makesizhuyi jingjixue shi cong gudian jingjixue li yanshengerchu de ， kaer·makesi tichu le qi lilun de jiben moxing 。makesi zai 1867nian chuban le 《 zibenlun 》 yi shu ， yi laodong jiazhi lilun wei jichu ， zhuzhang zibenzhuyi de shengchan moshi biran hui chansheng shengyu jiazhi ， ye jiushi ziben duiyu laogong de boxue 。yiju laodong jiazhi lilun ， yige chanpin de jiazhi shi you shengchan guocheng zhong suo bixu de shehui laodongsuo jueding de ， er shengyu jiazhi lilun ze zhuzhang laogong de gongzi zhi goucheng le chanpin jiage li de laodongli jiage ， ji rang laodongli zaishengchan de bufen ， congci renwei you boxue cunzai 。\n \n cong 1870nian zhi 1910nian zhijian ， yixilie jingjixuejia kaishi dui gudian jingjixue de jiashe tichu tiaozhan ， zhe yi xilie de biange houlai bei chengwei shi 「 bianji geming 」 。you yinggelan de weilianmu·sitanli·jiewensi 、 aodili de kaer·mengeer he ruishi de liang·waerlasi suo gezi tichu ， bianjizhuyi fouding le gudian jingjixue de laodong jiazhi lilun ， renwei jiazhi shi you bianji xiaoyong er fei laodongsuo jueding de 。bianjizhuyi budan jiejue le gudian jingjixue suo wufa jieshi de zuanshi yu shuibeilun ， tongshi ye cusheng le chengwei xiandai xin gudian jingjixue gujia de zhuguan jiazhi lilun 。\n \n 19shijimo de bianji geming shi jingjixue de yida fenshuiling 。gudian jingjixue zhongshi de shi shehui huodong jian de yinguo guanxi ， liru caifu de shengchan he fenpei ， yiji touguo zhengzhi jingjixue fenxi butong zhengti xia caifu fenpei jiegou 。suizhu bianji xiaoyong gainian de tichu ， duiyu shengchan he jiaoyi de yanjiu deyi cong shehui lilun （ ru makesizhuyi ） zhong fenli chulai ， er maixiang kexuexing de fenxi 。zhezhonggaibian shide jingjixue deyi tuoli shoudao jiazhi panduan yingxiang de guifan jingjixue ， bu zai jujiao yu shehui he shengchan 「 yinggai zenmeyang 」 de wenti ， ershi yanjiu xianshi shijie 「 shi shenme 」 ， jiner chengwei keguan er juyou kexuexing de xuewen 。\n \n kaiensizhuyi jingjixue fazhan ziyuehan·meinade·kaiyinsi 1936nian chuban de 《 jiuye 、 lixi yu huobi de yiban lilun 》 yi shu ， cishu queli le zongti jingjixue yi lingyu de duli 。kaiensi zai cishu zhong yanjiu xuduo zai duanqi （ yi ji ， changqi de jingji junheng dadao zhiqian ） yingxiang zongshouru he shengchan de yinsu ， ta renwei gaodu de shiye keneng hui yinwei shichang quefa youxiao xuqiu er wufa zixing tiaozheng ， bingqie zhuzhang weile zengjia zong xuqiu ， zhengfu yinggai touguo kuozhangxing de caizheng zhengce lai kefu zhezhong qingkuang 。zai dangshi jingji da konghuang de huanjing xia ， kaiensi de ci yi lilun dui jingjixuejie chansheng zhongda yingxiang 。\n \n suizhu shijian fazhan ， kaien sixuepai chuxian liang ge fenzhi 。hou kaien sixuepai zhuzhongyu yanjiu zongti jingjixue de tanxing quefa yiji tiaozheng guocheng ， lingwai tamen zai geti jingjixue shang ze yi shiji shijie de guancha lizi lai zuowei yanjiu jichu ， er fei touguo liyi zuidahua de moxing ， gai xuepai de zhuyao renwu you qiong·luobinxun deng ren 。\n \n xinxing kaien sixuepai tongyang ye shi yanshengzi yuanshi de kaiensizhuyi ， ci liupai tongyi qita jingjixuejia liyong liyi zui da hualai jieshi geti jingjixue de moxing ， dan tichu le jiage he gongzi nianxing de lilun ， yongyi gengxin yuanshi de kaiensizhuyi ， jinguan tamen dui yuanshi kuangjia de zhichi yijing zhuanbian wei qiangdiao qi chixu chuxian tezheng ， er bushi jianchi qi cunzai de benzhi 。\n \n bianji geming cusheng le zhudao dangdai zhuliu jingjixue de xin gudianzhuyi jingjixue ， aerfuleide·maxieer tichu le 「 jingjixue 」 yi ci lai xingrong duiyu 「 jingji kexue 」 de yanjiu ， yongyi duizhao zhiqian de zhengzhi jingjixue 。zhezhong zhuanbian jiu youru zai dangshi shuxue moxing duiyu ziran kexue de yingxiang 。xin gudianzhuyi jingjixue jiang gongji yu xuqiu zuowei fenxi shichang junheng xia jiage he gongji shuliang de moxing ， yici jieshi chanchu yiji shouru de fenpei 。biqi gudian jingjixue ， xin gudianzhuyi zhongshi de shi shichang de bianji xuqiu 。dao le 20shiji ， xin gudianzhuyi jingjixue yuanli le gudian jingjixue yi jishu zuowei fenxi geti zhijian shengchan guanxi he shehui zonghe liyi de fangshi 。\n \n zai geti jingjixue fangmian ， xin gudianzhuyi renwei dongji he jihui chengben goucheng le juece de zui zhongyao jizhun ， lizi zhiyi shi xiaofeizhe lilun fenxi jiage （ ye jiushi chengben ） yiji shouru shi ruhe yingxiang xuqiu de shuliang 。er zai zongti jingjixue shang ， yu kaiensizhuyi zonghe de xin gudian zonghe xuepai chengwei dangjin zongti jingjixue de zhuliu 。\n \n xin gudianzhuyi jingjixue jingchang bei chengwei shi 「 zhengtong jingjixue 」 ， xiandai de zhuliu jingjixue jiaokeshu daduo shi yi xin gudianzhuyi wei jichu ， suiran zai xuduo fangmian ye you gaidong huoshi zhongshi butong de lingyu ， liru jiliang jingjixue 、 saiju lilun 、 duiyu shichang shiling he bu wanquan jingzheng de fenxi deng 。\n \n 1970niandai chuxian de tingzhixing tonghuopengzhang zhijie tiaozhan le kaiensizhuyi de jiben jiashe 。yiju feilipusi quxian ， kaiensizhuyi renwei tonghuopengzhang hui shide wujia tigao ， youci daidong chanye guyong geng duo laogong yi zengda channeng ， er geng gao de guyongdu ze hui daidong xuqiumian 。raner ， zai 1970 zhi 1980niandai tongshi chuxian le tonghuopengzhang he gao shiyelv ， zhe shide yuanxian zhipei zongti jingjixue de kaiensizhuyi kaishi beishou zhiyi 。\n \n zai zhezhong beijing xia ， zhijiage jingji xuepai he qi yansheng de huobizhuyi kaishi tiaozhan kaiensizhuyi 。yiju gai xuepai de mierdun·fuliman deng ren de shuofa ， shichang jingji zai huobi gongji chiping （ yi ji ， meiyou guo duo de pengzhang huo jinsuo ） de tiaojian xia ， keyi zixing tiaozheng gongxu 。yiju zhezhong lilun ， zhengfu de juese shi touguo zhongyang yinhang ， tiaokong zai jingjiti zhong liutong de huobi shuliang ， chucizhiwai ， bu xuyao ganyu ziyou shichang de huodong 。zhijiage xuepai yiji houlai xiao luobote·lukasi tichu de lixing yuqi lilun ， dafudu qudai le kaiensizhuyi zai zongti jingjixue de zhipei diwei 。qian meiguo lianbang zhunbei lishihui zhuxi ben·bonanke bian shi zhichi fuliman jieshi jingqi xunhuan shuofa de jingjixuejia zhiyi 。dangdai de zhuliu jingjixue jingchang bei erfen wei meiguo donghaian yu xihaian daxue daibiao de xianshui xuepai yu zhijiage deng neidi daxue daibiao de danshui xuepai 。\n \nmierdun·fuliman jibenshang caina le xuduo yadang·simi he qita gudian jingjixuejia tichu de geti jingjixue gainian bingqie jiang zhi xiandaihua ， biru ta zai 1970nian ceng zhuzhang yige qiye de shehui zeren shi yao 「 zai ziyou shichang de jingzheng xia ， nuli liyong jiyou ziyuan jinxing keyi zuidahua lirun de shangye huodong 」 ， zhe yi shuofa yu yadang·simi renwei shichang tongguo sili keyi zuihao dacheng shehui zong liyi de kanfa yizhi 。\n \n yixie zai zhuliu jingjixue yiwai de jingji xuepai he yanjiu fangshi ye dui jingjixue lingyu you zhongda he chixu de yingxiang ， biru aodili jingji xuepai 、 luosang xuepai 、 houkaien sixuepai 、 sidegeermo xuepai deng 。yu xin gudianzhuyi jingjixue pingxing fazhan de aodili jingji xuepai ， bian shi yanshengzi bianji geming de zhongyao renwu kaer·mengeer de lilun ， er qi xuduo yanjiu kuangjia ye yu zhuliu jingjixue you gaodu chongdie 。\n zai zongti jingjixue shang you xianzhu taolun er zicheng yi pai de hai baokuo le ru xinxing gudian jingji xuepai he gongji mianxuepai deng 。chucizhiwai ， yixie bijiao bu shou zhuliu jingjixue taolun de yanjiu baokuo le shengtai jingjixue 、 zhidu jingjixue 、 yanhua jingjixue 、 yilai lilun deng 。\n \n 19 shiji weiduoliya shidai lishixuejia tuomasi·kalaier ceng fengci de cheng jingjixue wei 「 youyu de kexue 」 。yixie jingjixuejia ru yuehan·situerte·mier he liang·waerlasi ze renwei dui jingjixue de yanjiu bu gai yuqi chanchu de fenpei hunweiyitan ， tamen renwei houzhe suo qianshe de 「 shehui jingjixue 」 shi shuyu zhengzhixue de lingyu 。\n \n zai 《 guofulun 》 yi shu zhong ， yadang·simi dali pengji naxie ta renwei shi yilai zhengzhi quanli lai yingxiang shichang yunzuo de geren huo tuanti ， zai simi de niandai zhexie ren tongchang bei chengwei 「 paixi 」 ， jintian ze shi women suo shuzhi de liyi tuanti liru zhengdang 、 yinhang 、 gongsi 、 gonghui dengdeng 。zuowei shehui kexue de yibufen ， jingjixue yanjiu yinggai yao duli yu zhengfu zhengce huo qita juece tuanti de yingxiang zhiwai ， raner ， zhengce zhidingzhe he zhengzhi renwu jingchang yi teding jingjixue de lilun huo shuoci lai zhengdanghua shi lisuodangran you yingxiangli de ， erqie zai mouzhong chengdu shang keyi shuo shi zhengzhi jingjixue de fenzhi 。xuduo xueshujie de qikan jingchang tantao jingji xuezhe zhijian duiyu mouzhong zengjin shehui zhengti liyi de fangshi \n 。yiju meiguo jingji xuehui de diaocha ， meiguo jingjixuejia zhijian yi dacheng mingxian gongshi de yiti baohan le zhichi ziyou maoyi 、 zhichi woerma deng 2013nian huanqiu jinrong weiji bian yinfa xuduo ren piping zhuliu jingjixue de jiaokeshu yu xianshi tuoli 。guoji huobi jijin zuzhi zai 2002 bian ceng fabiao tamen dui yi qun jingjixuejia diaocha tamen digu le jinsuo de yanzhongxing 。\n \n jingjixue changjiu lai chixu bei zhiyi shi yikao bu shiji de 、 wufa yanzheng de 、 huoshi guodu jianhua de jiashuo lai zuowei lilun yiju ， zhiyizhe zhuzhang
