 zhengzhixue \n \n zhengzhixue shi yi men yi yanjiu zhengzhi xingwei 、 zhengzhi tizhi yiji zhengzhi xiangguan lingyu weizhu de shehui kexue xueke 。zai xifang ， zhengzhixue zai xueshu lingyu li de yanjiu ye bei chengwei zhengzhi yanjiu 、 zhengzhi kexue 、 huo zhiyou zhengzhi liang zi 。zhengzhi xueyi weizhu zai xueshu shang de yanjiu lingyu ， zhengzhi yanjiu ze daibiao le geng guangfan de yanjiu lingyu 。\n \n dui zhengzhi de yanjiu youyu zhengzhixuejiamen dui zhengzhi guocheng de qianshe er biande gengwei fuza ， tamen tichu de xueshuo chang chengwei qita pinglunjia lixiang zhong de zhengzhi kuangjia ， liru jizhe 、 teshu liyi jituan 、 zhengzhijia （ zhengke ） 、 he xuanminmen de yiti fenxi yiji xuanze 。zhengzhi xuejia keneng chengwei mouxie teding zhengzhijia de guwen ， shenzhi zishen touru zhengtan danren gongzhi 。zhengzhi xuejiamen ye chang zai zhengfu bumen li gongzuo ， huo ti mouxie zhengdang gongzuo 。tamen ye you keneng canyu feizhengfu zuzhi huo qita zhengzhi yundong 。shou guo zhengzhixue jiaoyu he xunlian de ren ye keneng juyou shangye qiye he tuanti suo xuyao de jingyan ji jiazhi 。zhiku 、 yanjiu zuzhi 、 yiji he minyi ceyan ji gonggong guanxi youguan de siren qiye ye keneng guyong zhengzhixuejia 。yi meiguo wei li ， zhengzhixuejia bei chengwei 「 meiguo wenti zhuanjia 」 （ Americanists ） ， zhuanzhuyu gezhong shuju ru xuanju 、 yulun he gonggong zhengce （ ru shehui fuli de gaige ） 、 guowai zhengce 、 meiguo guohui quanli 、 he zuigao fayuan zai yixie yiti shang de lichang dengdeng 。\n \n dui zhengzhi de yanjiu zuizao kaishi yu guxila ， zhengzhixue yi ci dansheng yu shehui kexue zhihou 。buguo ， zhe men xueke de qianshen mingxian shi lunlixue 、 zhengzhi zhexue he lishi ， yiji qita weirao zhu yanjiu guojia tese he gongneng de xueshu lingyu 。zai jihu mei yige lishi shidai he zai mei yige difang ， women dou neng kandao yixie zhuanmen yanjiu he xuexi zhengzhi de renshi 。\n \n zhengzhixue de qianshen shenzhi neng zhuisu zhi bolatu he yalishiduode zhiqian de niandai ， youqishi zai xiluoduode 、 hema 、 hexiede 、 xiuxi dide he oulibidesi deng ren de zhuzuo li 。houlai bolatu kaishi fenxi xila chengbang de zhengzhi zhidu ， jiang tamen yuanben yi wenxue he lishi wei fangxiang de yanjiu fenxi chouqu chulai ， yingyong zhi women muqian suo cheng de zhexue shang 。tongyang di ， yalishiduode zai bolatu de fenxi shang you jianli le yi lishi jingyan wei genju de yanjiu ， ji fazhan le yi bijiao fangshi yanjiu zhengzhi ， ye jiu mengsheng le rihou de bijiao zhengzhi lilun ， bei yuwei zhengzhixue zhi fu 。er bolatu de 《 lixiangguo 》 he yalishiduode de 《 zhengzhixue 》 geng bei renwei shi zhengzhixue de chuangshi zhi zuo 。youqishi yalishiduode zai xiangdang chengdu shang zhichu le houlai xifang zhengzhixue yanjiu de zhengque fangxiang 。\n \n zai luoma tongzhi shiqi ， suizhe siduo gexuepai de xingqi ， zhuming de lishixuejia ru bolibia 、 dituo·liwei 、 pulutake ye jizai le luoma gonghe jueqi guocheng ， he qita guojia de zuzhi ji lishi ， yiji kaisa he xisailuo deng zhengzhijia ， shi women deyi gengjia liaojie dangshi luoma de zhengzhi he zhanzheng 。zai dangshi dui zhengzhi de yanjiu zhuyao shi yi dui lishi de xuexi 、 zhengfu zhili de shouduan 、 he miaoshu zhengfu yunzuo de qingkuang wei fangxiang 。er xisailuo geng shi dui guojia （ Res Publica ） gainian jinxing le jieding ， sheji chu le quanli zhiheng de yunzuo moshi ， bing fazhan le ziran fa sixiang 。\n \n suizhu luoma diguo de shuailuo ， zhengzhi yanjiu de wutai gengjia kuosan 。yi shenjiao de jueqi ， youqishi xifang wenhua li jidujiao de jueqi ， zai zhengzhi he zhengzhi xingwei shang chansheng geng duo yanjiu kongjian 。\n \n dao le zhongshiji shiqi ， jiyu dangshi ouzhou fengxing zhengjiaoheyi ， zhengzhixue shangwei chengwei yi duli xueke ， duiyu zhengzhi wenti dou qingxiang you zongjiao jiaoyi lai jieshi ， guci ， dangshi suowei de zhengzhixue ， naili shuyu shenxue 。danshi ， jiaohui he chaoting jian dui zhengzhi de yanjiu rengran xiangdang guangfan 。dangshi de zhengzhi yanjiu yi xibo de aogusiding de jiaofu shenxue he tuomasi·akuina de jingyuan zhexue wei daibiao 。\n \n xibo de aogusiding suo zhu de 《 shangdi zhi cheng 》 yi shu zonghe le dangshi jidujiao de zhexue he zhengzhi chuantong ， chongxin dingyi le zongjiao yu zhengzhi jian de lingyu jiexian 。daduoshu zhege shidai de zhengzhi yiti dou weiraoyu jiaohui yu guojia jian de lichang chengqing he huxiang jingzheng 。er akui na jiang xila zhexue he jidujiao shenxue jinxing le youji jiehe ， bingqie lunzheng le xinyang 、 lixing 、 daode he zhengzhi jiefen de kenengxing 。\n \n zai zhongdong he houlai qita de yisilan diqu ， oumaer·haiyamu suo zhu de 《 lubai shiji 》 yiji feierduo xi suo zhu de guowang de shishili dou tigong le dui zhengzhi de fen de ， er qita yalishiduo depai de yisilan xuezhe ru aweisenna ye jixu yanjiu yalishiduode de fenxi he jingyanzhuyi ， xiexia xuduo zhendui yalishiduode zuopin de pinglun 。er zai gudai zhongguo ， dui zhengzhi de yanjiu zhuyao shi zhiding liyue 、 bingxing 、 zhiguan deng dianzhang zhidu ， yu xiandai de zhengzhi yanjiu cunzai xiangdang da de chayi 。\n \n wenyi fuxing shi xifang zhengzhixue yanjiu de zhongyao zhuanzhedian 。zhengzhixue kaishi baituo shenxue de shufu ， renmen yi lixing he jingyan de yanguang lai guancha he jieshi zhengzhi xianxiang 。yidali de nikeluo·majiya weili shuli le xiandai zhengzhixue de yanjiu zhongdian ， zhendui zhengzhi jigou he zhengzhi canyuzhe zuo zhijie de guancha ， qi zhuzuo 《 junzhulun 》 ， jiaodao junzhu qi zhigu houguo bugu guocheng de zhengzhi shouduan ， neirong yu jidujiao jiaoyi chongtu shen da 。《 junzhulun 》 de wancheng ， bei shiwei zhengzhixue you jidujiao zhong wanquan fenli de yige lichengbei 。houlai zai qimeng shidai li ， xueshu lingyu de kuozhang jinyibu de tuoguang zhengzhixue de yanjiu fanwei ， 
 faxue \n \n faxue （ jurisprudence 、 legal theory ） shi shehui kexue zhong yi men teshu de xueke ， yanjiu falv ci yi teding shehui xianxiang jiqi guilv 。suoyou de zhixu dou keyi shuo shi yi zhong 「 falv 」 ， liru ziran guilv 、 lunchang 、 luoji faze huo meixue ， er faxue jiushi yanjiu falv de faze 。suiran xuduo faxuejia ， liru 、 ， rending faxue meiyou xueshu xingzhi ， raner faxue yanjin zhijin reng baohan you falv zhexue 、 falv shixue yiji falv kexue deng sanda bumen 。ciwai ， you yinwei yanjiu duixiang dou shi shehui shang de xianxiang ， yinci faxue yu zhengzhixue 、 jingjixue 、 caizhengxue 、 shehuixue he xinlixue deng shehui kexue you xiangdang chengdu de miqie guanlian 。\n \n faxue sixiang zui zao yuanyuanyu dongzhou shiqi de fajia zhexue sixiang ， ru guanzi zhuzhang ： 「 fazhe ， suoyi xinggong jubao ye ； lvzhe ， suoyi dingfenzhizheng ye 。 」zai oumei diqu de chuantong zhong ， guluoma faxuejia wuerbian dui faxueyici de dingyi shi ： 「 renshi he shenshi de gainian ， zhengyi he feizhengyi zhi xue 」 ， helan faxuejia gelaoxiusi renwei faxue shi renlei yanjiuzun cong zhengyi er shenghuo de xueke 。wenyi fuxing shiqi ， faxueyu daxue zhongbei shou zhongshi ， wei dangshi xueshujie zui ju diwei de kexi zhiyi ， yu yixue ji shenxue sanzudingli 。zai lishi yanjin guocheng zhong xian you xisu ， ranhou you lunli fenli chu falv ， zuihou cai you daode ， danshi xiangduiyu xisu yu daode ， falv juyou guding yiji qiangzhi de texing ， ye baohan renmin shenghuo zhong xianshi kexing de quanli ， qitu jieshi lixiang shijie de yingran faze 。\n \n faxue （ ） cong gudai ladingyu zhong de \" Juris prudentia \" yanbian er lai ， yuanyi shi falv de yanjiu 、 zhishi huo xuewen ， qizhong juris shi jus de suoyouge ， yisi shi falv de ； prudentia shi shenzhong ， yi ji kaolv zhoudao 、 xianjian 、 xixin ， tebieshi zai shiji xingshi zhong yunyong gaoming panduan zhiyi 。zai meiguo yujing zhong ， faxue tongchang zhicheng falv zhexue ， zhuyao you si da yanjiu mianxiang ， shouyao shi xunqiu fenxi 、 jieshi 、 liqing yu pipan falv benti ， dier zhong zaiyu bijiao falv yiji qita zhong xuewen ru wenxue 、 jingji 、 zongjiao 、 shehui kexue de neirong ， disan wei jiexi falv teding zhuti de lishi 、 daode huo wenhua beijing ， zuihou ze shi zhuanzhuyu huida 「 falv weihe ？ 」 、 「 faguan ruhe gongzheng panjue ？ 」 deng chouxiang wenti 。\n \n zai zhongguo cong xizhou kaishi ， jiu you wanzheng xingzheng zhidu ， er zhouli yi shu ， kewei jigongfa yu sifa zhi dacheng ， ye shi shitifa yu chengxufa de zonghui ， erqie xueshu shang baijiazhengming ， sixiang ziyou fada ， cong guanzhong kaishi ， baohan shangyang 、 shenbuhai 、 yinwen 、 shendao 、 hanfei deng ren ， houren chengzhiwei fajia ， duo yin zhongfa er shide qi guochangsheng 。faxue yi ci ， zaixian qinshi bei chengwei xingming zhi xue ， zi handai kaishi you lvxue de mingcheng ， dao tangdai ze shi chengshu shiqi ， xianhou you wudelv 、 zhen guanlv 、 yonghuilv ji kaiyuanlv deng fadian ， er 《 siku tiyao 》 dui 《 tanglv shuyi 》 de shuoming tidao ： 「 lunzhe wei tanglv yizhun huli ， yiwei churu de gujin zhi ping 。 」keyi shuo shi zhonghua chuantong zhong duiyu falv yanjiu de qingchu biaozhun ， ye jiushi faguzi 「 fa 」 zai 《 shuowen 》 zhong de jieshi ： 「 xing ye 。pingzhirushui ， gu cong shui 。zhi suoyi chubuzhizhe qu zhi ， gu cong zhi cong qu 。 」\n\nren de xingwei zhongdu you mouzhong yingran de faze ， er guifan renlei yizhi he xingwei de lunli faze keyi qufen wei daode 、 xisu yiji falv 。qianshu falv shi sanzhe zhizhong weiyi juyou xialie si xiang texing de faze ， waizai guanxin quxiang 、 waizai panduan fangshi 、 waizai mudi zhuti yiji waizai xiaoli laiyuan 。yejiushishuo ， falv guanxin xingwei suo chansheng de jieguo er bushi neixin de yitu ， zhiyao xingwei fuhe falv tiaowen jiu shuyu hefa xingwei ， er falv lingyu zhong you xiangdui quanli yiwu de zhuti ， bingqie you lifazhe yu zhongcaizhe 。deguo zhuming faxuejia gusitafu·ladebuluhe renwei ， falv juyou sanda jiazhi ： gonggong liyi 、 faming quexing yiji zhengyi ， raner yinwei ren de buwanmei zhe sanda jiazhi bingbu zongshi hexie gongcunyu meibu falv zhizhong 。\n \n cong daode 、 xisu 、 falv 、 guojia 、 kexue 、 yishu he zongjiao zhexie wenhua neirong zhong ， yizhao butong de xuepai ceng you sanda tixi lai taolun falv de mudi ， zaojiu fazhi guojia 、 wenhua guojia 、 yiji weiquan guojia deng butong xingtai de falv neirong 。shouxian shi shibashiji mo ， kangde 、 xilei 、 hongbote deng ren renwei ziyou de lunli renge shi zui gao de jiazhi ， er yishu he kexue zhishi renge jiaoyang de gongju ， falv he guojia zhishi ta de baohu jizhi ， yushi falv jinjin juyou gerenzhuyi lunli de congshu jiazhi ， er meiyou zishen de jiazhi ， zhejiu shi fazhi guojia zhong pubian renwei falv zhishi lixing mudi de jishuxing guifan 。zai weiquan guojia zhong ， duo yiwei minzu guojia 、 quanli jiqi chengzhang shi renshijian zui gao de shiming ， guojia fuyu suoyou geren daode de neirong ， suoyou wenhua chengguo dou shi wei guojia fuwu ， ru heigeer 、 zhexie lilunjia dou ba guojia shiwei yige zhengti ， renlei jiushi zhiti ， er zhiti shi weile zhengti er cunzai ， falv juyou chaohu geren de zishen jiazhi 。zuihou shi wenhua guojia ， ru duonisi zai 《 shehui yu shequn 》 zhong miaoshu ， shengming de zuigao shiming bu zaiyu geren huo jiti de renge shang ， er zai chuangzao he yiliu xialai de chengjiu yiji chengjiu de zonghe ， ye jiushi wenhua ， er guojia de zuigao shiming ye zaiyu baohu zhexie wenhua gongzuo 。\n \n falv de zhiding bujin you you zuzhi de zuqun huo guojia de chengwenfa ， ye keyi congmeiyou zuzhi de shequn zhong ningju xiguan er cheng ， raner guojia bujin shi falv de zhuyao laiyuan ， ta tongshi ye shi falv de chanwu ： guojia de lixian jiqi zai fali shang de diwei ， shi cong xianfa he xiangguan falv yanyi dedao de 。yejiushishuo ， guojia yushe le xianfa ， er xianfa you yi guojia wei qianti 。shishishang ， guojia yu xianfa shi yiti liangmian ， jiu xiang youjiwu he ta de zuzhi hen nan bici fenli 。lixian sixiang jianyu mengdesijiu 《 lunfa de jingshen 》 de san  shehuixue \n \n shehuixue （ ） qiyuanyu 19shiji moqi ， shi yi men yanjiu shehui de xueke 。shehuixue shiyong gezhong yanjiu fangfa jinxing shizheng diaocha he pipan fenxi ， yi fazhan ji wanshan yi tao youguan renlei shehui jiegou ji huodong de zhishi tixi ， bing hui yi yunyong zhexie zhishi qu xunqiu huo gaishan shehui fuli wei mubiao 。shehuixue de yanjiu fanwei guangfan ， baokuo le you weiguan cengji de shehui xingdong (agency ) huo renji hudong ， zhi hongguan cengji de shehui xitong huo jiegou ， shehuixue de benti you shehui zhong de geren 、 shehui jiegou 、 shehui bianqian 、 shehui wenti 、 he shehui kongzhi ， yinci shehuixue tongchang gen jingjixue 、 zhengzhixue 、 renleixue 、 xinlixue deng xueke bing lieyu shehui kexue lingyu zhixia 。\n \n shehuixue zai yanjiu ticai shang huo yanjiufa ze shang jun you xiangdang de guangfanxing ， qi chuantong yanjiu duixiang baokuo le shehui fenceng 、 shehui jieji 、 shehui liudong 、 shehui zongjiao 、 shehui falv 、 yuegui xingwei deng ， er caiqu de moshi ze baokuo dingxing he dingliang de yanjiu fangfa 。youyu renlei huodong de suoyou lingyu dou shi you shehui jiegou 、 geti jigou de yingxiang xia suzao er cheng ， suoyi suizhu shehui fazhan ， shehuixue jinyibu kuoda qi yanjiu zhongdian zhi qita xiangguan kemu ， liru yiliao 、 huli 、 junshi huo xingshi zhidu 、 wangji wanglu deng ， shenzhi shi liru kexue zhishi fazhan zai shehui huodong zhong de zuoyong yilei de keti 。lingyifangmian ， shehui kexue fangfa (social scientific methods) de fanwei ye yuelaiyue guangfan 。zai 20 shiji zhongye yilai duoyanghua de yuyan 、 wenhua zhuanbian ye tongshi chansheng le geng duo geng ju quanshixing 、 zhexuexing de shehui yanjiu moshi 。raner ， zi 20shiji moqi de keji langchao ， ye wei shehuixue dailai le zhanxin de shuxuehua jisuan fenxi jishu ， liru geti wei benmoxing he shejiao wanglu 。\n \n yin qi xingqi de lishi beijing ， shehuixue yanjiu de zhongxin hen dayi bufen fang zai xiandaixing shehui zhong de gezhong shenghuo shitai ， huoshi dangdai shehui ruhe xingcheng yanjin yizhi jinri de guocheng ， budan zhuzhong miaoshu xiankuang ， ye bu hulve shehui bianqian 。shehuixue de yanjiu duixiang fanwei guangfan ， xiao dao ji geren mianduimian de richang hudong ， da dao quanqiuhua de shehui qushi ji chaoliu 。jiating 、 geshigeyang de zuzhi 、 qiye gongchang deng jingjiti 、 chengshi 、 shichang 、 zhengdang 、 guojia 、 wenhua 、 meiti deng dou shi shehuixue yanjiu de duixiang ， er zhexie yanjiu duixiang de gongtongdian shi yixie juyou shehuixing de shehui shishi 。suiran 「 shehuixing 」 de dingyi zai butong xuepai zhijian reng you zhengzhi ， dan shehui shishi waizaiyu geren ， qie dui geren de xingwei gen renzhi you yingxiang ， zhe yidian shi dazhi shang wei shehui xuezhe suo gongtong jieshou de 。\n \n zai 19shiji chuqi ， kongde renwei guoqu shenxue de shiqi ， zhezhong guoduxing de chongtu ji hunluan shi wukebimian 。zai jiu zhidu xiaoshi qian ， renmen wufa tiyan xin zhidu ， wangwang xuyao duoci shehui zhuanbian caineng gaizu shehui 。shehuixue jiushi zhendui shehui gaizu de wenti （ xiandaixing ） er fazhan chengwei yi men shehui kexue 。tuer ganxuepai de shehuixuejia budan xiwang liaojie shenme shide shehui tuanti juji qilai ， geng xiwang liaojie shehui wajie de fazhan guocheng ， conger zuochu “ jiuzheng ” 。jiuzheng de guannian bingbu anshi shehuixuejia yushe yige 「 zhengque shehui 」 de muban 。tuer ganbenren dou bu renwei you yige zhongji de 、 wanmei de shehui keyi cankao 。jiandan laishuo ， dang yi qun ren hudong xingcheng yige wending de cankao jiagou ， yunxing liangjiu ， dui tamen laishuo jiushi 「 changtai 」 。dang shehui \nxiangfandi ， falankefu xuepai de shehuixuejia bingbu tansuo dui jiuzheng shehui de fangfa 。yinwei tamen renwei dui shehui bingji tichu de jiuzheng fangan ， wangwang shi yi yige xiao qunti de shenghuo de fenliehua 。youqishi zai yishu wenhua lingyu ， daliang fuzhi jishu de chuxian ， zaocheng yishu jingshen de sangshi 。falankefu dier dai habomasi jicheng shangshu guandian ， bing canzhao cai shi beiguan xiandaixing de chulu 。er shangshu de guannian ， leisi shehui chongtulun ， zhiming renshi ru dalundaofu ， ye shi yi makesi dui shehui jieji fenxi weizhu ， renwei shehui you zhangwo ziyuan de de jieji ， yiji shou tongzhi de jieji ， wei butong de shi ， makesi renwei zichanjieji woyou shengchan gongju ， wuchanjieji yin wu gongju er shou zaizhi ， xuyao fankang geming ， guandian jiao shuyu zhengzhi jingjixue ， dan chongtu lunzhe ， jiehe weibo dui jieceng ── jiaru shehui diwei deng jiaodu ， renwei shehui bu pingdeng ， yuanziduo fangmian ， buzhi jingji bu pingdeng 。\n \n jintian ，  junshi xue\n \n junshi xue yu shen duo fanchou youguan ， zhuyao yu zhanzheng youguan 。ciwai ， junshi xuebenshen baohan le gezhong xuewen 。junshi shi zhengzhi de yibufen ， zhanzheng shi zhengzhi de yi zhong yanxu ， shi yi guo huozhe jituan yong baoli shouduan dadao ziji mubiao he mudi de fangshi ， er mubiao he mudi wangwang yu liyi youguan 。zhanzheng shi junshi de jizhong tixian ， dan bushi weiyi de tixian 。dier ci shijie dazhan （ 1939nian － 1945nian ） hou de meiguo he sulian lengzhan ， jiushi yi zhong weishe jichu shang de huibi zhanzheng fangshi de douzheng 。zai renlei keyi kandao de weilai ， junshi shizhong shi zhengzhi shenghuo zhong zhongyao de fangmian ， bing zai kexue jishu shang dui renlei shenghuo yu zhongda yingxiang ： renlei henduo keji chengjiu wangwang xian chansheng yu junshi lingyu ranhou puji dao feijunshi lingyu de 。\n \n xiandai junshi baokuo junshi lilun he junshi keji liang dabufen 。\n \n \n \n genju zhonghua renmin gongheguo jiaoyubu de dingyi ， qi xiashu de yiji xueke you ： junshi sixiang ji junshi lishi 、 zhanlvexue 、 zhanyixue 、 zhanshuxue 、 jundui zhihuixue 、 junzhixue 、 jundui zhengzhi gongzuo 、 junshi houqinxue 、 junshi zhuangbeixue 、 junshi xunlianxue 。\n \n

 wulixue \n\n wulixue （ ， ziran ） shi yanjiu wuzhi 、 nengliang de benzhi yu xingzhi de ziran kexue 。youyu wuzhi yu nengliang shi suoyou kexue yanjiu de bixu sheji de jiben yaosu ， suoyi wulixue shi ziran kexue zhong zui jichu de xueke zhiyi 。wulixue shi yi zhong shiyan kexue ， wulixuezhe cong guance yu fenxi daziran de gezhong jiyu wuzhi yu nengliang de xianxiang lai zhaochu qizhong de moshi 。zhexie moshi chengwei 「 wuli lilun 」 ， jingdeqi shiyan jianyan de changyong wuli lilun chengwei wuli dinglv ， zhidao youyitian bei zhengming shi you cuowu weizhi (ju ke fouzheng xing) 。wulixue shi you zhexie dinglv jingzhi di jiangou er cheng 。wulixue shi ziran kexue zhong zui jichu de xueke zhiyi 。huaxue 、 shengwuxue 、 kaoguxue dengdeng kexue xueshu lingyu de lilun dou shi jiangou yu zhexie wuli dinglv 。\n \n wulixue shi zui gulao de xueshu zhiyi 。wulixue 、 huaxue 、 shengwuxue dengdeng yuanben dou guishuyu ziran zhexue de fanchou ， zhidao shiqi shiji zhi shijiu shiji qijian ， cai jianjian di cong ziran zhexue zhong fenbie chengzhang wei duli de xueshu lingyu 。wulixue yu qita henduo kua lingyu yanjiu you xiangdang de jiaoji ， ru liangzi huaxue 、 shengwu wulixue dengdeng 。wulixue de jiangjie bingbu shi guding bu bian de ， wulixue li de chuangshi tupo shichang keyi yonglai jieshi zhexie kualingyu yanjiu de jichu jizhi ， youshi hai hui kaiqi zhanxin de kualingyu yanjiu 。\n \n tongguo chuangjian xin lilun yu fazhan xin keji ， wulixue duiyu renlei wenming you jiwei xianzhu de gongxian 。liru ， youyu diancixue de kuaisu fazhan ， diandeng 、 diandongji 、 jiayong dianqi deng xin chanpin fenfen yongxian ， renlei shehui de shenghuo shuiping ye dedao dafu tisheng 。youyu hezi wulixue riqu chengshu ， heneng fadian yi bu zai shi lantu gouxiang ， dan qi suo yinzhi de anquan wenti ye shi renmen yishi dao diqiu huanjing 、 shengtai yu renlei de cuiruo miaoxiao 。\n \n 「 wuli 」 yi ci zai yingwen li shi 「 physics 」 ， zuixian chuziyu guxi lawen 「 」 ， yuanyi shi 「 ziran 」 。zai zhongwen li ， zhe ci zui zao ke zai zhanguo shiqi yishu 《 heguanzi·wangfupian 》 zhaodao ， 「 yuanwen qi renqing wuli suoyi sewanwu yu tiandi zong yu shenming tizheng zhi dao 。 」zai zheli ， 「 wuli 」 zhi de shi yiqie shiwu zhi daoli 。sanguo shiqi ， yangquanzhu you 《 wulilun 》 ， shi zui zao de shuming hanyou 「 wuli 」 yi ci de zhuzuo 。mingmo qingchu kexuejia fangyizhi shoudao xixue yingxiang ， zhuanxie le baikequanshushi zhuzuo 《 wuli xiaoshi 》 ， zai zheli ， 「 wuli 」 de hanyi yi yanhua wei xueshu zhili ， baokuo ziran kexue de ge men lingyu yu ren wenxue de bufen lingyu 。\n \n qingchao yapian zhanzheng hou ， xifang kexue chuanru zhongguo ， cishi de yizhe jiang 「 physics 」 fanyi wei 「 gezhixue 」 huo 「 gewuxue 」 。「 gewuzhizhi 」 zhe ci yuanziyu 《 liji ． daxue 》 ： 「 zhizhi zai gewu ， gewuerhouzhizhi 」 ， yong baihua shuo ， 「 ruo yao zengjin zhishi ， bixu qiongjiu shiwu zhili ， weiyou qiongjiu shiwu zhili ， cai ke zengjin zhishi 」 。zhe ju hua zhichu ， mingliao shiwu shi zengjin zhishi de guanjian fangfa 。zai wulixue li ， shichang hui liyong guancha 、 moni 、 shiyan 、 tuilun 、 yanyi deng fangfa lai huode zhishi 。yinci ， jiang 「 physics 」 fanyi wei 「 gezhixue 」 huo 「 gewuxue 」 sihu you daoli 。\n zhongguo zhanguo zhexuejia mingjia huishi 、 dengxi he gongsunlong ， yiji mojia ， ceng nuli zuanyan yuzhou jian wanwu goucheng de yuanyin 。huishi you shi ge mingti ， zhuyao shi dui ziranjie de fenxi ， qizhong youxie hanyou bianzheng de yuansu 。ta shuo ： “ zhi da wu wai ， wei zhi dayi ； zhi xiao wu nei ， wei zhi xiao yi 。 ” 。“ dayi ” shi zhi zhengge kongjian da dao wusuobubao ， bu zaiyou waibu ； “ xiao yi ” shi zhi wuzhi zui xiao de danwei ， xiao dao buke zai fenge ， bu zaiyou neibu 。mingjia de sixiang hetong yiyihuishi wei daibiao ， renwei “ tian yu dibei ， shan yu zeping ” ， wanwu “ biyi ” ben wei “ bitong ” ， bing wu qubie 。houqi mojia renwei wuzhi shijie shi you weixiao de buke zai fenge de wuzhi lizi suo goucheng 。\n \n cong gudai yilai ， renmen jiu changshi zhe liaojie daziran de aomiao ： weishenme wutihuiwang dimian diaoluo ， weishenme butong de wuzhi hui juyou butong de xingzhi ？ruci dengdeng 。cong guance yu fenxi daziran de xianxiang ， zaoqi renmen zhaodao qizhong de yangshi ， bing zhendui zhexie yangshi tichu le gezhong lilun ， shitu jieshi daziran de aomiao ， raner tamen suo tichu de daduoshu lilun dou bu zhengque 。yi xiandai zhunze laikan ， zaoqi de wuli lilun geng xiang shi yixie zhexue lilun ： xiandai de lilun dou xuyao jingguo yange de shiyan jianyan ， er naxie zaoqi de lilun bingmeiyou jingguo yange zhengshi 。xiang tuoleimi he yalishiduode tichu de lilun zhong ， youxie jiu yu richang suo neng guancha dao de shishi xiangbei 。\n \n jinguan ruci ， reng you xuduo gu xuezhe gongxian chu xiangdang zhengque de lilun 。gu xila zhexuejia taileisi （ yue qian 624nian －yue qian 546nian ） cengjing yuandu dizhonghai ， zai meisuo bu da miya aiji xuexi tianwenxue yu jihe ， hai jiayi tuiguang yanshen ， fayang guangda 。ta yuce chu gongyuanqian 585nian fasheng de rishi ， hai nenggou gusuan chuanzhi lian bian de juli ， you cong jinzita de yinying jisuan chu qi gaodu 。taileisi jujue yilai xuanyi huo chaoziran yinsu lai jieshi ziran xianxiang ， ta zhuzhang ， renhe shijian de fasheng dou you qi bu bian yu pushi de yinguo guanxi 。gongyuanqian 5 shiji gu xila zhexuejia liu jibo yu xuesheng demokelite shuaixian tichu yuanzilun ， renwei suoyou wuzhi jie shi you bu hui huihuai 、 bukefenge de yuanzi suo goucheng 。gu xila de sixiangjia ajimide zai zuoyongli fangmian tuidao chu xuduo zhengque de dingliang jielun ， ru duiyu ganggan yuanli de jieshi 。\n \n cong xiyuan 850nian zhi 950nian jian ， daliang xila xueshu bei fanyi cheng alabowen 。musilin kexuejia cong xilaren jicheng le yalishiduo dewu lixue 。zai yisilan huangjin shidai ， tamen jiang zhexie xueshu fayang guangda ， tebie qiangdiao guance de dongzuo ， fazhan chu yi zhong zaoqi xingshi de kexue fangfa 。 .\n 、 kendi 、 haishenmu 、 yiben·xina dengdeng kexuejia zai guangxue yu shijue lingyu geichu chuangxin lilun 。haishenmu zai zhuming zhuzuo 《 》 （ Kita b al - Manazir ） li ， jianding di bochi le gu xila de shijue lilun —— fashe shuo ， bingqie geichu anshi 」 ， guangxian jinru yige xiaodong hou ， zai anshi xingcheng diandao yingxiang 。hen mingxian di ， zai zheli ， ta suo zhi de shi zhenkong xiangji huo anxiang 。ta hai miaoshu zenyang yong anshi lai guance rishi 。\n\nhai shenmu de chengjiu zai alabo shijie bingmeiyou dedao yingyou de zhongshi 。shier shiji ， ta de zhuzuo bei fanyi chengladingwen ， shuming wei 《 toushi 》 （ Perspectiva ） 。zhizhi shiqishiji ， zhe zhuzuo zai ouzhou shi guangxue de biaozhun cankaoshu ， qianglie yingxiang le houlai yuehanneisi·kaipulei 、 、 luojie·peigen dengdeng kexuejia de yanjiu 。\n \n jingdian wulixuezhi de shi bu sheji dao liangzi lixue huo xiangduilun de wulixue ， liru ， niudun lixue 、 relixue 、 makeshiwei diancixue dengdeng 。jingdian wulixue de shengqi kaishi yu shiliushiji de diyi ci kexue geming ， zhongzhi yu shijiushiji mo 。nigula·gebaini daxiang le kexue geming de diyi qiang ， ta yu 1543nian tichu le miaoshu taiyang xitong de rixinshuo ， zhe lilun tuifan le tuo leimi de dixin shuo 。zai 1609nian yu 1619nian qijian ， yuehanneisi·kebolei fabiao le zhudao xingxing yundong de dinglv ， tayong shuxue fangcheng zhunque gusuan chu cong tianwen guance huode de xingxing raozhu taiyang de le wengu de jichu ， ta chuangjian le weijifen ， geichu yi zhong xin de gao gongneng shuxue fangfa lai yanxi wuli wenti 。ta wei diyi ci kexue geming huashang le wanmei de zhongzhifu 。wulixue zhanxian diancixue wufa jieshi guangdian xiaoying yu yuanzi guangpu ， fangshexing wuzhi de wuli xingzhi maosi yu jingdian wulixue de juedinglun beidaoerchi 。zhexie xiaci gei xueshujie dailai le yi chang zhe shuyu tongji lixue lingyu 。cong tongji lixue de lilun keyi tuidao chu relixue dinglv 。tongji lixue yingyong jilv lunlai yanjiu you daliang lizi zucheng de xitong de wuli xingwei 。tongji lixue de tongshi ， ye biaoshu chunei han de shuxue gainian 。liru ， genju liangzi lixue de shuxue biaoshu ， zai liangzi lixue li ， you liang ge jichu gainian ： wuli xitong de liangzitai shi yi xierbote zhijian wubi shenao de guanxi 。liru ， 1915nian ， guangyi xiangduilun zuichu chuangli zhi shi ， shang meiyou shenme laokao de jingyanxing guance jichu ， ta zai dangshi suo neng jieshi de zui zhuming xianxiang jiushi niudun lixue wufa jieshi de shuixing jinri dian de fanchang jindong 。1919nian tianti wuli xuezhe yase·aidingdun jueshi guance dao le guangyi xiangduilun yuyan de guangxian zai taiyang yinlichang zhong de pianzhe （ zhe yi shiyan zhidao 1959nian cai kaishi bei jingque di dingliang celiang ） ， zhe zai dangshi shi dui guangyi xiangduilun zui youli de zhichi 。shizhijinri ， guangyi xiangduilun de lilun yuce yi you shiyan celiang jieguo zhengshi 。\n \n wulixue shi yi men jichu kexue ， bushi yingyong kexue 。wulixue ye bei renwei shi jichu kexue zhong de jichu kexue ， yinwei qita zhuanzhuyu yuanzi chicun ， zheshi huaxue yu wuli de zhuyao jiexian ） 。jiegou de xingcheng shi yinwei lizi yu lizi zhijian bici xianghu zuoyong 。nengliang shouheng 、 dongliang shouheng 、 dianhe shouheng deng ， zhexie wuli dinglv zhudao le wuzhi xingzhi he huaxue fanying 。\n \n yingyong wulixuezhi de shi zhendui shiji yongtu er jinxing de wuli yanjiu 。yingyong wulixue de kecheng guihua tongchang hui xuanxiu yixie yingyong xueke de kecheng ， xiang dizhixue huo dianji gongchengxue 。yingyong wulixue yu gongchengxue butong ， yingyong wulixue bu hui tebie di sheji mouzhong yuanjian huo jiqi ， ershi yong wuli lilun huo congshi wuli yanjiu lai fazhan mouzhong xin keji huo jiexi mou wenti 。\n \n gongchengxue yingyong dao henduo wuli lilun 。liru ， zai xuexi jianzao qiaoliang yu qita yixie tanbensuyuan 、 gewuzhizhi de fangfa ye ke yongyu kuaxueke lingyu 。wulixue huoduohuoshao di yingxiang le henduo zhongyao xueshu lingyu ， liru ， yingyong daliang wulixue li de lilun yu fangfa lai jianshi bixu yongyou zhuachu kexue lilun de xiaci de nengli 。kaer·bopuer qiangdiao ， kexue lilun bixu juyou kezheng weixing 。huanjuhuashuo ， bixu nenggou duiyu lilun yuyan yu shiyan jieguo zuo bijiao ， jiaruo liangzhe bu yizhi ， ze bu neng chengren zhe kexue lilun de zhengquexing 。raner jinqi ， youxie xianlilun xuezhe yu yuzhouxue xuezhe zhuzhang ， yige zugou jingzhi bingqie nenggou dui xiangguan gainian ， shi wufa zuo shiyan guance dao de 。zai yuzhouxue fangmian ， duozhong yuzhoulun 、 qian da baozha lilun dou sheji dao wufa guance dao de lunshu 。lilun wuli xuezhe baoluo·sitaienhate biaoshi ， yiban shi fenkai jinxing de ， raner tamen bici zhijian xixixiangguan 、 queyibuke 。shiyan jieguo duiyu lilun fazhan geichu jianyi ， lilun yuce duiyu shiyan sheji geichu yinling 。\n guoqu jibai nian lai ， shiyan jieguo qushi le lilun wuli de jinzhan ， zuijin jishi nian lai ， wulixue de yanjin fangshi yi dafudu gaibian ， zai mouxie wuli xuefen zhi lingyu ， lilun yuce qushi le shiyan wuli de fangxiang  tianwenxue \n \ntian wenxue shi yi men ziran kexue ， ta yunyong shuxue 、 wuli he huaxue deng fangfa lai jieshi yuzhou jian de tianti ， baokuo xingxing 、 weixing 、 huixing 、 hengxing 、 xingxi dengdeng yanjiu fanwei 。\n \n wuli yuzhouxue yu tianwenxue miqie xiangguan ， dan ta ba yuzhou shiwei yige zhengti lai yanjiu 。\n \ntian wenxue you zhu yuangu de lishi 。ziyou wenzi jizai qi ， babilun 、 guxila 、 yindu 、 gu aiji 、 nubiya 、 yilang 、 zhongguo 、 maya yiji xuduo gudai meizhou wenming jiu you dui yekong zuo xiangjin de guance jilu 。\n \ntian wenxue zai lishi shang hai sheji dao tianti celiang xue 、 shi fusheceng ， zheli de denglizi tiyi fushe de xingshi ba nengliang chuandi chulai 。fusheceng yiwai shi dui liuceng ， zheli de qiti yi duiliu de xingshi ba nengliang chuandi dao waiceng 。kexuejia xiangxin ， dui liuceng qiti de fangun yundong suo chansheng de cichang huodong daozhi le taiyang lizi de xingcheng 。\n \n taiyang shishikeke dou cong biaomian xiang wai penshe daliang de dengliziti  lixue \n \n lixue shi wulixue de yige fenzhi ， zhuyao yanjiu nengliang heli yiji tamen yu wuti de pingheng 、 bianxing huo yundong de guanxi 。\n renmen zai richang laodong zhong shiyong ganggan 、 le xitong yanjiu ， queding tamen de jiben guilv ， chubu dianding le jingli xue ， ji pingheng lilun de jichu ， gu xila kexuejia yalisiduode ye tichu zuoyongli zaocheng yundong de zhuzhang ， ji wuti bu shouli ， bijiang tingzhi 。\n \n zi wenyi fuxing zhihou ， kexue geming xingqi ， jialilve de ziyou luoti yundong guilv ， yiji niudun de sanda yundong dinglv jie dianding le donglixue de jichu 。lixue lixue zhuyao ke fenwei gudian lixue ji liangzi lixue 。\n \n ruo yi faxian de shijian laikan ， gudian lixue jiao zao bei faxian ， qiyuanyu niudun de sanda yundong dinglv ， liangzi lixue ze shi 20shiji  dilixue \n\n dilixue shi guanyu diqiu jiqi tezheng 、 jumin he xianxiang de xuewen 。ta shi yanjiu diqiu biaoceng ge quanceng xianghu zuoyong guanxi ， jiqi kongjian chayi yu bianhua guocheng de xueke tixi 。\n\n dilixuejia zai chuantong shang bei shiwei he dituxuejia tongyi lei ， renwei liangzhe dou yanjiu diming yu shuzi 。suiran henduo dilixuejia dou jingli guo di mingxue ji ditu xue de xunlian ， dan liangzhe dou bushi tamen de guanzhu zhongdian 。dilixuejia yanjiu zhongduo xianxiang 、 guocheng 、 tezheng yiji renlei he ziran huanjing de xianghu guanxi zai kongjian ji shijian shang de fenbu 。yinwei kongjian ji shijian yingxiang le duozhong zhuti liru jingji 、 jiankang 、 qihou 、 zhiwu ji dongwu ， suoyi dilixue shi yige gaodu kuaxue kexing de xueke 。\n\n dilixue zuowei yige xueke keyi culve fenwei liang ge lingyu ： ziran dilixue ji renwen dilixue 。ziran dilixue diaocha ziran huanjing ji ruhe zaocheng dixing ji qihou 、 shui 、 turang 、 zhibei 、 shengming de gezhong xianxiang ji tamen de xianghu guanxi 。renwen dilixue zhuanzhuyu renlei jianzao de huanjing he kongjian shi ruhe bei renlei zhizao 、 kandai ji guanli yiji renlei ruhe yingxiang qi zhanyong de kongjian 。yinwei yishang liangzhe de yuanyin ， shiyong butong de fangfa ling disan lingyu chuxian ， wei huanjing dilixue 。huanjing dilixue zai ziran dilixue yu renwen dilixue de yanjiu chengguo shang ， pingjia renlei yu ziran de xianghu guanxi ， bing tichu renlei zhengfu ziran 、 gaizao ziran yi shiying zishen yongxu fazhan de anquan zhuangtai he jishu （ baokuo shengchan jishu he zhidu jishu ） tiaojian 。\n \n de zigen laizi （ Geographia ） ， you geo （ yuanyi wei dadi ） he \" \" （ yiwei “ xie ” ） ， zimian yisi wei dui dadi de miaoshu 。zuizao shiyong \" Geography \" de renwei ailatuositeni ， tayong ci ci lai biaoshi yanjiu dibiao jingwu de xuewen 。\n \n zhongguo gudai chengyu di huo yudixue ， 。riben zai mingzhi weixin hou ， jiang yiwei dili ， zhihou chuanru zhongguo 。\n \n 1902nian ， guangxu huangdi jieshou libu  dizhixue \n\n dizhixue （ fayu 、 deyu ： Geologie ；； ladingyu 、 xibanyayu ： Geologia ； yuanyu xilayu γῆ he λoγ ία ）shi dui diqiu de qiyuan tantao yali yu shijian 、 lishi he jiegou jinxing yanjiu de xueke 。zhuyao yanjiu diqiu de wuzhi zucheng 、 neibu gouzao 、 waibu tezheng 、 ge quanceng jian de xianghu zuoyong he yanbian lishi 。zai xianjieduan ， youyu guancha 、 yanjiu tiaojian de xianzhi ， zhuyao yi yanshiquan wei yanjiu duixiang ， bing sheji shuiquan 、 daqiquan 、 shengwuquan he yanshi quanxia geng shen de buwei ， yiji sheji qita xingxing he weixing de taikong dizhixue （ Astrogeology ） 。\n\n dizhi shijian chidu hangai le zhengge diqiu lishi 。qi qidian kaishi yu zui zao de taiyangxi cailiao shengcheng shi ， yue zai 4. 567 Ga ， diqiu de chuxian yue zai 4. 54 Ga ， yikaishi chengwei ming guzhou ， zui nianqing de dizhi niandai ze shi quanxinshi 。\n \n \n ruguo ba diqiu dansheng dao xianzai de dayue 45yinian suoxiao dao 1 nian ， ze renlei （ \"Homo sapiens \" ） cunzai de shijian zhiyou ji duan de ban ge xiaoshi 。\n \n ba xiansheng zhou fangda ： \n\n dui diqiu de wuzhi chengfen de yanjiu zuizao zhishao keyi zhuisu dao guxi latai aofulasituosi de zhuzuo 《 lunyanshi 》 （ Peri Lithon ） 。zai guluoma shiqi ， lao pulinni xiangxi de miaoshu le changyong de yixie kuangwu he jinshu ， hai zhengque de jieshi le hupo de laiyuan 。\n \n yixie xiandai xuezhe （ ru ） renwei ， xiandai dizhixue kaishi yu zhongshiji yisilan shijie 。bi luni jiushi zui zao de zhiyi ， ta de zhuzuo you zui zao de xushu de wenzhang ， tichu le yindu ci dalu cengjing shi haiyang de jiashe 。yisilan xuezhe yiben·xina dui shanmai de xingcheng ， dizhen de yuanyin ， yiji qita yixie xiandai dilixue de lunti geichu le xiangxi de jieshi ， zhexie neirong wei rihou dizhixue de fazhan tigong le jichu 。zai zhongguo ， boxuejia shenkuo （ 1031 – 1095 ）tichu ludi xingcheng de jiashuo 。ta zai yige li haiyang jibai gongli yuan de shanzhong de kandao ， zai yige dizhi di cengli you beikelei shengwu huashi 。youci ta tuilun ， ludi shi you shanmai de qinshi he yuni de chenji suo xingcheng de 。\n \n henzaoyiqian ， dizhixue de zhishi bijiao lingxing fensan 。guanyu zhe fangmian de zhishi ， ru cong dizhong kaicai jinshu 、 niantu 、 meiheyan de yixie zhishi ， zaoyi wei kuanggong he youguan de renmen suo zhixiao ， er ziran zhexuejiamen ze dadu tuoli zhexie shijian ， duli xingcheng ziji de sibianxing de dizhi lilun 。\n\n dizhixue zai 18 shiji kaishi chengwei yi men duli de kexue ， bing zai 19 shiji zaoqi dadao chengshu jieduan 。\n \n 1790nian zhi 1830nian zhe yi duan shiqi bei chengwei “ dizhixue de yingxiong shidai ” 。zai zhege shiqi ， zai kaocha yanceng shunxu yiji yanceng suo han kuangwu he huashi shang ， renmen zuo le daliang gongzuo 。zai xianjieduan ， youyu guancha 、 yanjiu tiaojian de xianzhi ， zhuyao yi yanshiquan wei yanjiu duixiang ， bing sheji shuiquan 、 daqiquan 、 shengwuquan he yanshi quanxia geng shen de buwei ， yiji sheji qita xingxing he weixing de taikong dizhixue （ Astrogeology ） 。 \n 。gongzuo fangfa de yida jinbu biaoxian zai yong genju huashi neirong lai jinxing yanceng fenlei 。\n\n dizhi xueshi shang you san chang zhuming de zhenglun 。\n \nqiyi wei shuichenglun yu huochenglun zhi zheng ， fasheng zai 18shiji mo 。zhenglun de jiaodian zaiyu yanshi de xingcheng lilun ， yifang yi deguo kexuejia yabolahan·geteluobu·weierna （ Abraham G . Werner ） wei daibiao ， qiangdiao xingcheng yanshi guocheng zhong de shui de zuoyong ； ling yifang yi sugelan kexuejia hetun （ James Hutton ） wei daibiao ， qiangdiao huo de zuoyong 。xianjin yijing zhidao ， yanshi zhuyao you sanda lei goucheng ， chule shuicheng weizhu de chenjiyan he huocheng weizhu de yanjiangyan ， hai cunzai yilei bianzhi yan 。shuicheng guocheng he huocheng guocheng zai yanshi de xingcheng zhongdu banyan le zhongyao juese 。\n \nqier wei zai bianlun yu jian bianlun （ ye chengjun bianlun ） zhi zheng ， fasheng zai 19 shiji zaoqi 。chizai bianlun guandian de xuezhe renwei ， diqiu lishi shang ceng fasheng guo duoci da de zainan ， shi zainan daozhi le jiu de wuzhong de miejue he xin wuzhong de zai chuangzao 。chijian bianlun guandian de xuezhe renwei ， wuzhong yanhua de dongli laiziyu weiruo de dizhi zuoyong zai diqiu yanbian guocheng zhong de changqi jilei ， bu yikao daxing de zainan ye nenggou fasheng 。\n \n disan chang zhenglun shi gudinglun yu huodong lun zhi zheng 。guding lunxue shuo renwei diqiao de weizhi shi yongyuan bu bian de ， qi yundong fangshi yi chuizhi yundong weizhu 。chuantong de dicao 、 di taixue shuo jiushi yi zhong guding lunxue shuo 。huodong lunxue shuo renwei diqiao de yundong shi yi shuiping yundong weizhu de ， chuizhi yundong suiran cunzai ， danshi shi shuiping yundong guocheng zhong paisheng chulai de （ biru liang dikuai shuiping ji yachu diqiao xiangshang longqi ） 。huodong lun suizhe bankuai gouzaoxue shuo de fazhan ， zhujian bei xuezhe suo rentong 。\n \n \n 
 qixiangxue \n \n qixiangxue shi ba daqi dangzuo yanjiu de keti ， cong dingxing he dingliang liang fangmian lai shuoming daqi tezheng de xueke ， jizhong yanjiu daqi de tianqi qingkuang he bianhua guilv he dui tianqi de yubao 。qixiangxue shi daqi kexue de yige fenzhi 。\n \n diyi wei jianli qixiangxue de ren shi gu xila zhexuejia yalishiduode 。zai ta de zhuanshu 《 qixiang huilun 》 zhong ， ta zuixian xushu he cuqian di jieshi le feng 、 yun 、 yu 、 xue 、 lei 、 bao deng tianqi xianxiang ， er zhe shu shi shijie shang zui zao de qixiang shuji 。zhidao 18 - 19 shiji ， youyu wulixue he huaxue de fazhan yiji qiya 、 wendu 、 shidu he fengdeng celiang yiqi de luxu faming ， shi daqi kexue yanjiu you danchun de miaoshu jinru le keyi dingliang fenxi de jieduan 。1820nian ， deguoren budelan huizhi le diyi zhang dimian tianqi tu ， kaichuang le jindai tianqi fenxi he yubao fangfa 。1835nian ， faguoren keli aoli tichu feng pianzhuan de gainian ； er 1857nian helanren baibeiluo tichu feng he qiya de guanxi ， tamen de gainian dou chengwei daqi donglixue he tianqi fenxi de jichu 。1854nian 11yue 14ri kelimiya zhanzheng qijian ， yi chang baoyu shi hengli si shi de junjian ji shangchuan huihuaidaijin ， zaocheng 400 ren siwang ， dangshi de guofang buzhang wayang （ ） qing tianwenxuejia - {yu }-erban·leiweiye fuze zhaochu yuanwei 。jingguo yanjiu hou ， - {yu } - erban zhengming zhe chang baofengyu zai 11yue 12ri ji yi cunzai ， qie zai liang tian zhinei bianzi xibei wang dongnan fangxiang xijuan zhengge ouzhou 。yinci ta zhichu yingxiang tianqi de dabufen yinzi dou juyou qianyixing 。cici shijian shi ta renwei you biyao fazhan qixiangxue ， ta cushi zhe men xueke zai 1855nian huode zhengshi diwei ， xiandai qixiangxue jiuci tachu diyi bu 。\n \n 19 20nian qianhou ， nuowei de piyekenisi fuzi tichu le yi tao ming wei 「 jifengxue shuo 」 de lilun ， lai shuoming zhongweidu diqu de tianqi bianhua qingkuang 。zhe tao lilun zai 1920niandai fabiao zhihou ， zhijin yi you 70duo nian ， dan rengran shi jinri zuo tianqi yubao de zhuyao lilun yiju ， yi wei fenxi he yubao weilai 1-2 tian de tianqi dianding le lilun jichu 。1930niandai ， wuxian diantan kongyi de guangfan shiyong ， zhenzheng kaishi le sanwei kongjian de daqi kexue yanjiu 。genju daliang tankong ziliao huizhi de gaokong tianqi tu ， faxian le daqichangbo 。1939nian kaer-gusitafu·luosibei tichu le zhang bodonglixue ， ta de lilun yi dui tianqi yubao you moda de gongxian 。dao le 1950niandai zhi 60niandai ， diannao 、 tianqi leida ， weixing he yaogan de jishu de yingyong ， shi daqi de gezhong xianxiang ， da zhi daqi huanliu ， xiao zhi yudi de xingcheng guocheng ， dou ke yizhao wulixue he huaxue de shuxue xingshi lai biaoshi ， liru relixue diyi dinglv 、 pian weifen 。conger shi daqi kexue you le tufeimengjin de fazhan 。\n \n yanjiu de fangfa zhuyao you si zhong ， fenbie wei guance yanjiu 、 lilun yanjiu 、 shuzhi moshi yanjiu ji shiyan yanjiu ： \n\n guance yanjiu shi jiguan cequ liaojie butong de daqi xianxiang ， keyi shuo shi qixiangxue lilun de qizhong yikuai jishi ， yi shi yiban qixiang aihaozhe suo guanzhu de 。guance fangfa yi you henduo zhong ， qixiangzhan 、 gaokong qiqiu 、 weixing yuntu 、 leida hui botu deng 。guance yanjiu buzhi shi guance ， ye you yiding chengdu de guina he fenxi ， liru yi ju 「 mingtian zhuanleng 」 ， bian shi yi zhong fenxi 。ciwai ， huizhi tianqitu 、 zhengli redai qixuan lujing 、 qihou quyu fenlei deng ， yi shi guance yanjiusuo yao zuo de 。\n \n lilun yanjiu you sanda bufen ， chuguan cewai ， wuli he shuxue dui lilun yanjiu yi hen zhongyao 。lilun keyi cong liang fangmian chansheng ， yifangmian shi cong guance shuju zhong zhijie jianli chulai de ， liru fenxi redai qixuan qiangdu de dewozhake fenxifa ， lingyifangmian shi cong wuli lilun huo qita qixiang lilun yanhua chulai de ， liru dizhuan fangcheng 、 qiya tidu fangcheng deng 。wuli lilun henduo shi xuyao shuxue de bangzhu ， fanguolaishuo ， shuxue yuyan youshi geng neng shi women mingbai wuli he qixiang lilun 。\n \n xiandai de tianqi yubao ji shi jianli zai shuzhi moshi shang ， shuzhi moshi touguo feixianxing fangchengshi yiji chaoji diannao de cha diange yunsuan ， fan yanchu yi diqu weilai shu tian tianqi 。shuzhi moshi yanjiu shi jiao shao ren suo renshi de ， tamen dou xuyao xiangdang de lilun zhishi 、 diannao chengxu jiqiao he shiyan jiqiao 。shuzhi moshi yanjiuhui ba butong de wuli he qixiang fangcheng ， yi diannao chengxu de fangshi fangjin diannao li ， zai jisuan chu weilai wendu 、 shidu 、 qiya 、 fengxiang deng bianhua ， yi xiezhu tianqi yubao huo lilun yanjiu 。\n \n bijiao youming de tianqi shuzhi moshi you ： \n\n shiyan yanjiu  shengwuxue \n \n shengwuxue （ ；； deyu ： ； fayu ： ； ） huo cheng shengwu kexue （ ） 、 shengming kexue （ ） ， shi ziran kexue de yida menlei ， you jingyanzhuyi chufa ， guangfan yanjiu shengming de suoyou fangmian ， baokuo shengming qiyuan 、 yanhua 、 fenbu 、 gouzao 、 fayu 、 gongneng 、 xingwei 、 yu huanjing de hudong guanxi ， yiji shengwu fenleixue deng 。xiandai shengwuxue shi yige pangda er jianshoubingxu de lingyu ， you xuduo fenzhi he fenzhi xueke zucheng 。raner ， jinguan shengwuxue de fanwei hen guang ， zai ta limian you mouxie yiban he tongyi gainian zhipei yiqie de xuexi he yanjiu ， ba ta zhenghe cheng danyi de ， he lianguan de lingyu 。zai zongti shang ， shengwu yi xibao zuowei shengming de jiben danwei ， jiyin zuowei yichuan de jiben danyuan ， he jinhua shi tuidong xin wuzhong de hecheng he chuangjian de yinqing 。jintian renmen hai liaojie ， suoyou shengwuti de shengcun yi xiaohao he zhuanhuan nengliang ， tiaojie tinei huanjing yi weichi wending de he zhongyao de shengming tiaojian 。\n \n shengwu xuefen zhixue ke bei yanjiusheng wuti de guimo suo dingyi ， he yanjiu tamen shiyong de fangfa suo dingyi ： shengwu huaxue kaocha shengming de jiben huaxue ； fenzishengwuxue yanjiu shengwu fenzi zhijian cuozong fuza de guanxi ； zhiwuxue yanjiu zhiwu de shengwuxue ； xibao shengwuxue jiancha suoyou shengming de jiben zucheng danwei , xibao ； shenglixue jiancha zuzhi ， qiguan ， he shengwuti de qiguan xitong de wuli he huaxue de gongneng ； jinhua shengwuxue kaocha le shengming de duoyangxing de chansheng guocheng ； he shengtaixue kaocha shengwu zai qi huanjing ruhe xianghu zuoyong 。zuizhong nenggou dadao zhiliao zhenduan yichuanbing 、 tigao nongzuowu chanliang 、 gaishan renlei shenghuo 、 baohu huanjing deng mudi 。\n \n shengwuxue zhi yingyu danci 「 」 ( deyu 、 fayu 「 Biologie 」 )yuanyu xilawen ，， yiwei shengming ， yiji ziwei ， \" - logia \" ， yiwei xuewen ， hebing wei “ yanjiu shengming de xuewen ” 。1802nian ， faguo bowuxuejia lamake zuizao tichu zhege mingci 。\n \n xiandai shengwuxue de wuda jichu ， ye shi zhuyao de yanjiu fangxiang ：\n\n xibaoxue shuo renwei xibao shi shengwu de jiben danwei ， erqie suoyou shengwu dou shi you yi zhiduo ge xibao yiji xibao fenmi de wuzhi zucheng （ liru waiguge ） 。suoyou xibao dou shi you qita xibao jieyou xibao fenlie de fangshi chansheng 。duo xibao shengwu yikaishi shi cong yige shoujingluan de danyi xibao kaishi ， zai jianjian fenlie wei gege xibao ， er xibao ye shi xuduo de jiben danwei . 。ciwai ， xibao zhijian nengliang zhuanyi de xianxiang chengwei daixie ， er xibao baohan de yichuan zixun （ DNA ） ， zai xibao fenlie shi ye hui chuandi gei qita de xibao 。\n \n xiandai shengwuxue renwei shengming shi cong yanhua er lai ， suoyou yizhi de shengwu dou you yi gongtong qiyuan 。yanhualun jiashe suoyou diqiu shang huozhu ji yi juezhong de shengwu dou shi laizi yi gongtong qiyuan huo yiji yinku 。suoyou shengwu zui wan de gongtong qiyuan yue chuxian zai yue 35yi nianqian 。\n \n muqian yi you yadaoxing de zhengju zhichi yanhua de zhenshixing ， xuejie pubian renwei yanhua shi shishi ， er bujinjin shi lilun huo jiashuo ， duiyu yanhualun de zhenquexing ， cunzai you qianglie de kexue gongshi ， yanhua yiwai renhe guanyu wuzhong qiyuan huo renlei qiyuan de xueshuo ， muqian dou bu huo zhichi 。juedaduoshu de kexue shequn he xueshu tuanti ， dou renwei yanhua lunshi weiyi neng wanquan manzu zai shengwuxue 、 gushengwuxue 、 fenzishengwuxue 、 yichuanxue 、 renleixue ji qita ge lingyu zhong suo guancha dao de xianxiang de lilun 。yi xiang zai 1991nian suo zuo de gailuopu mindiao xianshi ， zhiyou dayue 5% de kexuejia （ baokuo shengwuxue lingyu yiwai de qita kexuejia ） renwei ziji shi chuangzao lunzhe 。jiezhi muqian weizhi ， meiyou renhe fandui yanhua lunqie jingguo kexue fangmian tonghang shencha de lunwen ， minglie kexue yu yixue qikan souxun yinqing PubMed dangzhong 。\n \n jiyin shi shengwuti yichuan de jiben danwei ， jiyin duiying yi teding quyu de DNA ， yi teding fangshi yingxiang shengwu de mou yi buwei huo mou yi jineng 。cong xijun dao dongwu de suoyou shengwuti dou you tongyang fuzhi DNA ， bing yici chansheng danbaizhi de nengli 。xibao jiang DNA de jiyin zhuanlu wei duiying de hetanghesuan （ RNA ） ， ranhou he tangti jiang R N A zhuanyi wei yi chuan you an jisuan zucheng de danbaizhi 。you R N A zhuanhuan wei an jisuan de yichuan mima zai dabufen shengwu zhong shi xiangtong de ， dan youxie shengwu reng you shaoxu chayi 。liru ruo jiang renlei dui yingyi daosu de DNA fangzai zhiwu zhong ， ye keyi chansheng yidaosu 。\n \n tinei pingheng () ： pingheng shi yige kaifang xitong keyi jieyou xuduo bici xiangguan jizhi de dongtai pingheng tiaozheng ， shide qi neizai qingxing weichi zai wending de zhuangtai 。suoyou de shengwu ， bulun shi dan xibao huoshi duo xibao shengwu ， dou you tinei pingheng de jizhi 。\n \n yige huo de shengwuti de shengcun yilaiyu nengliang de lianxu shuru 。shengwuti shi kao huaxue fanying lai cong shiwu zhong tiqu nengliang ， caineng weichi shenti jineng ， bing jianli xin de xibao 。zai shangshu fanying zhong ， zucheng shiwu huaxue wuzhi de fenzi banyan liang ge zhongyao juese 。diyi ， zhexie fenzi zhong youxie keyi jieyou shengwu tinei de huaxue fanying chansheng nengliang 。dier ， youxie ze keyi zucheng shengwu fenzi zhong de xin de fenzijiegou 。\n \n fuze yinjin nengliang dao shengtai xitong de shengwu bei chengwei shengchanzhe huo ziyang shengwu 。jihu suoyou de zhexie shengwuti zuichu dou cong taiyang xiqu nengliang 。\n \n shengwuxuejia cong henduo mianxiang yanjiu shengwu ， yinci chansheng henduo yanjiu lingyu 。liru ： \n\n shengwuxue benshen buduan de kuaisu fazhan ， yu qita xueke de guanlian zhenghe ye yuelaiyue duo 。yida yuanyin shi fenzishengwuxue zai jindai tufeimengjin ， zhongyu daozhi renlei jiyin xulie dingxu jiben wancheng 。youci ， weile jiedu juda shuliang de jiyin zixun ， cucheng le jiyin zuxue 。weile tanjiu jiyin he danbaizhi de jiaohu zuoyong ， kaichuang chu danbaizhi zuxue 。zhexie xin de yanjiu lingyu bangzhu jiejue jibing 、 liangshi 、 huanjing shengtai deng wenti 。qi zhongduo de yanjiu zixun he jilei hailiang yanjiu shuju ze xuyao xin de diannao yansuanfa lai chuli 。\n \n fenzishengwuxue shi zai fenzi shuiping de shengwuxue yanjiu 。gai lingyu yu shengwuxue de qita lingyu chongdie ， tebieshi yichuanxue he shengwu huaxue 。fenzishengwuxue zhuyao guanzhu de shi lijie yige xibao nei de gezhong xitong de xianghu zhijian de xianghu zuoyong ， baokuo DNA ， RNA he danbaizhi de hecheng he xuexi zhexie xianghu zuoyong ruhe bei tiaojie 。\n \n xibao shengwuxue yanjiu xibao de jiegou he shenglixue texing ， baokuo tamen de xingwei ， xianghu zuoyong he huanjing 。\n \n jiepouxue kaolv de shi hongguan jiegou de xingshi ， liru qiguan he qiguan xitong 。\n \n yichuanxue shi yanjiu jiyin 、 yichuan he shengwuti de bianyi de kexue 。\n \n \n tamen shi yu （ regio ） 、 jie （ regnum ） 、 men （ divisio huo phylum ） 、 gang （ classis ） 、 mu（ordo ） 、 ke（familia ） 、 shu （ genus ） 、 zhong （ species ） 。\n \n \n shuang mingfa shi xueming de mingming fangfa ， yingwen wei Binomial Nomenclature 。ta gei meige wuzhong dingli liang ge wenzi ， qianzi shi gai wuzhong de shu （ genus ） ming ， houzi shi ta de zhong xiaoming ( zhong jiaci ) ， liangzhe hewei zhongming 。chule qian zixu shou zimu daxie ， qiyu zimu dou yao xiaoxie 。yiban shiyong ladingwen ， huo yi qita yuyan cizuo yuyuan ， zai jiashang ladinghua houzhui 。liru zhongguo jinlai faxian de konglong ， youxie xueming shi yong zhongwen pinyin zuo yuyuan de 。\n \n youxie wuzhong yinwei huanjing gejue huo fasheng tubian ， bixu zai wangxia xi fenchu yazhong （ subspecies ） 。weile fangbian qubie ， kexuejie gei yazhong sheji yi tao san mingfa ， yingwen wei Trinomial Nomenclature 。\n \n shengtaixue yanjiu shengwu yuqi huanjing zhijian de xianghu guanxi de kexue 。huanjing baokuo shengwu huanjing he feishengwu huanjing ， shengwu huanjing shi zhi shengwu wuzhong zhijian he wuzhong neibu ge geti zhijian de guanxi ， feishengwu huanjing baokuo ziran huanjing ： turang 、 yanshi 、 shui 、 kongqi 、 wendu 、 shidu deng 。\n \n shengwuxuejia duiyu shengming xianxiang de yanjiu tongchang caiyong guancha he shiyan de fangfa ， tongchang zhe liang zhong fangfa shi yiqi shiyong de 。\n shiyan fangfa shi renwei di ganyu 、 kongzhi suo yanjiu de duixiang ， bing tongguo zhezhong ganyu he kongzhi suo zaocheng de xiaoying lai yanjiu duixiang de mouzhong shuxing 。17 shiji qianhou shengwuxue zhong chuxian le zui zao de yipi shengwuxue shiyan ， ru yingguo shenglixuejia weilian·hawei guanyu xueye xunhuan de shiyan ， yang·bapudisita·fan·haier mengte guanyu liushu shengzhang de shiyan deng 。dao le 19shiji ， wulixue 、 huaxue bijiao chengshu le ， shengwuxue shiyan jiu you le jianshi de jichu ， yiner shouxian shi shenglixue ， ranhou shi xijunxue he shengwu huaxue xiangji chengwei mingque de shiyanxing de xueke 。19 shiji 80niandai ， shiyan fangfa jinyibu bei yingyong dao le peitaixue ， xibaoxue he yichuanxue deng xueke 。\n \n jinguan women jin jishi nian lai duiyu shengming de de jiben guocheng de renshi qude le de shenke jinbu ， yixie jiben de wenti rengran meiyou dedao jiejue 。liru ， zai shengwuxue de zhuyao wei jiejue de wenti zhiyi shi xingbie de zhuyao zi shiying gongneng ， he tebieshi zai zhenhe shengwu zhong ta de guanjian guocheng ， jianshu fenlie he tongyuan chongzu 。yi zhong guandian renwei ， xingbie zhuyao shi fazhan chengwei yige shiying zengjia yichuan duoyangxing （ qing canyue cankao ziliaoru ） 。ling yi zhong guandian renwei ， xingbie shi yi zhong shiyingyu shengzhi xibaoxi DNA cujin zhunque de DNA xiufu ， bingqie zengjia yichuan duoyangxing zhuyao shi keneng shi cong changyuan laikan shi youyong de yige fuchanpin 。（ canjian you xingshengzhi de yanhua ） 。\n \n zai shengwuxue ling yige jiben wei jiejue de wenti shi laohua de shengwuxue jichu 。muqian ， meiyou renhe shuailao de genben yuanyin gongshi 。gezhong jingzheng de lilunlie zai laohua # shuailao lilun 。\n \n zhexie shi shengwuxue de zhuyao  xinlixue \n \n - {H | zh - hant : xinli xue; zh - hans : xinli xue ;} - \n \n xinlixue （ yingwen : psychology ） shi yi men yanjiu renlei yiji qita dongwu de neizai xinli licheng 、 jingshen gongneng he waizai xingwei de kexue ， ji shi yi men lilun xueke ， ye shi yi men yingyong xueke 。baokuo lilun xinlixue yu yingyong xinlixue liang da lingyu 。\n \n xinlixue yanjiu sheji yishi 、 ganjue 、 zhijue 、 renzhi 、 dongji 、 qingxu 、 renge 、 xingwei he renji guanxi deng zhongduo lingyu ， yingxiang qita xueke de fazhan ， liru ： jiaoyuxue 、 guanlixue 、 chuanboxue 、 shehuixue 、 jingjixue 、 jingshenbingxue 、 tongjixue 、 jisuanji kexue yiji wenxue dengdeng 。xinlixue yifangmian changshi yong danao yunzuo lai jieshi geti jiben de xingwei yu xinli jineng ， tongshi ， xinlixue ye changshi jieshi geti xinliji neng zai shehui xingwei yu shehui dongli zhong de juese 。xinlixuejia congshi jichu yanjiu de mudi shi miaoshu 、 jieshi 、 yuce he kongzhi xingwei 。yingyong xinlixuejia haiyou diwu ge mudi —— tigao renlei shenghuo de zhiliang 。zhexie mubiao goucheng le xinlixue shiye de jichu 。\n \n zai guxilayu zhong ， xinlixue you 「 linghun 」 （ ） he 「 yanjiu 」 （ ） suo zucheng 。\n \n 「 xinlixue 」 hanyi yiming zhi laiyuan ， touguo lishixue yu xinlixue zhi xiangguan kaozheng ， chubu zhengming yu zhongguo mingdai xinxue 、 song dailixue 、 ji songming ruxue dongdu riben you zhijie guanxi 。\n \n zaoqi de xinlixue yanjiu shi shuyu zhexue de fanchou ， chengwei zhexue xinlixue 。zhexue xinlixue de yanjiu keyi zhuisu dao aiji 、 xila 、 yindu he huaxia deng gudai wenming 。zhongguo gudai renwei ren de xingqing sixiang shi you yiding de qiguan chengdan de ， bingqie qi huodong hui zai qiguan shang fanying chulai ， ru 「 xinzhiguanzesi 」 （ 《 mengzi 》 ） ， 「 ren jing zai nao 」 、 「 touzhe shenzhisuoju 」 （ 《 chun qiuyuan mingbao 》 ） 。「 shenxingheyi 」 、 「 xingshen xiangyin 」 deng sixiang zai 《 huangdineijing 》 deng sheji yixue xinli de zhuzuo zhong you henduo chanshu he yingyong 。bolatu tichu guo eryuan bingcun de linian ， youren renwei yalisiduode 《 lun linghun 》 shi xifang zui zao de yi bu lunshu xinlixue sixiang de zhuzuo 。jingyou changjiu de yanbian ， manman de chansheng geshigeyang butong de xueke ， baokuo le xianzai ren suo liaojie de xinlixue 。\n \n zhexue xinlixue zhuyao shi zai tantao xinshen guanxi 、 tianxing yu jiaoyang 、 ziyou yizhi yu juedinglun 、 zhishi laiyuan deng si da yiti 。qi zaoqi de lilun you yiyuanlun 、 eryuanlun 、 huanjing juedinglun 、 jingshen jueding lundeng 。jindai de zhexue xinlixue ze shi you sanda sixiang liupai ， baokuo le lixingzhuyi 、 jingyanzhuyi yu langmanzhuyi 。zhengru deguo xinlixuejia aibinhaosi suo shuo ： “ xinlixue you yige manchang de guoqu ， que zhiyou yige duanzan de lishi ” 。\n zai zhongshiji de yisilan yixue yu xinlixue zhong ， yijing kaishi jinxing linchuang de jingshenke zhiliao he shiyan yanjiu 。\n \n suiran xinlixue shiyan keyi zhuisu dao alabo xuezhe haishenmu de zhuzuo 《 guangxue 》 （ 1021nian ）buguo ， xinlixue zuowei yi men duli de xueke shi kaishi yu 1874nian ， na yi nian ， deguo de shenglixuejia weilian·fengte fabiao liang ce de xinlixue jiaokeshu —— 《 shengli xinlixue de yuanli 》 （ Principles of Physiological Psychology ） —— ， zai xuyan li dadan xuancheng ： 「 yao jianli yige xin de kexue lingyu 」 ； fengte ye yinci bei chengwei “ xinlixue zhi fu ” 。1875nian ， laibixi daxue pinfeng tewei jiaoshou ；1879nian ， ta zai laibixi daxue jianli shijie diyi ge zhuanmen de xinli shiyanshi ， xiyin le laizi shijie gedi de xuesheng 。10yu nianhou ， ye jiushi 1890niandai ， meiguo ge daxue fengqiyunyong di fangxiao ciju ， jianli shushi zuo xinlixue shiyanshi ， youqi 1892 zhe yi nian jiu chengli le 20 zuo ， zhe yi nian ye shi meiguo xinlixuehui de chengli nian 。tongchang jiang 1874nian zuowei kexue xinlixue dansheng de shijian ， zhe yishijian bi xuduo ziran kexue tuoli zhexue er xingcheng duli xueke de shijian wei wan 。fengte ye shi diyi geba ziji chengwei xinlixuejia de ren 。qita zaoqi er zhongyao de xinlixuejia baokuo aibinhaosi deng 。19shijimo 、 20 shiji chu ， xigemengde·fuluoyide de jingshen fenxi xuepai xingqi 。\n \n deguo xinlixuejia weilian·fengte bei renwei shi jiang shiyan yinru xinlixue yanjiu de ren ， bei yuwei “ shiyan xinlixue zhi fu ” 。1879nian ， ta zai laibixi daxue jianli le diyi ge xinlixue shiyanshi 。fengte zhe zhongyu jiang xinli fenjie chengwei jiben de yuansu ， zheshi youyu dangshi huaxue de jinbu ， houzhe zai fenxi wuzhi yuansu yu jiegou shang qude tupo 。suiran fengte ziji bushi gouzaozhuyizhe ， ta de xuesheng aidehua·B·tieqinna chengwei le gouzaozhuyi de sixiangjia ， yu jinengzhuyizhe duili 。tieqinna shi meiguo zaoqi xinlixuejia de zhongyao renwu 。\n \n jinengzhuyi xiangduiyu jiegouzhuyi ersheng ， bing shoudao meiguo zhexuejia 、 kexuejia 、 xinlixuejia weilian·zhanmushi yingxiang po duo 。zhanmushi renwei xinlixue yinggai you shiyong jiazhi ， xinlixuejia yinggai zhaodao youyiyu ren de kexue fangshi 。ta de zhuzuo zhong yu 1890nian chuban ， qizhong you xuduo pudianxing wenti ， wei houxu kexuejia tigong le fangxiang 。qita zhuyao jinengzhuyizhe baokuo yuehan·duwei he 。\n \n qita 19 shiji de jiechu renwu you deguo xinlixuejia heerman·aibinhaosi ， ta shi yanjiu jiyi shiyan de xianqu ， zai bolin hongbao daxue chuangli le xuexi yu yiwang de lianghua moxing 。sue xinlixuejia yiwan·bideluoweiqi·bafuluofu ， ta zai dui gou jinxing shiyan shi faxian le “ gudian zhiyue ” ， bing jiang qi yingyong yu renlei 。zi ershishiji 50niandai qi ， fengte 、 zhanmushi 、 aibinhaosi yu qita shiyan xinlixuejiamen suo fazhan de shiyan jishu fangxiang gengjia quxiang yanjiu renzhi —— guanzhu xinxi yiji xinxi chuli —— zuizhong yanhua wei renzhi kexue zhong de yibufen 。zai zaoxieshihou ， zhe bei shiwei “ gemingxing ” de fazhan ， yinwei renzhi kexue huifu bing duiying zhiqian de liuxing lilun ， baokuo jingshen fenxi he xingweizhuyi lilun deng 。\n \n aodili yisheng xigemengde·fuluoyide zi shijiushiji 90niandai kaishi yanjiu jingshen fenxixue ， zhidao ziji 1939nian qushi weizhi 。jingshen fenxixue shi yi zhong yanjiu yishi 、 jieshi jingli de fangfa ； shi yi zhong guanyu renlei xingwei de lilun xitong ； shi yi zhong zhendui xinli 、 qingxu de zhiliao fangfa ， tebieshi dui qianyishi zhong de chongtu jinxing xinli zhiliao 。fuluoyide de jingshen fenxi zhong de henduo lilun jiyu jieshifa 、 neixingfa yiji linchuang guancha 。jingshen fenxi faguang wei liuchuan ， yinwei ta de yanjiu duixiang sheji xingbie 、 yayi 、 xinli fazhan zhong de qianyishi deng 。zhexie wenti zai dangshi dou bei liewei shehui jinji ， fuluoyide ze tigong le cuihuaji ， shide wenti keyi zai zhengshi shejiao zhong deyi gongkai taolun 。zai linchuang shang ， fuluoyide shi ziyou lianxiang de xianqu ， ta dui shimeng zhiliao ye hen you yanjiu 。\n \n fuluoyide dui ruishi jingshenke yishi kaer·rongge de yingxiang hen da ， houzhe de fenxi xinlixue yu shendu xinlixue hubu 。20 shiji zhongye xinli xuezhemen yanjiu jingshen fenxi 、 xinlixue 、 jingshenbing zhiliao 、 yiji zhexue 。zhexie zhuming de xuezhe baokuo ailike·ailikesen 、 meilanni·kelaiyin 、 tangnade·weinikete 、 kalun·huoni 、 ailixi·fuluomu 、 yuehan·baobi 、 yiji fuluoyide de nver anna·fuluoyide 。zai zhengge ershi shiji li ， jingshen fenxi yansheng chu butong de fenzhi xuepai ， tamen zhong henduo bei huafen wei xinfuluoyidexuepai 。\n \n jingshen fenxi jiqi zhiliao shoudao zhuduo renshi de piping ， ru xinlixuejia hansi·aisenke 、 yiji zhexuejia kaer·bopuer 。bopuer shi wei kexue zhexuejia ， renwei jingshen fenxi zuowei kexue shi cuowu de ，， er aisenke ze cheng jingshen fenxi yuanli yu shiyan shuju bufu 。dao ershishiji mo ， meiguo gaodeng yuanxiao xinli xueyuan biande gengjia qingxiangyu shizhengzhuyi ， jiang fuluoyide lilun bianyuanhua ， bing miecheng qi wei “ ganbie laosi ” de lishi gudong 。yucitongshi ， yanjiu renyuan zai shenjing jingshen fenxi lingyu shang weihu fuluoyide de kexue lichang ， er qita ren wenxue kexuezhemen ze gushou fuluoyide “ genben bushi kexuejia ， ershi ge ... quanshizhe 。 ”\n\n zai zhengge 20 shiji de shangbanye ， xingweizhuyi xuepai zhipei le dangshi de xinlixue ， qi zhuzhang xinlixue shi ： “ xunqiu lijie teding de huanjing ciji ruhe kongzhi teding leixing de xingwei ” 。qi zhuzhang xinlixue ying fenxi xianxing de huanjing tiaojian ， ji zai xingwei zhiqian chuxian 、 erqie wei yige jiti chansheng fanying huo yizhi fanying tigong huodong changsuo de tiaojian 。yinci ， tamen ba xingwei fanying kanzuo shi jiti lijie 、 yuce he kongzhi de xingwei ， bing yinci zuochu xiangying de jieguo 。jiyu dui shiyan he bianliang de yange kongzhi he qiangdiao ， xingweizhuyi xue dui houlai de xinlixue yanjiu youzhe zhongyao de yingxiang 。qi daibiao renwu wei shijinna ， raner qi duiyu neizai de renzhi licheng shi cunerbulun ， jinqi liuxing de renzhizhuyi ze shi zhongshi zhiqian hushi de neizai renzhi licheng ， daibiao renwu you piyajie 、 milei 、 ximeng deng 。\n \n dangjin shijie zhuyao de xinlixue xuepai you wuda guandian ， mei yige guandian dou qiangdiao xingwei ji xinli guocheng de butong fangmian 。qi zhuyao baokuo shenjing xinlixue 、 jingshen fenxixue 、 xingweizhuyi xinlixue 、 renbenzhuyi xinlixue 、 renzhi xinlixue 。\n \n ershi shiji 50niandai ， zai xingweizhuyi yu jingshen fenxi de yingxiang xia ， renben xinlixue yingyuersheng 。yingyong xianxiangxue 、 、 diyi rencheng shijiao ， renbenzhuyi shitu buzhuo zhengge ren —— er bushi renge huo renzhi de yibufen 。renbenzhuyi xinlixue guanzhu renlei dute wenti de jichu ， liru geren de ziyou yizhi 、 chengzhang 、 ziwo shixian 、 rentong 、 siwang 、 gudu 、 ziyou yu 。renben guocheng de tedian zaiyu ta guanzhu zhuguan yixiang 、 jujue suming 、 zhuozhong chengzhang de jijixing er bushi bingli yinsu 。yixie ren benxuepai de dianjiren ， ru meiguo xinlixuejia yabolahan·masiluo ， chuangli le xuqiu cengci lilun ； kaer·luozhesi ， chuangli le geren zhongxin zhiliao 。zai ci zhihou ， zhengmian xinlixue pouxi le renbenzhuyi ， dui qi gengjinyibu de kexue fenxi 。\n \nwoerfugang·kelei 、 makesi·weitemo 、 kete·kaofuka san ren lianhe chuangli le wanxing xinlixuepai 。zhezhongxinli yanjiu jianli zai geren jingli wei yi zhengti de guandian shang 。duiying wuzhi de fenzijiegou ， zhezhong guandian yu shijiu shiji wanqi zai deguo 、 aodili chansheng 。wanxing xinlixue meiyou jiang siwei 、 xingwei fenjie chengwei xixiao de yuansu ， ershi jianchi jingyan zuowei zhengti de zhongyaoxing ， renwei zongti butongyu bufen xiangjia de he 。\n wanxing xinlixue bu ying yu de xianghun xiao ， houzhe zhi zai waibiao shang yu wanxing xinlixue you guanlian 。\n \n zai ershishiji 50 dao 60niandai ， meiguo yuan jingshen fenxixuejia luoluo·mei zai deguo zhexuejia mading·haidegeer 、 danmai zhexuejia suolun·aobei·keerkaiguoer de yingxiang xia ， zoushang le xinlixue cunzai zhuyi zhi lu 。zhe baokuo cunzai xinli zhiliao 。\n \n cunzai zhuyi xinlixue butongyu qita renben xuepai ， ji renxing zhongli shijiao 、 dui jiaolv de jiji guandian deng 。cunzai zhuyi xinli xuezhu zhongyu renwen zhuti ， ru siwang 、 ziyou yizhi 、 yiyi ， bing renwei yiyi keyi bei shenhua 、 huoshi jiangshu fangshi gaibian 。duiyu siwang ji weilai de zhenshixing ， tongchang hui guli renmen jieshou ziyou yizhi ， jinguan ling ren jiaolv 。\n \n aodili cunzai zhuyi jingshenbing yisheng 、 datusha xingcunzhe weikeduo·fulanke cong jizhong yingzhong xiqu jiaoxun ， zong jiechu butong banben de cunzai zhuyi zhiliaofa ， zhezhong fangfa zhe zhongyu cunzai zhuyi ， butongyu adelei de nicaizhuyi de quanli yizhi huo fuluoyide de kuaile yuanze 。\n \n ruishi jingshen fenxixuejia ludeweige·binsiwange （ Ludwig Binswanger ） ， meiguo xinlixuejia qiaozhi·kaili （ George Kelly ） he mei （ May ） 、 fulankeer （ Frankl ） yidao ， ye bei renwei shi cunzai zhuyi xuepai xuezhe 。\n \n renzhizhuyi xinli xuepai yanjiu xinli huodong ， baokuo jiejue wenti 、 zhijue 、 jiyi 、 xuexi deng 。zuowei renzhi kexue de yibufen ， zhege xinli xuefen zhi yu qita xueke you miqie lianxi ， baokuo shenjing kexue 、 zhexue 、 yuyanxue deng 。\n \n nuomu·qiaomusiji zai piping xingwei xuegai nian zhong de “ ciji ” 、 “ xiangying ” 、 “ qianghua ” shi ， chufa le yi chang xinlixue “ renzhi geming ” 。qiaomusiji biancheng zhezhong guandian hui yi yi zhong fuqian 、 mohu de fangshi yingyong dao fuza de renlei xingwei zhong ， tebieshi zai yuyan xide de lingyu shang 。you yi zhong jiading renwei renlei tiansheng yongyou yi zhong “ neizai de ” yuyan xi de jineng ， raner duiyu xingweizhuyi laishuo ， zhege wenti zaiyu suoyou xingwei ， baokuo yuyan zainei ， dou bixu tongguo xuexi he qianghua lai huode 。shehui xuexi lilunjia ， ru aerbote·bandula cheng ertong de shenghuo huanjing youzhuyu xingwei de gailiang 。\n \n yucitongshi ， jishu jinbu bangzhu renmen zhongshi bei xingweizhuyi paoqi de xinli huodong yu biaoshu ， ru renzhi deng 。yingguo shenjing kexuejia chaersi·sikete·xielingdun jueshi yu jianada xinlixuejia tangnade·hebu yingyong shiyan zongjie le xinli xianxiang yu rennao jiegou 、 gongneng zhijian de lianxi 。jisuanji kexue yu rengong zhineng de xingqi ， shide renlei xinxi chuli shichang yu jixie xinxi chuli xianghu leibi 。dui renzhi de yanjiu bei yingyong yu erzhan ， yongyi lijie wuqi caozuo 。zai ershi shiji wanqi ， renzhizhuyi chengwei xinlixue de tongling fanshi ， renzhi xinlixue chengwei le liuxing fenzhi 。\n \n renzhi xinlixue renwei yinbi de xinli huodong yinggai shiyong kexue de fangshi jinxing yanjiu ， xinlixuejia chuangli le liang zhong gainian ： yuxia cijiwu yu neiyin jiyi ， duiying jingshen fenxi de qianyishi huo xingwei xue de ouran xingcheng xingwei 。xingweizhuyi yuansu yu renzhi xinlixue bei zhenghe chengwei renzhi xingwei liaofa de jichu 。zhezhongxinli zhiliao you meiguo xinlixuejia aerbote·ailisi he jingshen bingxuejia yalun·T·beike chuangli er cheng 。renzhi xinlixue yu qita xueke ， ru jingshen zhexue 、 jisuanji kexue 、 shenjing kexue ， yidao bei guiru de shangceng xueke renzhi kexue 。\n \n shengwu xinlixue huo xingwei shenjing kexue cong shengwu jiaodu yanjiu xingwei he xinli guocheng 。shengwu xinlixue zhong you butong de zhuanye fenzhi 。liru ， shengli xinlixue yunyong dongwu moxing ， tebieshi laoshu ， lai yanjiu shenjing 、 jiyin 、 xibaoji neng zai xuexi 、 jiyi 、 kongju zhong chansheng de zuoyong 。zhi shenjing kexuejia liyong shenjing chengxiang gongju yanjiu shenjing yu renlei xinli huodong zhijian de guanxi ， shenjing xinlixuejia shiyong xinli ceping lai jinxing kexue yanjiu ， ru danao sunshang dailai renzhi queshi de chengdu yu biaoxian xingshi 。\n \n linchuang xinlixue de yanjiu yu yingyong baokuo lijie 、 yufang 、 huanjie xinli tongku yu wenluan ， cujin xinli jiankang he geren chengzhang 。suiran linchuang xinlixuejia ye hui canyu yanjiu 、 jiaoxue 、 zixun 、 chutingzuozheng 、 chengxu bianding yu guanli ， dan gai fenzhi de zhongxin shi xinli ceping yu zhiliao 。yixie linchuang xinlixuejia hui zhuozhongyu duinao sunshang de bingren jinxing linchuang jianhu ， zhe yi lingyu bei chengwei 。zai xuduo guojia li ， linchuang xinlixue shi shoudao guanzhi de xinli jiankang zhuanye 。\n \n linchuang xinlixuejia suo zuo de nuli shoudao zhuduo zhiliao fangan de yingxiang ， suoyou fangan dou baokuo zhuanye renshi yu huanzhe （ tongchang shi geren 、 fuqi 、 jiating 、 huo xiao qunti ） zhijian de zhengshi guanxi 。butong de zhiliao shijian fangan yu butong de lilun guandian xianghu guanlian ， caiyong butong de liucheng lai jianli zhiliao zuhe 、 tanjiu xinli bingyin 、 guli xin de fangfa lai sikao 、 ganshou 、 xingdong 。si da zhiliao lilun guandian baokuo 、 renzhi xingwei zhiliao 、 cunzai — renbenzhuyi zhiliao he 。muqian you qushi biaoming yibufen xinlijia zhengzai nuli zhenghe gege zhiliao paixi ， tebieshi zai dui wenhua 、 xingbie 、 jingshen 、 xingquxiang de lijie jiashen de qingkuang xia ， zhege qushi gengjia xianzhu 。zai fengfu de yanjiu chengguo xia ， you zhengju biaoming ge da zhiliao paixi de xiaoguo quyu dengtong ， bing gongxiang xiangtong de jichu yuansu ， keyi xingcheng qiangda de xinli zhiliao zuhe 。zheng yinwei ruci ， geng duo de xinlixue peixun kecheng caiqu le 。\n \n renzhi xinlixue yanjiu xinli huodong zhong de renzhi 。zhijue 、 zhuyi 、 lizhi 、 siwei 、 jieti 、 jiyi 、 xuexi 、 yuyan 、 qingxu dou zai ta de yanjiu lingyu zhizhong 。jingdian renzhi xinlixue yu renzhizhuyi xuepai you xianghu lianxi ， genju jinengzhuyi yu shiyan xinlixue ， renzhizhuyi zhichi xinli xinxi chuli moxing 。\n \n zai geng guangyu de cengmian shang ， renzhi kexue shi yi zhong kuaxue kefanchou ， baokuo renzhi xinlixue 、 renzhi shenjing kexue 、 rengong zhineng 、 yuyanxue 、 renji hudong 、 jisuan shenjing kexue 、 shuli luoji yu renleixue 。jisuanji chang bei yongyu moni zhe lei shiyan xianxiang 。jisuanji moni wei yanjiu siwei de gongneng zuzhi tigong le gongju ， shenjing xitong kexue ze wei danao huodong tigong le duliangheng 。\n \n bijiao xinlixuezhi dui fei butong wuzhong de xingwei ， cong kunchong dao lingzhanglei dongwu 。bijiao xinlixue yu qita yanjiu dongwu xingwei de xueke ， ru dongwu xingwei xue you jinmi lianxi 。bijiao xinlixue de yanjiu youshi hui renlei xingwei xiangguan de shenjing chuli guocheng ， liru zai renzhi shenjing kexue jiu changchang yingyong dongwu moxing 。\n \n fazhan xinli xuezhe zhongyu renlei yizhi zai bisheng dangzhong de zhuanbian （ liru qingshaonian he laonian ） 。fazhan xinlixuejia sheji le yizhengtao xinlixue lilun lai zhichi tamen de yanjiu 。\n \n jiaoyu xinlixue shi yanjiu renlei zai jiaoyu guocheng zhong de xuexi jiaoshou fangshi yu jiaoxue shijian dou you zhongyao yingxiang 。zai xuduo guojia li ， jiaoyu xinlixue dou shi jiaoshi de bixiuke 。\n \n zuhe le jiaoyu xinlixue he linchuang xinlixue ， shitu lijie 、 xiaoduo·sitelin （ Theodore Sterling ）jisuan faxian 97% de xinli shiyan zhichi le tamen zuichu de jiashe ， anshi le piancha cunzai de keneng 。yu zhi leisi ， jianeier （ Fanelli ， 2010 ) faxian 91 . 5% de jingshen / xinli yanjiu dedao le zhengming ， suo dechu de wenti （ yangxing jieguo ） shi kongjian huo diqiu kexue de 5 bei da 。jianeier renwei jiao “ ruan ” kexue de yanjiu renyuan jiu tamen de  haiyangxue \n \n haiyangxue （ ） shi yanjiu haiyang de ziran xianxiang 、 xingzhi jiqi bianhua guilv ， yiji kaifa liyong haiyang de zhishi tixi 。ta shi yanjiu haiyang de dilixue de fenzhi 。ta hangai le butong de zhuti fanying le haiyangxuejia ronghe duo ge xueke dui shijieyang de jinyibu renshi he dui tianwenxue ， shengwuxue ， huaxue ， qihou xue ， dilixue ， dizhixue ， shuiwen kexue ， qixiangxue he  shuiwenxue \n \n shuiwenxue shuyu dilixue ， yanjiu de shi guanyu diqiu - { biao} - mian 、 turang zhong 、 yan shixia he daqi zhong shui de gezhong xingwei ， baohan shuixunhuan 、 hanliang 、 fenbu 、 yu dixiashui 。jing liuliang keyi fanying yi di ke yongshui de yingkui ， ye jiushi yige diqu shifou wei shengshuiqu huo queshuiqu ， geng yiwei zhujing liuliang de chaju ， zai butong diqu hui yingxiang  cehuixue \n \n ce huixue yanjiu ceding he tuisuan dimian jihe weizhi 、 diqiu xingzhuang ji diqiu zhonglichang ， juci celiang diqiu biaomian ziran wuti he rengong sheshi de jihe fenbu ， bianzhi gezhong bilichi ditu de lilun he jishu de xueke 。ce huixue de yanjiu duixiang shi diqiu de xingtai 、 weizhi 、 zhongli fenbu deng dili kongjian xinxi ， yiner cehuixue ke renwei shi diqiu kexue de yige fenzhixueke 。jinnianlai ， cehuixue de yanjiu duixiang hai cong diqiu biaomian kuoda dao le diwai kongjian ji diqiu neibu gouzao deng lingyu 。\n \n ce huixue de jinbu yilai renlei dui diqiu xingzhuang renshi de shenhua 、 ditu zhitu jishu de tigao he cehui yiqi de chuangxin ji biange 。\n \n zai shijie shang gushi shidai ， jiu you liyong cehuixue zhili niluohe fanlan hou nongtian bianjie de shuofa 。gongyuanqian 7 shiji ， guanzhong zai qi suo zhu 《 guanzi 》 yi shu zhong yi shouji le zaoqi de ditu 27 fu 。gongyuanqian 5 shiji zhi 3 shiji ， zhongguo yi you liyong cishi zhicheng zui zao de zhinan gongju “ sinan ” de jizai 。gongyuanqian 2 shiji ， zai 《 shiji·xiabenji 》 zhong jiu jizai you dayu zhishui shi “ zuo zhunsheng ， you guiju ” ， shuoming dangshi yijing you jiandan de cehui huodong 。\n  shuju jiegou \n\n zai jisuanji kexue zhong ， shuju jiegou （ ） shi jisuanji zhong cunchu 、 zuzhi shuju de fangshi 。\n \n shuju jiegou yiweizhe jiemian huo fengzhuang ： yige shuju jiegou ke bei shiwei de shuju jiegou xuanze keyi tigao yansuanfa de xiaolv （ qing cankao ） 。zai diannao chengshi sheji de guocheng zhong ， xuanze shidang de shuju jiegou shi yi xiang zhongyao gongzuo 。xuduo daxing xitong de bianxie jingyan xianshi ， chengshi sheji de kunnan chengdu yu zuizhong chengguo de zhiliang yu biaoxian ， qujueyu shifou xuanze le zui shihe de shuju jiegou 。\n \n xitong jiagou de guanjian yinsu shi shuju jiegou er feisuanfa de jianjie ， daozhi le duozhong xingshihua de sheji fangfa yu biancheng yuyan de chuxian 。juedaduoshu de yuyan dou daiyou mouzhong chengdu shang de mokuaihua sixiang ， touguo jiang shuju jiegou de juti shixian fengzhuang yincangyu shiyongzhe jiemian zhihou de fangfa ， lai rang butong de yingyong chengxu nenggou anquan di zhongyong zhexie shuju jiegou 。C + + 、 Java 、
