 zhonghua renmin gongheguo \n \n zhonghua renmin gongheguo ， tongcheng zhongguo ， shi weiyu dongya de shehuizhuyi guojia ， shoudu weiyu beijing 。zhongguo lingtu ludi mianji yue 960wan pingfanggongli ， shi shijie shang chun ludi mianji dier da 、 ludi mianji disan da 、 zongmianji disan da huo disi da de guojia ， qi fenwei 23 ge shengfen 、 5 ge zizhiqu 、 4 ge zhixiashi he 2 ge tebie xingzhengqu 。bei shiwei yazhou diqu zhongyao diyu daguo ， ye bei shiwei qianzai chaojidaguo 。shi shijie shang renkou zuiduo de guojia ， yue you 13 .9yi ren ， tongshi ye shi yige duo minzu guojia ， gongyou yi queren de minzu 56 ge ， qizhong hanzu renkou zhan 91 .51% 。yi putonghua he guifan hanzi wei guojia tongyong yuyan wenzi ， shaoshu minzu diqu ke shiyong ziji minzu de yuyan wenzi 。\n \n zhongguo dishi xigao dongdi er chengxian sanji jieti fenbu ， dabufen diqu shuyu wendai 、 furedai jifeng qihou ， dili jingzhi yu qihou xingtai fengfu duoyang ， you bingchuan 、 danxia 、 huangtu 、 shamo 、 kasite deng duozhong dimao ， beifang you gan caoyuan he huangmo ， nanfang you redai yulin ， xibu he xinan bianjing ze you tianshanshanmai 、 pamier gaoyuan 、 kala kunlun shanmai he ximalaya shanmai 。donglin taipingyang ， linghai you bohai （ neihai ） yiji huanghai 、 donghai 、 nanhai sanda bianhai zucheng ， shuiyu mianji yue 470wan pingfangqian mi ， fenbu you daxiao daoyu 7600 ge 。\n \n keji fangmian ， zhongguo zai - {zh-cn : hangtian ; zh - tw :hangtai ; zh - hk : hangtian ;} - hangkong 、 gaosu tielu 、 xin nengyuan 、 hejishu 、 chaoji jisuanji 、 liangzi wangluo deng lingyu you jiao qiang shili ， yanfa jingfei ze weiju shijie dier 。guofang yusuan wei shijie dier gao ， yongyou shijie guimo zui da de changbei budui ji sanweiyiti de he daji nengli 。zi 1986nian shixing jiu nian yiwu jiaoyu zhidu ， jiudu gongli xuexiao de xuesheng you zhengfu tigong qijian xuefei 。1978nian gaige kaifang hou ， zhongguo chengwei jingji chengzhang zui kuai de jingjiti zhiyi 。dangqian ， zhongguo duiwai maoyie shijie diyi ， shi shijie shang zui da de shangpin chukouguo ji dier da de jinkouguo ， yi guonei shengchan zongzhi an goumaili pingjia weilie shijie diyi 、 er guoji huilv ze paiming shijie dier 。2017nian ， zhongguo renjun guonei shengchan zongzhi yigou maili pingjia wei 18 , 119 meiyuan ， lie quanqiu di76 wei ； yi guoji huilv ze wei 8 , 643 meiyuan ， lie quanqiu di72 wei ， jun shang diyu shijie shuiping 。gaige kaifang yilai ， jinguan pinkun wenti dedao jida gaishan ， dan shouru chaju jiao da ， qie quyu jian fazhan bujun —— dongbu yanhai diqu de jingji jiao zhongxibu ji dongbei diqu fada —— de wenti reng ji xu jiejue 。\n \n 1949nian zhongguo gongchandang zai neizhan zhong qude youshi ， zhongjie le zhongguo guomindang zai zhongguo dalu de tongzhi ， yu tongnian 10yue 1ri jianli le zhonghua renmin gongheguo zhongyang renmin zhengfu ， bing yu tuishou taiwan diqu de zhonghua minguo zhengfu xingcheng liangan fenzhi de zhengzhi geju 。zunxun heping gongchu wu xiang yuanze de waijiao zhengce ， zai 1971nian qude zai lianheguo de zhongguo daibiaoquan hou ， chengwei lianheguo anquan lishihui changren lishiguo bing jiaru le xuduo guoji zuzhi 。\n \n zhonghua renmin gongheguo guoming zhong 「 zhonghua 」 daibiao zhonghua minzu ， 「 renmin 」 daibiao gongren 、 nongmin 、 xiao zichanjieji he minzu zichanjieji ， 「 gongheguo 」 daibiao guoti 。zuichu guoming ceng kaolv 「 zhonghua renmin minzhu gongheguo 」 ， bing jiazhu 「 jiancheng zhonghua minguo 」 。dan zai 1949nian 7yue 9ri juxing de zhongguo renmin zhengzhi xieshang huiyi choubei huiyi disi xiaozu dier ci huiyi shang ， zhangxiruo deng ren renwei mingcheng guochang er ying quchu 「 minzhu 」 erzi ， shiyong “ zhonghua renmin gongheguo ” ； er situmeitang deng xuduo minzhupai daibiao dui “ jiancheng zhonghua minguo ” 6 ge zichi you yiyi ， renwei ying queli xin guoming 。zuizhong ， zhongguo renmin zhengzhi xieshang huiyi diyi jie quanti huiyi zai 1949nian 9yue 27ri tongguo 《 》 ， jueyi guoming wei 「 zhonghua renmin gongheguo 」 bing quchu jiazhu 。gai huiyi hai jueding ： zhonghua renmin gongheguo de guodu dingyu beiping ， zi ji riqi gaiming beiping wei beijing ； zhonghua renmin gongheguo de jinian caiyong gongyuan ， jinnian wei yijiusijiunian ； zai zhonghua renmin gongheguo de guoge wei zhengshi zhiding qian ， yiyi yongjun jinxing quwei guoge ； zhonghua renmin gongheguo de guoqi wei wuxing hongqi ， xiangzheng zhongguo geming renmin datuanjie 。\n \n zhonghua renmin gongheguo youshi hui chengzuo 「 xin zhongguo 」 ， lai he xinminzhuzhuyi geming shiqi de 「 jiu zhongguo 」 zuo qufen 。buguo zai 1949nian ， zhonghua minguo zhengfu qianwang taiwan diqu hou ， reng bei guoji shehui shiwei zhongguo zhengfu ， bing zai lianheguo zhong yongyou zhongguo xici ； cishi zhonghua renmin gongheguo ze bei chengwei 「 hongse zhongguo 」 huo 「 gongchan zhongguo 」 ， bing jianchi ziji shi daibiao zhongguo de weiyi hefa zhengfu 。1971nian 10yue ， lianheguo dahui zai tongguo 《 lianheguo dahui 2758 hao jueyi 》 hou ， zhonghua renmin gongheguo qude zhongguo xici he xiangguan diwei ， 「 zhongguo 」 ye zhujian chengwei guoji shehui dui zhonghua renmin gongheguo de changjian chenghu 。ciwai ， zhonghua renmin gongheguo you jiancheng 「 zhong 」 huo 「 hua 」 ， ru “ zhong ri guanxi ” 、 “ zhuhua dashi ” deng 。youyu muqian liangan fenzhi de taihai xianzhuang ， yu taiwan diqu duiying shi ， zhonghua renmin gongheguo shiji guanxia de quyu you hui yin dili weizhi er chengzuo 「 zhongguo dalu 」 ， zhonghua renmin gongheguo zhengfu you bei chengwei 「 dalu dangju 」 、 「 beijing dangju 」 、 「 beijing 」 huo 「 zhonggong 」 ， huo yi zhonghua minguo xianfa zhong de tiaowen guiding chengwei 「 dalu diqu 」 。dang zhonghua renmin gongheguo dalu diqu yu gangao diqu bingcheng shi ， ze hui chengzuo 「 neidi 」 。\n \n 1912nian ， zhongguo zouxiang gonghe shiqi 。dan zai 7 nianhou zhonghua minguo beiyang zhengfu zai bali hehui shang weineng weihu guojia liyi ， daozhi le wusi yundong 。zai gongchanzhuyi sichao de yingxiang xia ， bufen zhongguo zhishifenzi yu 1921nian chengli le zhongguo gongchandang ， mubiao shi yao jianli yige wuchanjieji zhuanzheng de zhengquan 。1923nian zhonggong sanda jueding yu zhongguo guomindang jianli 「 geming tongyi zhanxian 」 ， tongshi zhongguo guomindang ye queding le 「 lian e 、 ronggong 、 fuzhu nonggong 」 de zhengce 。1927nian guomin gemingjun beifa qude jielian shengli zhiji ， zhongguo guomindang neibu zuopai he youpai douzheng que zai jiaju ， jiangjieshi zai nanjing lingli zhongyang bing shishi qingdang 。tongnian 8yue 1ri ， zhongguo gongchandang zai jiangxi nanchang fadong wuzhuang duoquan ； 10yue ， maozedong shuailing jing “ sanwan gaibian ” hou de qiushou qiyi budui shang jinggangshan ， genju 「 nongcun baowei chengshi ， wuzhuang duoqu zhengquan 」 de zhengce chuangli le jinggangshan geming genjudi 。\n \n 1928nian 4yue ， zhudelv lingnan changqi yiyubu yu xiangnan qiyi nongminjun daoda jinggangshan yu maozedong huishi 。1930nian 12yue dao 1931nian 9yue ， maozedong 、 zhude lingdao hongyi fangmianjun lianxu qude diyi 、 er 、 san ci fan “ weijiao ” zhanzheng de shengli ， xingcheng le yi ruijin wei zhongxin de yongyou 21 zuo xiancheng 、 5wan pingfanggongli mianji 、 250wan renkou de quanguo zui da de zhongyang geming genjudi 。1931nian 11yue ， zhonghua suweiai gongheguo zai jiangxi ruijin chengli 。1933nian ， zhongguo gongchandang cuobai guomin zhengfu fadong de disi ci weijiao ， tongguo sannian geming genjudi de zhili shijian ， jilei le jingyan 。1934nian 10yue ， zhongguo guomindang diwu ci jiaogong zhanzheng poshi zhonghua suweiai gongheguo linshi zhongyang zhengfu cheli jiangxi zhongyang suqu kaishi changzheng ， bing yu 1935nian 10yue dida shangan suqu 。1935nian 11yue ， zhonghua suweiai gongheguo zhongyang zhengfu xibei banshichu chengli 。tongnian 12yue ， zhonggong zhongyang zhaokai wayaobu huiyi ， jueding jiang zhonghua suweiai gongheguo gaiwei zhonghua suweiai renmin gongheguo 。1936nian zaidu gaiguohao wei “ zhonghua suweiai minzhu gongheguo ” ； xian shibian poshi jiangzhongzheng fangqi 「 rangwai bixian annei 」 zhengce ， jieshou 「 tingzhi jiaogong 、 yitong kangri 」 。\n \n 1937nian 9yue 6ri ， zhonghua suweiai minzhu gongheguo zhongyang zhengfu xibei banshichu gengming “ zhonghua minguo shanganning bianqu zhengfu ” ， chengwei zhonghua minguo de yige tebie xingzhengqu 。zhongguo gongchandang lingdao de zhongguo gongnong hongjun xiangji gaibian wei zhongguo guomin gemingjun diba lujun he xinbian disi jun ， xingcheng guogong hezuo kangri de jumian 。1945nian riben wutiaojian touxiang hou ， zai kangri zhanzheng qijian ji yi “ moca ” buduan de guogong shuangfang ， shengji wei gengwei yanzhong de “ chongtu ” 。shuangfang zuigao lingdaoren canjia de chongqing tanpan yi weineng zuzhi quanguoxing neizhan baofa 。neizhan jinxing zhi 1947nian 6yue ， zhongguo gongchandang lingdao jiefangjun cong zhanlve fangyu zhuanru zhanlve jingong 。1948nian mo zhi 1949nian chu ， jiefangjun luxu qude sandazhanyi shengli ， suihou zai dujiang zhanyi zhong zhanling le zhonghua minguo shoudu nanjingshi ji jingji zhongxin shanghaishi 。\n \n 1949nian 9yue 21ri ， you zhongguo gongchandang faqi zhaokai de ， you ge minzhu dangpai 、 ge renmin tuanti 、 ge diqu 、 renmin jiefangjun 、 ge shaoshu minzu he qita daibiao canjia de zhongguo renmin zhengzhi xieshang huiyi diyi ci quanti huiyi zai beijing kaimu 。huiyi tongguo le juyou linshi xianfa zuoyong de 《 gongtong gangling 》 he 《 zhonghua renmin gongheguo zhongyang renmin zhengfu zuzhifa 》 。\n \n 1949nian 10yue 1ri ， zhongguo gongchandang zhongyang weiyuanhui zhuxi maozedong zai beijingshi xuangao zhonghua renmin gongheguo zhengfu zhengshi chengli 。13ri ， jiefangjun zhanling hunan quanjing ，cishi zhongguo guomindang lingdao de zhonghua minguo zhengfu jin kongzhi xinan he huanan diqu ， bing zai shuyue jian bei jiefangjun zhubu zhanling 。guojun he zhengfu renyuan ze zhujian chewang taiwan 、 hainandao yu bufen yanhai daoyu ， bing zai 1950niandai xialing budui yu xibu diqu faqi panluan 。1950nian ， zhongguo zhengfu faqi zhenya fangeming 、 tudi gaige deng daguimo zhengzhi yundong 。touguo dui yue 100wan zhi 200wan ming tudi zhupi doufa fangyuan gengdi de tudi gaige ， zhonghua renmin gongheguo zhengfu deyi gonggu ， bing huode diceng minzhong de huanying 。tongnian 10yue ， zhiyuanjun chubing chaoxian ， jiaru chaoxian zhanzheng 。\n \n 1951nian ， zhonghua renmin gongheguo paiqian budui zhanling hainandao ， bing jiang xizang diqu naru tongzhi ， dazhi jiang menggu yiwai de wanqing shiqi guotu chongxin naru kongzhi ， bing chedi jieshu le zhongguo dalu zi minguo chunian yilai de junfa geju jumian ， jianli tongyi de quanguoxing zhengquan 。zhongguo jieyou 1953nian de diyi ge wunianjihua ， fazhan chu duli de gongye tixi ， bing zai ci jichu shang yanfa liangdanyixing jishu 。maozedong guli minzhong shengyu ， zhe shiqi renkou cong yuanxian de 5.5yi ren zengzhang zhi 9yi ren 。1956nian ， zhengfu tuichu 「 baihuaqifang 、 baijiazhengming 」 zhengce ， guli duli sikao yanlun ziyou 。1957nian qi damingdafang yundong ， guli qunzhong yao dui zhongda wenti shuochu ziji de yijian 。1957nian mo ， zhongguo gongchandang kaishi fadong fanyou yundong dui zhishifenzi jinxing zhengsu he laodong jiaoyang 。dao 1956nian di ， sanda gaizao jiben wancheng hou ， shangpin jingji zai zhongguo bufu cunzai ， shehuizhuyi zhidu jiben jianli 。1958nian ， zhongguo gongchandang tichu shehuizhuyi jianshe zongluxian 、 dayuejin he renmin gongshe yundong ， dui jingji he shehui zhankai gongchanzhuyi gaige ， qitu kuaisu dacheng gongchanzhuyi shehui 。dan ciju chongxian le sulian shehui gaizao de zainan ， zaocheng 1958nian zhi 1961nian zhishao shangqianwan ren yin jihuang siwang 。\n \n 1962nian qiqian ren dahui hou ， zhongguo gongchandang zhongyang weiyuanhui zhuxi maozedong he zhonghua renmin gongheguo zhuxi liushaoqi fasheng fenqi 。1966nian maozedong fadong wenhuadageming 。qijian ， hongweibing de posijiu yundong ji zhengzhi pidou dui shehui 、 jingji 、 wenhua 、 minzhu yu falv zhidu zaocheng le jiwei canzhong de huimieshi pohuai ， wenhuadageming zaocheng de shehui dongdang chixu zhi 1976nian maozedong shishi ， bing yin tongnian sirenbang zaodao daibu cai jieshu 。\n \n waijiao fangmian ， youyu zhong su jiaowu ， shehuizhuyi guojia jian xianru yanzhong fenlie ， maozedong tichu “ san ge shijie ” lilun ， xingcheng le yi disan shijie wei mengyou de guoji tongyi zhanxian celve ， zhongguo chengwei gongchanzhuyi de ling yi ji ， yu xifang guojia zhuliu guojia cedong fansu ， yinci 1971nian 10yue zhonghua renmin gongheguo qudai zhonghua minguo huode zai lianheguo zhong de zhongguo xiwei ， bing chengwei lianheguo anquan lishihui changren lishiguo 。1972nian nikesong fanghua huanhe le zhong mei guanxi 。1979nian meiguo xuanbu duanjue yu zhonghua minguo de waijiao guanxi ， zhuaner chengren zhonghua renmin gongheguo 。\n \n 1978nian ， wenge de pingfan gongzuo shi zhonggong gaoceng chuxian bianhua ， dengxiaoping fuchu hou jueding yi jingji fazhan wei zhongxin ， tichu gaige kaifang zhengce ， pipan zhonggong zhongyang weiyuanhui zhuxi huaguofeng de lianggefanshi ， bing jinxing zhenli biaozhun da taolun 、 pingfan yuanjiacuoan deng shixiang 。zhihou bujiu huaguo fengbian ciqu qi lingdao zhiwu ， gai you dengxiaoping 、 chenyun 、 lixiannian deng yuanlao jieshou zhangquan 。zhongguo gongchandang chengren “ wenhuadageming ” zai lilun he shijian shang shi wanquan cuowu de ， bing zhujian fangsong dui shehui de kongzhi ， renmin gongshe deng zhidu zaodao chexiao ， yi li nongmin siren tudi zulin 。1982nian ， zhongguo tongguo xianxing de 《 zhonghua renmin gongheguo xianfa 》 。1987nian ， zhonggong zhongyang zongshuji huyaobang yin baliu xuechao er xiatai ， gaiyou guowuyuan zongli zhaoziyang jieren ； 1989nian ， beijingshi xuesheng faqi liusi shijian ， zhongguo zhengfu paichu jundui zhenya ， er shoudao xifang guojia de qianze he jingji zhicai ， zhaoziyang ye yinci xiatai 。zhihou zhonggong shanghai shiwei shuji jiangzemin zai 1989nian xianhou fenbie jieti zhaoziyang he dengxiaoping danren zhonggong zhongyang weiyuanhui zongshuji 、 zhongyang junshi weiyuanhui zhuxi ， liusi shijian zhong biaoxian qiangying de lipeng jixu danren guowuyuan zongli 。\n \n zai jiangzemin ji xianhou liang ren guowuyuan zongli lipeng he zhurongji lingdao xia ， zhongguo cong jihua jingji zhuanxing wei you zhongguo tese de shehuizhuyi shichang jingji ， shichang jingji huanjing riyi kaifang 。qijian guji you 1.5yi ming nongmin tuoli pinkun ， guonei shengchan zongzhi pingjun meinian zengzhang 11 .2% 。jinguan minzhong shenghuo pinzhi yousuo tigao ， buguo zhengfu reng wei fangsong shehui guankong 。2001nian ， zhongguo jiaru shijie maoyi zuzhi 。dan chixu de jingji kuaisu - { zh-cn : zengzhang ; zh - tw : chengzhang } - ， ye wei jingnei ziyuan he huanjing dailai yanzhong yingxiang ， yiji daguimo de renkou qianxi 。2002nian 11yue ， dishiliu ci quanguo daibiao dahui xuanchu hujintao he wenjiabao deng zucheng disi dai lingdao jiti ， rennei juban xiaji aolinpike yundonghui 、 shanghai shijie bolanhui deng huodong 。2010nian hou ， zhongguo jingji zengzhang yin quanqiu jingji da shuaitui er jianhuan 。2011nian ， zhongguo guonei shengchan maoe chaoyue riben ， chengwei quanqiu dier da jingjiti 。2014nian ， yi goumaili pingjia jisuan ， zhongguo guonei shengchan zongzhi yijing chaoguo meiguo ， chengwei shijie diyi da jingjiti 。\n \n 2012nian 11yue ， zai dishiba ci quanguo daibiao dahui shang ， xijin pingjie ti hujintao jiuren zhonggong zhongyang weiyuanhui zongshuji he zhongyang junshi weiyuanhui zhuxi 。2013nian ， likeqiang zai dishier jie quanguo renmin daibiao dahui shang jieti wenjiabao danren guowuyuan zongli 。zai yi xijin pingwei zongshuji de xin yi jie zhongyang lingdao jiti zhudao xia ， zhengfu zhankai baokuo jihua shengyu 、 jianyu zhidu zainei de dafudu gaige ， yi jiejue jiegou bu wen he - { zh-cn : zengzhang ; zh - tw : chengzhang } - fanghuan de yingxiang 。2014nian zhaokai de yatai jinghe zuzhi fenghui shang ， xijinping biaoshi zhongguo jingji jiang jinru 「 xin changtai 」 。zai 2015nian ， zhongguo zhudao chengli yazhou jichu sheshi touzi yinhang 、 juban zhongguo kangri zhanzheng 70 zhounian jinian dahui 、 jinxing liangan lingdaoren huimian 。2016nian ， zhongguo shouci juban ershi guo jituan fenghui ； zai donghai 、 nanhai zhuquan zhengyi wenti shang ， tongguo yixilie daojiao jianshe he junshi yanxi zhujian baituo le beidong jumian 。2017nian ， 130 ge guojia daibiaotuan chuxi le zai beijing juban de yidai yilu fenghui 。\n \n zhonghua renmin gongheguo weiyu yazhou dongbu yu taipingyang xian 。zhongguo lingtu chun ludi mianji shijie dier 、 lingtu zongmianji disan 。buguo yi zongmianji de butong dingyi ， youxie shuju jiang zhongguo liezai eluosi 、 jianada 、 meiguo zhihou de disi ming 。zhongguo zongmianji yiban renwei yue you 960wan pingfanggongli ， butong difang ye you butong shuju ziliao ， baokuo da yingbai ke quanshu gongsi de 《 da yingbai ke quanshu 》 tidao de 9 , 572 , 900 pingfanggongli 、 de 《 》 biaoji de 9 , 596 , 961 pingfanggongli 、 ji zhongyang qingbaoju de 《 shijie gaikuang 》 biaoji de 9 , 596 , 961 pingfanggongli 。\n \n zhongguo fading jiangyu bei zhi mohexian yibei de heilongjiang hechuan hangdao zhongxinxian zhi beidian ， dongzhi heilongjiang he  zhongguo jisuanji kexue dashi nianbiao \n\n zhongguo jisuanji kexue dashi nianbiao anzhao shijian shunxu luolie le zhonghua renmin gongheguo jianguo yilai ， zai jisuanji kexue lingyu fasheng de zhongda shijian 。\n \n 
 kelisideng·naijiate \n\nkelisideng·naijiate （ ， ） ， nuowei jisuanji kexuejia ， shehui huodongjia ， tuling jiang he feng·nuoyiman jiang huodezhe ， Simula de chuangshiren ， mianxiang duixiang jishu de xianqu 。\n\nkelisideng·naijiate 1926nian shengyu nuowei de aosilu ， 1956nian yu aosilu daxue huode shuxue shuoshi xuewei ， lunwen shi 《 mengtekaluo fangfa de lilun fangmian 》 。\n \n 1948nian — 1960nian jian kelisideng·naijiate quanzhi gongzuoyu nuowei fangwu kexue yanjiu zhongxin （ Norwegian Defense Research Establishment ） ， jinxing jisuan 、 biancheng （ 1948nian — 1954nian ） he yunchouxue （ 1952nian — 1960nian ） fangmian de yanjiu 。\n \n 1957nian — 1960nian jian ta shi nuowei fangwu xitong zhong zui zao de yunchou yanjiu xiaozu de fuzeren 。ta shi nuowei yunchou yanjiu xuehui （ Norwegian Operational Research Society ） de gongtong chuangbanzhe he diyi ren zhuxi （ 1959nian — 1964nian ） 。1960nian ta shoupinyu nuowei jisuan zhongxin （ Norwegian Computing Center ） ， fuze ba nuowei jisuan zhongxin jianshe chengwei yige yanjiu jigou ， bingqie yu 1962nian chengwei yanjiu zhuguan （ Director of Research ） 。\n \n yu aoli - yuehan·daer （ Ole-Johan Dahl ）yidao ， ta kaifa le zui zao de mianxiang duixiang de chengxu sheji yuyan SIMULA -I （ 1961nian — 1965nian ） he SIMULA - 67 ， shouci yinru le mianxiang duixiang chengxu sheji yuyan de jiben gainian ： duixiang 、 lei 、 jicheng 、 virtual quantities 、 duoxiancheng （ zhun bingxing de ） de chengxu zhixing 。ta wei nuowei de gonghui jinxing jihua 、 kongzhi he shuju chuli fangmian de yanjiu ， yiqie dou yi canjia gonghui laogong de liyi lai pinggu （ 1971nian — 1973nian ， yu Olav Terje Bergo ） 。qita de yanjiu he kaifa gongzuo hai baokuo ： jisuanji jishu dui shehui de yingxiang he tongyong xitong miaoshu yuyanDELTA （ 1973nian — 1975nian yu Erik Holbaek - Hanssen he Petter Haandlykken ） 。\n\nkelisideng·naijiate shi danmaiaohusi daxue de jiaoshou （ 1975nian — 1976nian ） ， bingqie suihou chengwei nuowei aosilu daxue de jiaoshou （ 1977nian jianzhi ， 1984nian — 1996nian quanzhi ） 。ta zai aoerhusi he aosilu daxue de gongzuo baokuo xitong kaifa he jisuanji jishu dui shehui de yingxiang fangmian de yanjiu yu jiaoxue ， zhexie gongzuo wei rihou chengwei xitong kaifa zhong de sikandenaweiya xuepai dianding le jichu 。sikandenaweiya xuepai de gongzuo yu canyushi kaifa （ Participatory Design ） de lingyu miqie xiangguan 。1987nian ta chengwei meiguo paluoatuo de sitanfu daxue de fangwen jiaoshou ， shile paluo aertuo yanjiu zhongxin de fangwen xuezhe ， yiji pingguo gongsi de gaoji jishu xiaozu de guwen yu jiangshi 。\n \n 1990nian 6yue ta chengwei ruidian longde daxue de rongyu jiaoshou ， bing yu 1991nian 6yue chengwei danmaiaoerbao daxue de diyi ge rongyu jiaoshou 。ta shi nuowei kexueyuan de chengyuan 。\n \n 1990nian 10yue meiguo de xiehui — weile shehui zeren de jisuanji zhiyezhe （ Computer Professionals for Social Responsibility ， CPSR ） — yinwei ta shehui zerengan he zhiye gongzuo er shouyu ta nuobote·weina jiang 。1992nian tayin “ shi nuowei zai xinxi kexue lingyu wenming shijie ” er huode jisuanji shijie （ Computer world ） de rongyu jiangjin 。1999nian ta yu aoli - yuehan·daer yiqi huode le luoxinjiang （ Rosing Prize ） 。luoxinjiang shi nuowei shuju xiehui de wei zhuanye shang tebie de jinbu er sheli de xin jiangxiang 。2000nian 6yue mianxiang duixiang jishu de guoji biaozhunhua zuzhi —— duixiang guanli zuzhi （ Object Management Group ）yin ta zai “ duixiang jishu gainian shang de kaichuang gongzuo ” er shouyu rongyu huiyuan 。\n \n 2001nian 11yue ta yu aoli - yuehan·daer yiqi huode le dianji dianzi gongchengshi xuehui （ IEEE , Institute of Electrical and Electronics Engineers ） de yuehan·fengnuoyi manjiang ， bing pingjia ： “ jiangyu tamen zai sheji he shixian SIMULA67 shi yinru de gainian ， zhexie gainian shi mianxiang duixiang jishu de jishi 。 ”\n\n 2002nian 2yue ta you yi ci yu aoli -  Linux neihe \n\nLinux neihe （ ） ， shi yi zhong kaiyuan de lei Unix caozuo xitong hong neihe 。zhengge Linux caozuo xitong jiazu jiyu gai nei hebushu zai chuantong jisuanji pingtai （ ru geren jisuanji he fuwuqi ， yi Linux faxingban de xingshi ） he gezhong qianrushi pingtai ， ru luyouqi 、 wuxian jierudian 、 zhuanyong xiao jiaohuanji 、 jidinghe 、 、 zhineng dianshi 、 shuzi shipin luxiangji 、 wangluo fujia cunchu （ NAS ） deng 。gongzuo yu pingban diannao 、 zhineng shouji ji zhineng shoubiao de Android caozuo xitong tongyang tongguo Linux neihe tigong de fuwu wancheng zishen gongneng 。jinguan yu zhuomian diannao de zhanyonglv jiao di ， jiyu Linux de caozuo xitong tongzhi le jihu cong yidong shebei dao zhuji de qita quanbu lingyu 。jiezhi 2017nian 11yue ， shijie qian 500 tai zui qiang de chaoji jisuanji quanbu shiyong Linux 。\n\nLinux neihe zuizao shi yu 1991nian you fenlan heike linnasi·tuowazi wei ziji de geren diannao kaifa de ， ta dangshi zai Usenet xinwenzu codice _1 dengzai tiezi ， zhe fen zhuming de tiezi biaozhi zhe Linux neihe jihua de zhengshi kaishi 。rujin ， gai jihua yijing tuozhan dao zhichi daliang de jisuanji tixi jiagou ， yuanchao qita caozuo xitong he neihe 。ta xunsu xiyin le yipi kaifazhe he yonghu ， liyong ta zuowei qita ziyou ruanjian xiangmu de hexin ， ru zhuming de GNU caozuo xitong 。er jintian ， Linux neihe yi jieshou le chaoguo 1200 jia gongsi de jin 12000 ming chengxuyuan de gongxian ， qizhong baokuo yixie zhiming de ruanyingjian faxingshang 。\n \n cong jishu shang shuo ， Linux zhishi yige fuhe POS IX biaozhun de neihe 。ta tigong le yi tao yingyong chengxu jiekou （ API ） ， tongguo jiekou yonghu chengxu neng yu neihe ji yingjian jiaohu 。jinjin yige neihe bingbu shi yi tao wanzheng de caozuo xitong 。you yi tao jiyu Linux neihe de wanzheng caozuo xitong jiaozuo Linux caozuo xitong ， huoshi GNU /Linux （ zai gai xitong zhong baohan le henduo GNU jihua de xitong zujian ） 。\n\nLinux neihe shi zai GNU tongyong gonggong xukezheng di2 ban zhixia fabu shijie gedi ， richang kaifa xiangguan de taolun zai shang 。\n \n 1991nian ， linnasi·tuowazi ， yi ming 21 sui de jiudu yufenlan heerxinji daxue de jisuanji kexue zhuanye xuesheng ， jiyu yixie jiandan zuli fa le yi feng tiezi ： \n\n zhihou ， xuduo renwei zhege xiangmu gongxian le daima 。zai zaoqi ， MIN IX shequ xiang Linux neihe gongxian le daima he xiangfa 。dangshi ， GNU xiangmu yijing chuangjian 2006nian 5yue 12ri taneng baomu xie le yi fen lichang shengming 。\n\nLinux shi yige danti neihe ， zhichi zhenzheng de qiangzhanshi duorenwu chuli （ yu yong hutai ， he banben 2.6 xilie zhihou de nei hetai ） 、 xuni neicun 、 gong xiangku 、 、 gongxiang xieshi fuzhi ke zhixingti （ tongguo ） 、 neicun guanli 、 Internet xieyizu he xiancheng deng gongneng 。\n \n shebei qudong chengxu he neihe kuozhan yunxing yu neihe kongjian （ zai henduo CPU jiagou zhong shi ring 0 ） ， keyi wanquan fangwen yingjian ， dan ye you yunxing yu yonghu kongjian de yixie liwai ， liru jiyu FUSE / CUSE de wenjian xitong ， he bufen UIO 。duoshu ren yu Linux yiqi shiyong de tuxing xitong bu yunxing zai neihe zhong 。yu biaozhun danti neihe butong ， Linux de shebei qudong chengxu keyi qingyi de peizhi wei neihe mokuai ， bing zai xitong yunxing qijian ke zhijie zhuangzai huo xiezai 。ye butongyu biaozhun danti neihe ， shebei qudong chengxu keyi zai teding tiaojian xia bei qiangzhan ； zengjia zhege tezheng yongyu zhengque chuli yingjian zhongduan bing geng haode zhichi duichen duo chuli 。chuyu ziyuan xuanze ， Linux neihe meiyou erjinzhi neihe jiekou 。\n \n yingjian ye bei zhenghe ru wenjian cengji zhong 。yonghu yingyong dao shebei qudong de jiekou shi zai huo mulu xia de rukou wenjian 。jincheng xinxi ye tongguo mulu yingshe dao wenjian xitong 。\nLinux shi yong Cyuyan zhong de GCCban （ zhezhong Cyuyan you dui biaozhunC jinxing kuozhan ） xie de ， haiyou ji ge yong zuhe yuyan （ yong de shi GCC de \"AT&T fengge \" ）xie de mubiao jiagou duanduan 。yinwei yao zhichi kuozhan de Cyuyan ， GCC zai hen zhang de shijian li shi weiyi yige neng zhengque bianyi Linux de bianyiqi 。you xuduo qita de yuyan yong zai yixie fangmian shang ， zhuyao jizhong zai neihe goujian guocheng zhong （ zheli zhi congyuan daima chuangjian ke qidong jingxiang ） 。baokuo Perl 、 Python he duozhong jiaoben yuyan 。you yixie qudong keneng shi yongC + + 、 Fortran huo qita yuyan xie de ， danshi zheyang shi qianglie bu jianyi de 。\n \n GCC shi Linux nei heyuan daima de quesheng bianyiqi 。zai 2004nian ， Intel zhuzhang tongguo xiugai neihe ， yibian Intel C + + bianyiqi neng zhengque bianyi neihe 。zai 2009nian ， you tongguo xiugai nei he2 .6 . 22 ban er chenggong bianyi de baogao （ bing dailai pingjun 8-9 %xiao neng zengzhang ） 。\n \n zicong 2010nian ， yijing kaishi jinxing shiyong Clang jianzao Linux neihe de nuli ， Clang shi yige ke zuowei tidai de Cyuyan bianyiqi ； jiezhi 2014nian 4yue 12ri ， guanfang neihe jihu keyi wanquan yong Clang bianyi 。zhiliyu zhege mubiao de jihua jiaozuo “ LLVMLinux ” ， de mingyu Clang suo jiyu de LLVM bianyiqi xiabu gouzao 。LLVMLinux bu yitu fuzhi Linux neihe huo LLVM ， yinci ta shi you zuizhong tijiao gei shangyou jihua de buding goucheng de yige yuan jihua 。shi Linux neihe keyi yong Clang bianyi zui da de haochu shi bi GCC you geng kuai de bianyi sudu ， neihe kaifazhe keyi deyiyu youcierlai de geng kuai de gongzuo liucheng 。\n \n fuhe biaozhun shi Linux neihe neibu de pubian celve 。ling yige guize shi Linux neihe zhuxian bu jieshou zhi you zhuanyou yonghu kongjian ruanjian shiyong de neihe mokuai 。\n \ nyuan daima ke yizhixing quebao fuhe biaozhun de Cchengxu keyi zai fuhe tongyang biaozhun de renhe xitong shang bianyi he yunxing 。Linux neihe kaifa 、 GNU Chan shuku he xiangguan de shiyong gongju zhiliyu zhuisui POS IX he danyiUN IX guifan 。shi neihe de xitong diaoyong jiekou 。\n \n er jinzhi ke yizhixing jiang baozheng renhe chengxu zai fuhe biaozhun de geiding yingjian pingtai shang yidan bianyi tongguo ， keyi zai fuhe tongyang biaozhun de renhe qita yingjian pingtai shang yi bianyi hou de xingshi yunxing 。er jinzhi ke yizhixing shi zai jiyu Linux neihe de caozuo xitong shang jianzao duli ruanjian gongyingshang （ ISV ） yingyong you shangye kexingxing de benzhi yaoqiu 。xianyou weiyi de erjinzhi jianrong biaozhun shi Linux biaozhun guifan （ LSB ） 。\n \n zai bu tongzi xitong jian shiyong le shu ge neihe neibu API 。qizhong yixie shi kuayue duo ge neibu ye jiaozuo codice _6 ， er neihe hai hanyou liang ge zunxun POS IX de shishi diaodu lei ， fenbie jiaozuo codice _ 7 （ shishi xianjin xianchu ） he codice _8 （ shishilunliushi ） ， erzhe dou shixian le （ EDF ） suanfa ， ta zengjia yu 2014nian 3yue 30ri faxing de neihe banben 3 . 14 。\n \n jinguan linnasi·tuowazi de chuzhong bushi shi Linux chengwei yige ke yizhi de caozuo xitong ， jintian nuojiya Maemo 。\n \n zai Linux zhong ， neihe cuowu （ ） shi zhi caozuo xitong zai jiance dao neihe xitong neibu wufa huifu de cuowu ， xiangduiyu zai yonghu kongjian daima leisi de cuowu 。caozuo xitong shitu du xie wuxiao huo bu yunxu de neicun dizhi shi daozhi neihe cuowu de yige changjian yuanyin 。neihe cuowu ye you keneng zai yudao yingjian cuowu huo caozuo xitong BUG shi fasheng 。zai xuduo qingkuang zhong ， caozuo xitong keyi zai neicun fangwen weili fasheng shi jixu yunxing 。raner ， xitong chuyu bu wending zhuangtai shi ， caozuo xitong tongchang hui tingzhi gongzuo yi bimian zaocheng pohuai anquan he shuju sunhuai de fengxian ， bing tigong cuowu de zhenduan xinxi 。\n \n zai Linux shang ， oops ji Linux neihe de xingwei bu zhengque ， bing chansheng le yi fen xiangguan de cuowu rizhi 。xuduo leixing de oops hui daozhi neihe cuowu ， jiling xitong liji tingzhi gongzuo ， dan bufen oops ye yunxu jixu caozuo ， zuowei yu wendingxing de tuoxie 。zhege gainian zhi daibiao yige jiandan de cuowu 。dangnei hejian cedao wenti shi ， ta hui dayin yige oops xinxi ranhou shasi quanbu xiangguan jincheng 。oo ps xinxi keyi bangzhu Linux neihe gongchengshi tiaoshi ， jiance oops chuxian de tiaojian ， bing xiufu daozhi oops de chengxu cuowu 。\n \n jisuanji anquan shi yige feichang gongzhonghua de zhuti ， guanxi dao Linux neihe ， yinwei daliang zainei hezhong de cuowu keneng chengwei qianzai de anquan loudong ， shifou yunxu tisheng quanxian loudong huo jujue fuwu gongji yuan loudong 。zai guoqu de ji nianzhong ， xuduo zheyang de quexian bei faxian ， bing zai Linux neihe zhong bei xiubu hao 。xin de anquan gongneng bei jixu shixian ， yi jiejue zai Linux nei hezhong de diannao bu anquan wenti 。\n \n pipingzhe zhize neihe kaifa renyuan ， cheng tamen yangai （ zhishao bing wei gongbu ） anquan loudong 。2008nian ， zuowei huiying ， Torvalds cheng ： 「 geren renwei ， anquan loudong zhishi 『 zhengchang de loudong 』 。zhexie loudong wo bingbu qu yangai ， buguo wo bu renwei yingdang ba tamen teshuhua ， geng bu renwei yinggai zhuizong bing gongshi tamen …… wo bu lihui zhengge anquan tuandui ， yuanyin zhiyi jiushi ， wo renwei zhexie loudong bujin meihua hai guli le cuowu de xingwei 。zhe ling anquan renyuan cheng le 『 yingxiong 』 ， jiu youru bu xiubu zhengchang loudong de ren jiu bu zhi yi tishi de 。er shishishang ， suoyou wuliao de zhengchang loudong jiwei zhongyao ， jinjin yinwei tamen shizai tai duo le 。wo bu renwei gai meihua he guanxin naxie yanzhong de anquan loudong —— tamen bingbu ji naxie you sisuo zaocheng de suiji yanzhong bengkui laide geng teshu 。 」\n \n ru 2012nian wuyue ， SYSRET zhiling bei faxian zai AMD he yingteer chuli qijian zai shixian fangmian you chayi ， zhege chayi zai Windows 、 Fre eBSD 、 X enServer he Solaris zhexie zhuliu zuoye xitong hui daozhi loudong 。2012nian liuyue ， Linux hexin zhong gai wenti yi bei xiufu 。\n \n jiezhi 2007nian ， neihe kaifa yijing cong 20 wei zui huoyue kaifazhe xie 80% de daima zhuanbian wei dingduan 30 ren xie 30% de daima ， er dingduan kaifazhe huafei geng duo de shijian shenhe biangeng 。kaifazhe hai keyi an congshu guanxi lai guilei ； zai 2007nian ， dingduan leishu shi “ bu zhiming ” er dingduan gongsi shi shequ you 5000 huo 6000 ming chengyuan zucheng 。\n\nLinux jijinhui fabiao de 2016nian Linux neihe kaifa baogao de gengxin biaoming ， cong banben 3 . 18 （ 2014nian 12yue ） zhi 4.7 （ 2016nian 7yue ） zhiding banben ， name keyi shiyong renhe banben ； bingqie ailun·kaokesi zhichu ， henshao you qita Linux gongxianzhe zhiding le teding banben de GPL 。\n \n 2006nian 9yue ， dui 29 wei guanjian nei hecheng xuyuan de diaocha xianshi qizhong de 28 wei geng qingxiangyu shiyong GPL dier ban （ GPLv2 ） er fei dangshi de GPL disan ban （ GPLv3 ） caoan 。tuowazi pinglun shuo ： “ wo renwei yixie waijie renshi ... xiangxin wo cai shi nage guguai bu hequn de ren ， yinwei wo zheme dazhangqigu di bu zuo GPLv3 de zhongshi fensi 。 ”zhexie gao shuiping de neihe kaifazhe jiu dazhong meiti dui GPLv3 de fandui fabiao le pinglun ， qizhong baokuo linnasi·tuowazi benren 、 geleige·keluohaman he andelu·modun 。tamen tidao youguan DRM / 、 zhuanli ji “ fujia xianzhi ” de tiaokuan ， bing jinggao G PLv3 dui “ kaiyuan yuzhou ” de baerganhua 。jueding bu caiyong GPLv3 zuowei Linux nei hexu kezheng de tuowazi zai ji nianhou chongshen le ta de piping 。\n \n xukezheng zhengyi de yige zhongdian shi Linux shiyong renti er jinwei baoyi zhiyuan mouxie yingti zhuangzhi 。licha·maxiu·situoman renwei zhexie dongxi rang Linux mou bufen chengwei fei ziyou ruanti ， shenzhi yici sanbu Linux geng hui pohuai GPL ， yinwei xuangao de qudong chengshi yongyu hexin 。dan ye bushi meige ren dou ruci tongyi ， qie tuo wazi ye tongyi henduo LKM dique shi chuncui de yansheng chuangzuo ， ye xiexia 「 jibenshang ， hexin mozu shi yansheng chuangzuo 」 zheyang de juzi 。lingyifangmian tuowazi ye shuo guo ： \n\n tebie xiang huituka qudong chengshi jiu you feichang da de zhengyi ， yexu dao zuihou de you lifa jiguan gei ge daan 。\n \n zai 2003nian 3yue ， SCO Group dui IBM tigao ， shengcheng IBM jiang yixie zai SCO zhihui caichanquan xukezheng baohu xia de Unixyuan shima zhiru Linux zhong ， pohuai le SCO jiyu IBM de yuanshima shiyong xukequan 。lingwai SCO ye fachu yidadui cunzheng hangei xuduo gongsi ， jinggao tamen zai meiyou SCO xukequan de qingkuang xia shiyong le Linux ， ciju keneng daozhi qinfan zhihui caichanquan ， bingqie yi qisu wei shouduan dui gebie shiyongzhe shiya 。SCO ye tongshi dui Novell 、 daimuleikelaisilei （ DaimlerChrysler ， zai 2004nian 7yue bei bufen bohui ） yiji Auto Zone tichu gaosu ， qie bei Red bushi SCO 。2010nian 3yue 20ri ， meiguo lianbang dishi xunhui shangsu fayuan xuanpan ， Novell cai shi UN IX yu UnixWare shangbiao de hefa yongyouzhe 。cixiang panjue xuanbu hou ， yi jinru pochan baohu chengxu de SCO gongsi ， jueding tingzhi jixu tichu susong 。\n \n 
 linnasi·tuowazi \n \n linnasi·bennadikete·tuowazi （ ，， ） ， shengyu fenlan heerxinjishi ， yongyou meiguo guoji ， Linux neihe de zuizao zuozhe ， suihou faqi le zhege kaiyuan xiangmu ， danren Linux neihe de shouyao jiagoushi yu zhuanan xietiaozhe ， shi dangjin shijie zui zhuming de diannao chengxuyuan 、 heike zhiyi 。ta hai faqi le Git zhege kaiyuan xiangmu ， bing wei zhuyao de kaifazhe 。\n \n tuo wazi chusheng yu fenlan heerxinjishi 。fuqin niersi·tuowazi （ Nils Torvalds ） shi yi ming huoyue de diantai jizhe ， muqin anna·tuowazi （ Anna Torvalds ） ye shi yi ming jizhe 。zufu aoer·tuowazi （ Ole Torvalds ） shi yi ming shiren he jizhe 。waizufu shi fenlan diyi pi tongjixue jiaoshou 。fenlan tongji xuehui sheli Leo Törnqvist Award ， shouyu zai banjiang zhiqian de liang niannei jiechu de tongjixue shuoshi xuewei wanchengzhe 。linnasi·tuowazi zai 11 sui shi ， ying qiwai zufu yaoqiu yong BASIC yuyan bianxie yixie tongjixue fangmian de xiao chengxu ， zheshi ta biancheng jingli zhi shi 。\n \n tuowazi jiazu shuyu zai fenlan zhan 6% de fenlan ruidianzu ， qi fumu dou biyeyu heerxinji daxue ， zai xueqi jian shi jiji de xueyun fenzi 。ta de mingzi laiziyu lainasi·baolin （ Linus Pauling ） ， yi wei nuobeier huaxue jiang dezhu 。\n \n 1988nian ， ta jinru heerxinji daxue jisuanji kexuexi 。1989nian ， ta jinru fenlan lujun xin diqu lv ， fu11 ge yue de ， junjie wei shaowei ， zhuyao fuwu yu jisuanji bumen ， renwu shi dandao jisuan 。fuyi qijian ， goumai le andelu·situerte·taneng baomu suo zhu de jiaokeshu ji mini xyuan shima ， kaishi yanjiu zuoye xitong 。1990nian ， ta tuiwu hou huidao daxue ， kaishi jiechu Unix 。1991nian 8yue 25ri ， zai wanglu shang fabu le Linux neihe de yuanshima 。1994nian 3yue 14ri fabu le 1. 0 banben 。\n \n 1996nian ， ziheerxinji daxue shuoshi biye ， xuewei lunwen shi 《 Linux : A Portable Operating System 》 。zai baifang quan meida gongsi （ Transmeta ） zhihou ， tuowazi jueding jieshou tamen de pinyong ， bing yiju meiguo jiazhou 。zi 1997nian 2yue ， zhi 2003nian 6yue zhijian ， tuowazi dou zai quan meida gongsi fuwu ， canyu gai gongsi jingpian de code morph jishu yanfa 。zai 1997nian zhi 1999nian jian ， zhuyao touru 86open jihua 。\n \n 1999nian ， Red Hat ji V A Linux zhe liang jian gongsi ， jueding jiang tamen gongsi de gupiao qiquan （ stock option ） yi bufen zengyu tuowazi ， yi ganxie ta de gongxian 。tongnian ， zai zhe liang jian gongsi de gupiao  lichade·situoman \n \n lichade·maxiu·situoman （ ， jiancheng ， ） ， meiguo chengxuyuan ， ziyou ruanjian huodongjia 。ta faqi ziyou ruanjian yundong ， changdao ruanjian shiyongzhe nenggou dui ruanjian GDB 、 GNU Emacs ， tongshi bianxie le GNU tongyong gonggong xuke xieyi 。\n \n Stall man weile chuangjian yige wanquan you mianfei ruanjian zucheng de lei Unix jisuanji caozuo xitong zai 1983nian 9yue GNU ruanjian ， qizhong baokuo GCC GDB GNU Emacs 。zai 1985nian 10yue ta chuangli le ziyou ruanjian jijinhui 。\n \n situoman kaichuang le Copyleft de gainian ， ta shiyong banquanfa de yuanze lai baohu  sunzhongshan \n\n sunzhongshan （ ） ， mingwen ， youming dixiang ， puming deming ， zizai zhi ， haoyixian 、 rixin 。liuwang riben shi ， ceng huaming zhongshanqiao ， gutong cheng sunzhongshan zhonghua minguo dianjiren ， yi shi zhongguo guomindang zhi chuang dangren 。tichang sanminzhuyi 。\n \n qi tongnian ceng shou taiping tianguo de yingxiang er you geming sixiang 。28 sui shangshu qingchao  caozuo xitong \n \n caozuo xitong （ ， suoxie zuo ） shi guanli jisuanji yingjian yu ruanjian ziyuan de xitong ruanjian ， tongshi ye shi jisuanji xitong de hexin yu jishi 。caozuo xitong xuyao chuli ru guanli yu peizhi neicun 、 jueding xitong ziyuan gongxu de youxian cixu 、 kongzhi shuru yu shuchu zhuangzhi 、 caozuo wangluo yu guanli wenjian xitong deng jiben shiwu 。caozuo xitong ye tigong yige rang shiyongzhe yu xitong hudong de caozuo jiemian 。\n \n caozuo xitong de xingtai feichang duoyang ， butong jiqi anzhuang de caozuo xitong ke cong jiandan dao fuza ， ke cong xingdong dianhua de qianrushi xitong dao chaoji diannao de daxing zuoye xitong 。xuduo caozuo xitong zhizaozhe dui ta hangai fanchou de dingyi ye bujinyizhi ， liru youxie caozuo xitong zhenghe le tuxing yonghu jiemian ， er youxie jin shiyong minglingxing jiemian ， er jiang tuxing yonghu jiemian shiwei yi zhong fei biyao de yingyong chengshi 。\n \n caozuo xitong lilun zai jisuanji kexue zhong ， wei lishi youjiu de fenzhi ； 。\n \n zongguan diannao zhi lishi ， zuoye xitong yu diannao yingti de fazhan xixixiangguan 。zuoye xitong zhi ben yiyuan wei tigong jiandan de gongzuo paixu nengli ， hou wei fuzhu gengxin geng fuza de yingti sheshi er jianjian yanhua 。cong zui zao de pici moshi kaishi ， fenshi jizhi ye suizhi chuxian ， zai duo chuliqi shidai lailin shi ， zuoye xitong ye suizhi tian jiaduo chuliqi xietiao gongneng ， shenzhi shi fensanshi xitong de xietiao gongneng 。qita fangmian de yanbian ye leisi yu ci 。lingyifangmian ， zai geren diannao shang ， geren diannao zhi zuoye xitong yinxi daxing diannao de chengzhang zhi lu ， zai yingti yuelaiyue fuza 、 qiangda shi ， ye zhubu shijian yiwang zhi you daxing diannao cai youde gongneng 。\n \n zongeryanzhi ， zuoye xitong de lishi jiushi yi bu jiejue diannao xitong xuqiu yu wenti de lishi 。\n \n diyi bu diannao bingmeiyou zuoye xitong 。zheshi youyu zaoqi diannao de jianli fangshi （ rutong jianzao jixie suanpan ） yu xiaoneng bu zuyi zhixing ruci chengshi 。dan zai 1947nian faming le dianjingti ， yiji molisi·weierkesi faming de weichengxu fangfa ， shide diannao buzai shi jixie zhuangzhi ， ershi dianzi chanpin 。xitong guanli gongju yiji jianhua yingti caozuo liucheng de chengshi henkuai jiu chuxian le ， qie chengwei zuoye xitong de qiyuan 。dao le 1960niandai zaoqi ， shangyong diannao zhizaoshang zhizao le pici chuli xitong ， ci xitong ke jiang gongzuo de jianzhi 、 paicheng yiji zhixing xuliehua 。cishi ， changshang wei mei yi tai butong xinghao de diannao chuangzao butong de zuoye xitong ， yinci wei mou diannao er xie de chengshi wufa yizhi dao qita diannao shang zhixing ， jishi shi tongxinghao de diannao ye buxing 。\n \n dao le 1964nian ， IBM System / 360 tuichu le yixilie yongtu yu jiawei dou butong de daxing diannao ， er tamen dou gongyong daihao wei OS / 360 de zuoye xitong （ er fei mei zhong chanpin dou yong liangshen ding zuo de zuoye xitong ） 。rang danyi zuoye xitong shiyong yu zhengge xilie de chanpin shi System / 360 chenggong de guanjian ， qie shijishang IBM muqian de daxing xitong bian shi ci xitong de houyi ， wei System / 360 suo xie de yingyong chengshi yiran keyi zai xiandai de IBM jiqi shang zhixing 。\n \n OS / 360 ye baohan ling yige youdian ： yongjiu zhucun zhuangzhi — yingpan de mianshi （ IBM chengwei DASD ） 。ling yige guanjian shi fenshi gainian de jianli ： jiang daxing diannao zhengui de shijian ziyuan shidang fenpei dao suoyou shiyongzhe shenshang 。fenshi ye rang shiyongzhe you duzhanzhengbu jiqi de ganjue ； er Multics de fenshi xitong shi cishi zhongduo xin zuoye xitong zhong shijian ci guannian zui chenggong de 。\n \n 1963nian ， qiyi gongsi yu beier shiyanshi hezuo yi P L / I yuyan jianli de Multics ， shi jifa 1970niandai zhongduo zuoye xitong jianli de linggan laiyuan ， youqishi you AT & Tbeier shiyanshi de dannisi·liqi yu ken·tangpuxun suo jianli de Unix xitong ， weile shijian pingtai yizhi nengli ， ci zuoye xitong zai 1973nian you Cyuyan zhongxie ； ling yige guangwei shichang caiyong de xiaoxing diannao zuoye xitong shi VMS 。\n \n diyi dai weixing jisuanji bingbu xiang daxing diannao huo xiaoxing diannao ， meiyou zhuangshe zuoye xitong de xuqiu huo nengli ； tamen zhi xuyao zui jiben de zuoye xitong ， tongchang zhezhong zuoye xitong dou shi cong ROM duqu de ， ci zhong chengshi bei chengwei jianshi chengshi （ Monitor ） 。1980niandai ， jiayong diannao kaishi puji 。tongchang cishi de diannao yongyou 8 - bit chuliqi jiashang 64 KB jiyiti 、 yingmu 、 jianpan yiji di yinzhi laba 。er 80niandai zaoqi zui zhuming de taozhuang diannao wei shiyong weichuliqi 6510 （ 6502 jingpian tebieban ） de Commodore C64 。ci diannao meiyou zuoye xitong ， ershi yi yi8KB weidu jiyiti BIOS chushihua caise yingmu 、 jianpan yiji ruandieji he yinbiaoji 。ta keyong 8KB weidu jiyiti BASIC yuyan lai zhijie caozuo BIOS ， bing yici zhuanxie chengshi ， dabufen shi youxi 。ci BASIC yuyan de zhiyiqi mianqiang ke suanshi ci diannao de zuoye xitong ， dangran jiu meiyou hexin huo ruan yingti baohu jizhi le 。ci diannao shang de youxi daduo tiao guo BIOS cengci ， zhijie kongzhi yingti 。\n \n zaoqi zui zhuming de cidie qidongxing zuoye xitong shi CP / M ， ta zhiyuan xuduo zaoqi de weidiannao 。zuizaoqi de IBM PC qi jiagou leisi C64 。dangran tamen ye shiyong le BIOS yi chushihua yu chouxianghua yingti de caozuo ， shenzhi ye fu le yige BASIC zhiyiqi ！danshi ta de BASIC youyu qita gongsi chanpin de yuanyin zaiyu ta you kexiexing ， bingqie xiangrongyu renhe fuhe IBM PC jiagou de jiqi shang 。zheyang de PC ke liyong Intel - 8088 chuliqi （ 16 - bitzan cunqi ） dingzhi ， bing zuiduo ke you 1MB de jiyiti ， raner zuichu - { zhi } - you 640 KB 。ruanshi cidieji qudai le guoqu de cidaiji ， chengwei xinyidai de chucun zhuangzhi ， bing ke zai ta 512 KB de kongjian shang du xie 。weile zhiyuan gengjinyibu de dangan du xie gainian ， cidie zuoye xitong （ Dis k Operating System ， DOS ）yiner dansheng 。ci zuoye xitong keyi hebing renyi shuliang de ciqu ， yinci keyi zai yi zhang cidiepian shang fangzhi renyi shuliang yu daxiao de dangan 。dangan zhijian yi dangming qubie 。IBM bingmeiyou hen zaiyi qi shang de DOS ， yinci yi xiang waibu gongsi goumai de fangshi qude zuoye xitong 。1980nian weiruan gongsi qude le yu IBM de heyue ， bingqie shougou le yijia gongsi chuchan de zuoye xitong ， zai jiang zhi xiugai hou yi MS - DOS de mingyi chupin ， ci zuoye xitong keyi zhijie rang chengshi caozuo BIOS yu dangan xitong 。dao le Intel - 80286 chuliqi de shidai ， cai kaishi shizuo jiben de chucun zhuangzhi baohu cuoshi 。qihou ， MS - DOS chengwei le IBM PC shangmian zui changyong de zuoye xitong （ IBM ziji ye you tuichu DOS ， chengwei IBM - DOS huo PC - DOS ） 。MS - DOS de chenggong shide weiruan chengwei diqiu shang zui zhuanqian de gongsi zhiyi 。\n \n er 1980niandai ling yige jueqi de zuoye xitong yishu shi Mac OS ， ci zuoye xitong jinjin yu maijinta diannao kunbang zaiyiqi 。cishi yi wei shile paluoaoduo yanjiu zhongxin de yuangong Dominik Hagen fangwen le pingguo diannao de shidifu·qiaobusi ， bingqie xiang ta zhanshi le cishi quanlu fazhan de tuxinghua shiyongzhe jiemian 。pingguo diannao jingwei tianren ， bing dasuan xiang quanlu goumai ci jishu ， dan yin paluoaoduo yanjiu zhongxin bingfei shangye danwei ershi yanjiu danwei ， yinci quanlu huijue le zhexiang maimai 。zai ci zhihou pingguo yizhi renwei geren diannao de weilai biding shuyu tuxing shiyongzhe jiemian ， yinci ye kaishi fazhan ziji de tuxinghua zuoye xitong 。\n \n yanxu 1980niandai de jingzheng ， 1990niandai chuxian le xuduo yingxiang weilai geren diannao shichang shenhou de zuoye xitong 。youyu tuxinghua shiyongzhe jiemian riqu fanfu ， zuoye xitong de nengli ye yuelaiyue fuza yu juda ， yinci qiangren qie juyou tanxing de zuoye xitong jiu cheng le poqie de xuqiu 。ci niandai shi xuduo tao zhuanglei de geren diannao zuoye xitong huxiang jingzheng de shidai 。\n \n shang yi niandai yu shichang jueqi de pingguo diannao ， youyu jiu xitong de sheji buliang ， shide qi houji fazhan buli ， pingguo diannao jueding chongxin sheji zuoye xitong 。jingguo xuduo shibai de zhuanan hou ， pingguo yu 1997nian shichu xin zuoye xitong —— Mac OS X de ceshiban ， erhou tuichu de zhengshiban qude le juda de chenggong 。rang yuanxian shiyi likai pingguo de shidifu·qiaobusi fengguang zaixian 。\n \n chule shangye zhuliu de zuoye xitong wai ， cong 1980niandai qi zai kaifangyuan daima de shijie zhong ， BSD xitong ye fazhan le feichang jiu de yi duan shijian ， dan zai 1990niandai youyu yu AT&T de falv zhengduan ， shide yuanzai fenlan heerxinji daxue de ling yi gu kaiyuan zuoye xitong —— Linux xingqi 。Linux hexin shi yige biaozhun POS IX hexin ， qi xueyuan ke suanshi Unix jiazu de yi zhi 。Linux yu BSD jiazu dou dapei GNU jihua suo fazhan de yingyong chengshi ， danshi youyu shiyong de xukezheng yiji lishi yinsu de zuonong xia ， zhineng yunxing zai Intel CPUshang ） ， ta ye shi yige fenshi duo xingcheng hexin ， yiji lianghao de jiyiti kongjian guanli （ putong de xingcheng bu neng cunqu hexin quyu de jiyiti ） 。xiangyao cunqu renhe fei ziji de jiyiti kongjian de xingcheng zhineng touguo xitong diaoyong lai dacheng 。yiban xingcheng shi chuyu shiyongzhe moshi （ User mode ） dixia ， er zhixing xitong hujiao shi hui bei qiehuan cheng hexin moshi （ Kernel mode ） ， suoyou de teshu zhiling zhi neng zai hexin moshi zhixing ， ci cuoshi rang hexin keyi wanmei guanli xitong neibu yu waibu zhuangzhi ， bingqie jujue wu quanxian de xingcheng tichu de qingqiu 。yinci lilun shang renhe yingyong chengshi zhixing shi de cuowu ， dou bu keneng rang xitong - { zh - hant :dang ji; zh - hans : bengkui } - 。\n \n lingyifangmian ， weiruan duiyu geng qiangli de zuoye xitong husheng de huiying bian shi Windows NT yu 1993nian de mianshi 。\n \n 1983nian kaishi weiruan jiu xiang yao wei MS - DOS jiangou yige tuxinghua de zuoye xitong zhong caozuo xitong zhineng buting zhixing ziji de guanli chengshi bing haojin xitong ziyuan de zhuangtai ， qita shiyongzhe huo yingti de chengshi jie wufa zhixing 。xingcheng guanli tongchang shijian le fenshi de gainian ， dabufen de caozuo xitong keyi liyong zhiding butong de tequan dengji （ priority ） ， wei meige xingcheng gaibian suo zhan de fenshi bili 。tequan yue gao de xingcheng ， zhixing youxian shunxu yue gao ， danwei shijian nei zhan de bili ye yue gao 。hudongshi caozuo xitong ye tigong mouzhong chengdu de huikui jizhi ， rang zhijie yu shiyongzhe hudong de xingcheng yongyou jiao gao de tequanzhi 。\n \n chule xingcheng guanli zhiwai ， caozuo xitong shang you danfu qi xingcheng jian tongxun （ IPC ） 、 xingcheng yichang zhongzhi chuli yiji sisuo （ Dead Lock ） zhence ji chuli deng jiaowei jianshen de wenti 。\n \n zai xingcheng zhixia shang you zhixingxu de wenti ， danshi dabufen de caozuo xitong bingbu hui chuli zhixing xusuo zaoyu de wenti ， tongchang caozuo xitong jinzhiyu tigong yi zu API rang shiyongzhe zixing caozuo huo touguo xuni jiqi de guanli jizhi kongzhi zhixing xu zhijian de hudong 。\n \n genju pajinsen dinglv ： 「 ni gei chengxu zai duo neicun ， chengxu ye hui xiangjinbanfa haoguang 」 ， yinci chengshi shejishi tongchang xiwang xitong gei ta wuxianliang qie wuxian kuai de jiyiti 。dabufen de xiandai diannao jiyiti jiagou dou shi jiecengshi de ， zui kuaiqie shuliang zuishao de zancunqi weishou ， ranhou shi kuaiqu 、 jiyiti yiji zui man de cidie chucun zhuangzhi 。er caozuo xitong de jiyiti guanli tigong xunzhao keyong de jiyi kongjian 、 peizhi yu shifang jiyi kongjian yiji jiaohuan jiyiti he disu chucun zhuangzhi de nei hanwu …… deng gongneng 。cilei you bei chengzuo xuni jiyiti guanli de gongneng dafu zengjia meige xingcheng ke huode de jiyi kongjian （ tongchang shi 4GB ， jishi shijishang RAM de shuliang yuanshao yu zhe shumu ） 。raner zhe ye dailai le weifu jiangdi zhixing xiaolv de quedian ， yanzhong shi shenzhi ye hui daozhi xingcheng bengkui 。\n \n jiyiti guanli de ling yige zhongdian huodong jiushi jieyou CPU de bangzhu lai guanli xuni weizhi 。ruguo tongshi you xuduo xingcheng chucunyu jiyi zhuangzhi shang ， zuoye xitong bixu fangzhi tamen huxiang ganrao duifang de jiyiti neirong （ chufei touguo mouxie xieding zai ke kongzhi de fanwei xia caozuo ， bing xianzhi ke cunqu de jiyiti fanwei ） 。fenge jiyiti kongjian keyi dacheng mubiao 。meige xingcheng zhi hui kandao zhengge jiyiti kongjian （ cong 0 dao jiyiti kongjian de zuida shangxian ） bei peizhi gei ta ziji （ dangran ， youxie weizhi bei caozuo xitong baoliu er jinzhi cunqu ） 。CPUshi xiancun le ji ge biaoyi bidui xuni weizhi yu shiji jiyiti weizhi ， zhezhong fangfa chengwei fenye peizhi 。\n \n jieyou dui meige xingcheng chansheng fenkai duli de weizhi kongjian ， caozuo xitong ye keyi qingyi di yi ci shifang mou xingcheng suo zhanju de suoyou jiyiti 。ruguo zhege xingcheng bu shifang jiyiti ， caozuo xitong keyi jieshu xingcheng bing jiang jiyiti zidong shifang 。\n \n suowei de dangan xitong ， tongchang zhicheng guanli cidie ziliao de xitong ， ke jiang ziliao yi mulu huo dangan de xingshi chucun 。meige dangan xitong dou you ziji de teshu geshi yu gongneng ， liru rizhi guanli huo bu xu cidie zhongzheng 。\n \n caozuo xitong yongyou xuduo zhong neijian dangan xitong 。liru Linux yongyou feichang guangfan de neijian dangan xitong ， ruext 2 、 ext 3 、 ext 4 、 Reiser FS 、 Reiser 4 、 GFS 、 GFS 2 、 OC FS 、 OC FS 2 、 N I LFS yu Google dangan xitong 。Linux ye zhiyuan fei yuansheng dangan xitong ， liru XFS 、 JFS 、 FAT jiazu yu NT FS 。lingyifangmian ， Windows neng zhiyuan de dangan xitong zhi you FAT12 、 FAT16 、 FAT32 、 EX FAT yu NT FS 。NT FS xitong shi Windows shang zui kekao yu zui you xiaolv de dangan xitong 。qita de FAT jiazu dou bi NT FS laojiu ， qie duiyu dangan changdu yu fenge cidie nengli dou you hen da xianzhi ， yinci zaocheng henduo wenti 。er UN IX de dangan xitong duoban shi UFS ， er UN IX zhong de yige fenzhi Solaris zuijin ze kaishi zhiyuan yi zhong xinshi de ZFS 。\n \n dabufen shangshu de dangan xitong dou you liang zhong jianzhi fangfa 。xitong keyi yi rizhishi huo feirizhishi jianzhi 。rizhishi dangan xitong keyi yi jiao anquan de shoufa zhixing xitong huifu 。ruguo yige meiyou rizhishi jianzhi de dangan xitong yushang turan de xitong bengkui ， daozhi ziliao jianli zai yiban shi tingdun ， ze ci xitong xuyao teshu de dangan xitong jiancha gongju caineng fuyuan ； rizhishi ze ke zidong huifu 。weiruan de NT FS yu Linux de ext 3 、 ext 4 、 reiser FS yu JFS dou shi rizhishi dangan xitong 。\n \n meige dangan xitong dou shizuo xiangsi de mulu ／zi mulu jiagou ， dan zai xiangsi zhixia ye you xuduo butongdian 。weiruan shiyong 「 \\ 」 fuhao yi jianli mulu ／zi mulu guanxi ， qie dangan mingcheng hulve qi daxiao xie chayi ； UN IX xitong ze shi yi 「 / 」 jianli mulu jiagou ， qie dangan mingcheng daxiao xie you chayi 。( qishi zheshi gei xitong diaoyong de ， \" / \" huo \" \\ \" bingbu shiji cunzai yingdie ) \n\n xuduo xiandai de caozuo xitong dou jubei caozuo zhuliu wanglu tongxun xieding TCP / IP de nengli 。yejiushishuo zheyang de zuoye xitong keyi jinru wanglu shijie ， bingqie yu qita xitong fenxiang zhuru dangan 、 yinbiaoji yu saomiaoqi deng ziyuan 。\n \n xuduo caozuo xitong ye zhiyuan duo ge guoqu wanglu qimeng shidai de ge lu wanglu tongxun xieding ， liru IBM jianli de xitong wanglu jiagou 、 DEC zai ta suo shengchan de xitong suo sheding de jiagou yu weiruan wei Windows zhizuo de teshu tongxun xieding 。haiyou xuduo weile teshu gongneng er yanfa de tongxun xieding ， liru keyi zai wanglu shang tigong dangan cunqu gongneng de NFS xitong 。xianjin daliang yongyu yingyin chuanliu （ Streaming media ） ji youxi xunxi chuansong de UDP xieding deng 。\n \n daduoshu caozuo xitong dou hanyou mouzhong chengdu de zixun anquan jizhi 。zixun anquan jizhi zhuyao jiyu liang da linian ： \n\n chule yunxu ／ jujue xingshi de anquan jizhi ， yige gao anquan dengji de xitong ye hui tigong jilu xuanxiang ， yunxu jilu gezhong qingqiu dui ziyuan cunqu de xingwei （ liru 「 shui cengjing du le zhege dangan ？ 」 ） 。\n \n zhaoyinyu junfang yu shangye zuzhi jiang mingan ziliao jilu zai diannao shang ， anquan jizhi zai caozuo xitong lishi shang shi yige bei changjiu guanzhu yu taolun de wenti 。meiguo guofangbu （ DoD ） bian chuangli le 《 kexin laizhijisuanji xitong pingjian chengxu 》 （ ） ， ci shouce queli le pingjian anquan jizhi chengxiao de jiben yuanze 。zhe dui caozuo xitong zuozhe laishuo feichang zhongyao ， yinwei TCSEC shi yongyu pingjian 、 fenlei yu xuanba chuyong yu chuli 、 chucun yu huoqu mingan huo jimi ziliao de diannao xitong de biaozhun chengxu 。\n \n neibu zixun anquan ke shiwei fangzhi zhengzai zhixing de chengshi renyi cunqu xitong ziyuan de shouduan 。daduo caozuo xitong rang putong chengshi ke zhijie caozuo diannao de CPU ， suoyi chansheng le yixie wenti ， liru zenyang ba ke ru caozuo xitong yiyang chuli shiwu 、 zhixing tongyang teshu zhiling de chengshi qiangpo tingzhi ， bijing zai ci qingjing xia ， caozuo xitong ye zhishi ling yige pingqipingzuo de chengshi 。wei tongyong caozuo xitong suo shengchan de CPU tongchang yu yingti cengji shang shijian le yiding chengdu de teshu zhiling baohu gainian 。tongchang tequan cengji jiao di de chengshi xiangyao zhixing mouxie teshu zhiling shi hui bei zuduan ， liru zhijie cunqu xiangshi yingdie zhilei de waibu zhuangzhi 。yinci ， chengshi bixu de jingyou xunwen caozuo xitong ， rang caozuo xitong zhixing teshu zhiling lai cunqu cidie 。yinci caozuo xitong jiu you jihui jiancha ci chengshi de shibie shenfen ， bing yici jieshou huo jujue ta de qingqiu 。\n \n zai bu zhiyuan teshu zhiling jiagou de yingti shang ， ling yige ye shi weiyi de baohu fangfa ， ze shi caozuo xitong bingbu zhijie liyong CPU zhixing shiyongzhe de chengshi ， ershi jieyou moni yige CPU huo tigong yi P - codeji xitong （ weidaima zhixingji ） ， xiangshi Java yiyang rang chengshi zai xuni jiqi shang zhixing 。\n \n neibu anquan jizhi zai duo shiyongzhe diannao shang tebie zhongyao ： ta yunxu meige xitong shiyongzhe yongyou ziji geren de dangan yu mulu ， qie qita shiyongzhe bu neng renyi cunqu huo shanchu 。yinwei renhe chengshi dou keneng raoguo caozuo xitong de jiankong ， geng you keneng rao guo celu chengshi de jiankong ， yongyou qiangzhili de neibu anquan jizhi zai celu qidong shi ye feichang zhongyao 。\n \n tongchang yige zuoye xitong hui wei qita wanglu shang de diannao huo shiyongzhe tigong （ zhuchi ） gezhong fuwu 。zhexie fuwu tongchang jieyou duankou huo caozuo xitong wanglu dizhi hou de shuzi cunqudian tigong 。tongchang ci fuwu baokuo tigong dangan gongxiang （ NFS ） 、 lieyin gongxiang 、 dianzi youjian 、 wangye fuwu yu dangan chuanshu xieding （ FTP ） 。\n waibu zixun anquan de zui qianxian ， shi zhuru fanghuoqiang deng de yingti zhuangzhi 。zai caozuo xitong neibu ye chang shezhi xuduo zhonglei de ruanti fanghuoqiang 。ruanti fanghuoqiang ke sheding jieshou huo jujue zai caozuo xitong shang zhixing de fuwu yu waijie de lianxian 。yinci renhe ren dou keyi anzhuang bing zhixing mouxie bu anquan de wanglu fuwu ， liru Telnet huo FTP ， bingqie sheding chule mouxie ziyong tongdao zhiwai zudang qita suoyou lianxian ， yi dacheng fangdu buliang lianxian de jizhi 。\n \n jinri dabufen de caozuo xitong dou baohan tuxing yonghu jiemian （ GUI ） 。you ji lei jiao jiu de caozuo xitong jiang tuxinghua shiyongzhe jiemian yu hexin jinmi jiehe ， liru zui zao de Windows yu Mac OS shizuo chanpin 。ci zhong shoufa ke tigong jiao kuaisu de tuxing huiying nengli ， qie shizuo shi bu xu qiege mozu yiner jiaowei shenggong ， danshi hui you qianglie fuzuoyong ， liru tuxing xitong bengkui jiang daozhi zhengge xitong bengkui ， liru - {A | zh-cn : lan pingsiji ; zh - tw : lanbai dangji huamian ; zh -hk :BSOD} - 。xuduo jindai de caozuo xitong yi mozuhua ， jiang tuxing jiemian de zixitong yu hexin fenkai （ yi zhi Linux yu Mac OS X yuanxian jiushi ruci sheji ， er mouxie kuochong banben de Windows zhongyu ye caiyong ci shoufa ） 。\n \n xuduo caozuo xitong yunxu shiyongzhe anzhuang huo chuangzao renhe tamen xihuan de tuxing yonghu jiemian 。dabufen de Unix yu Unix yansheng xitong （ BSD 、 Linux yu Minix ） tongchang hui anzhuang X Window xitong peihe GNOME huo KDE zhuomian huanjing 。er mouxie caozuo xitong jiu meiyou zheme tanxing de tuxinghua shiyongzhe jiemian ， liru Windows 。zhe lei de caozuo xitong zhineng touguo waijia de chengshi lai gaibian qi tuxinghua shiyongzhe jiemian ， shenzhi genben zhineng gaibian zhuru xuandan fengge huo yanse peizhi deng bufen 。\n \ntu xinghua shiyongzhe jiemian yu shi bingjin ， liru Windows zai meici xin banben shangshi shi jiu hui jiang qi tuxinghua shiyongzhe jiemian gaitouhuanmian ， er Mac OS de GUI ye zai Mac OS X shangshi shi chuxian zhongda zhuanbian 。\n \n suowei de qudong chengshi （ Device driver ） shi zhi mou lei sheji lai yu yingti hudong de diannao ruanti 。tongchang shi yi sheji wanshan de zhuangzhi hudong jiemian ， liyong yu ci yingti lianjie de diannao huipailiu huo tongxunzi xitong ， tigong duici zhuangzhi xialing yu jieshou zixun de gongneng ； yiji zuizhong mudi ， jiang xunxi tigong gei caozuo xitong huo yingyong chengshi 。qudong chengshi shi zhendui teding yingti yu teding caozuo xitong sheji de ruanti ， tongchang yi zuoye xitong hexin mozu 、 yingyong ruantibao huo putong diannao chengshi de xingshi zai caozuo xitong hexin dixia zhixing ， yi dadao tongtoushun changdi yu yingti hudong de xiaoguo ， qie tigong yingti zai chuli feitongbu de shijian yilaixing jiemian （ asynchronous time-dependent hardware interface ） shi suoxu de zhongduan chuli changshi 。\n \n sheji qudong chengshi de zhuyao mudi zaiyu caozuo chouxianghua ， renhe yingti mozu ， ji shi shi tongyi lei de zhuangzhi ， zai yingti shejimian shang ye you juda chayi 。changshang tuichu de jiao xin mozu tongchang geng kekao geng you xiaolv ， kongzhi fangfa ye hui yousuo butong 。diannao yuqi caozuo xitong meimei bu neng yuqi naxie xianyou yu xin zhuangzhi de bianyi zhi chu ，  Linux \n\nLinux （ ） shi yi zhong ziyou he kaifang yuanma de leiUN IX zuoye xitong 。gai caozuo xitong de neihe you linnasi·tuowazi zai 1991nian 10yue 5ri shouci fabu ， zai jiashang shiyongzhe kongjian de yingyong chengshi zhihou ， chengwei Linux zuoye xitong 。Linux ye shi ziyou ruanjian he kaifangyuan daima ruanjian fazhan zhong zui zhuming de lizi 。zhiyao zunxun GNU tongyong gonggong xukezheng （ GPL ） ， renhe geren he jigou dou keyi ziyou di shiyong Linux de suoyou di cengyuan daima ， ye keyi ziyou di xiugai he zai fabu 。daduoshu Linux xitong hai baokuo xiang tigong GUI de X Window zhilei de chengxu 。chule yibufen zhuanjia zhiwai ， daduoshu ren dou shi zhijie shiyong Linux faxingban ， er bushi ziji xuanze mei yiyang zujian huo zixing shezhi 。\n\nLinux yange laishuo shi danzhi zuoye xitong de neihe ， yin zuoye xitong zhong baohan le xuduo yonghu tuxing jiemian he qita shiyong gongju 。rujin Linux changyong lai zhi jiyu Linux de wanzheng caozuo xitong ， neihe ze gai yi Linux nei hecheng zhi 。youyu zhexie zhichi yonghu kongjian de xitong gongju heku zhuyao you lichade·situoman yu 1983nian faqi de GNU jihua tigong ， ziyou ruanjian jijinhui tiyi jiang qi zuhe xitong mingming wei GNU / Linux ， dan Linux bu shuyu GNU jihua ， zhege mingcheng bingmeiyou dedao shequn de yizhi rentong 。\n\nLinux zuichu shi zuowei zhichi yingteerx86 jiagou de geren diannao de yige ziyou caozuo xitong 。muqian Linux yijing bei yizhi dao geng duo de jisuanji yingjian pingtai ， yuanyuan chaochu qita renhe caozuo xitong 。Linux keyi yunxing zai fuwuqi he qita daxing pingtai zhishang ， ru daxing jisuanji he chaoji jisuanji 。shijie shang 500 ge zui kuai de chaoji jisuanji 90％ yishang yunxing Linux faxingban huo bianzhong ， baokuo zui kuai de qian10 ming chaoji diannao yunxing de dou shi jiyu Linux neihe de caozuo xitong 。Linux ye guangfan yingyong zai qianrushi xitong shang ， ru shouji （ Mobile Phone ） 、 pingban diannao （ Tablet ） 、 luyouqi （ Router ） 、 dianshi （ TV ） he dianzi youxiji deng 。zai yidong shebei shang guangfan shiyong de Android caozuo xitong jiushi jianli zai Linux neihe zhishang 。\n \n tongchang qingkuang xia ， Linux bei dabao cheng gong geren jisuanji he fuwuqi shiyong de Linux faxingban ， yixie liuxing de zhuliu Linux fabuban ， baokuo Debian （ jiqi yansheng banben Ubuntu 、 Linux Mint ） 、 Fedora （ jiqi xiangguan banben Red Hat Enterprise Linux 、 CentOS ） he openSUSE deng 。Linux faxingban baohan Linux neihe he zhicheng neihe de shiyong chengxu heku ， tongchang hai daiyou daliang keyi manzu gelei xuqiu de yingyong chengxu 。geren jisuanji shiyong de Linux faxingban tongchang baohan X Window he yige xiangying de zhuomian huanjing ， ru GNOME huo KDE 。zhuomian Linux caozuo xitong changyong de yingyong chengxu ， baokuo Firefox wangye liulanqi 、 LibreOffice bangong ruanjian 、 GI MPtu xiang chuli gongju deng 。youyu Linux shi ziyou ruanjian ， renhe ren dou keyi chuangjian yige fuhe ziji xuqiu de Linux faxingban 。\n \n genju tuowazi de shuofa ， Linux de fayin he 「 Minix 」 shi yayun de 。\n \n 「 Li 」 zhong 「 i 」 de fayin leisi yu 「 Minix 」 zhong 「 i 」 de fayin ， er 「 nux 」 zhong 「 u 」 de fayin leisi yu yingwen danci 「 profess 」 zhong 「 o 」 de fayin 。yizhao guoji yinbiao yinggai shi ['linэks ][ ˈl ɪnəks] 。\n \n ciwai you yi fen linnasi·tuowazi benren shuohua de luyin ， luyin neirong wei 「 Hello , this is Linus Torvalds , and I pronounce Linux as \" Linux \" 」 ， ye biaoming le zuozhe dui danci de dufa 。\n \nUN IX caozuo xitong （ ） ， shi meiguo AT&T gongsi beier shiyanshi yu 1969nian wancheng de caozuo xitong 。zui zao you ken·tangpuxun （ Ken Thompson ） ， dannisi·liqi （ Dennis Ritchie ） ， daogelasi·maikeluoyi （ Douglas McIlroy ） ， he qiaoyi·ousangna yu 1969nian zai AT & Tbeier shiyanshi kaifa 。yu 1971nian shouci fabu ， zuichu shi wanquan yong huibian yuyan bianxie 。houlai ， zai 1973nian yong yige zhongyao de kaituoxing de fangfa ， Unix bei dannisi·liqi yong biancheng yuyanC （ neihe he I / Oliwai ） chongxin bianxie 。gaoji yuyan bianxie de caozuo xitong juyou geng jia de jianrongxing ， neng geng rongyi di yizhi dao butong de jisuanji pingtai 。\n \n 1983nian ， lichade·maxiu·situoman chuangli GNU jihua 。zhege jihua you yige mubiao ， shi weile fazhan yige wanquan ziyou de lei Unix zuoye xitong 。zi 1984nian faqi zhege jihua yilai ， zai 1985nian ， lichade·maxiu·situoman faqi ziyou ruanti jijinhui bingqie zai 1989nian zhuanxie GPL 。1990niandai zaoqi ， GNU kaishi daliang di chansheng huo shouji gezhong xitong suo bibei de yuanjian ， xiangshi —— hanshi ku 、 bianyiqi 、 zhencuo gongju 、 wenzi bianjiqi ， yiji yige Unix de shiyongzhe jiemian （ Unix shell ） —— danshi xiang yixie diceng huanjing ， ru yingti qudong 、 shouhu jincheng 、 xitong hexin （ kernel ） rengran bu wanzheng he xianyu tingdun ， GNU jihua zhong shi zai Machwei neihe de jiagou zhishang kaifa xitong hexin ， ye jiushi suowei de GNU Hurd ， danshi zhege jiyu Mach de sheji yichang fuza ， fazhan jindu ze xiangdui huanman 。linnasi·tuowazi ceng shuo guo ruguo GNU hexin zai 1991nian shi keyi yong ， ta bu hui ziji qu xie yige 。\n \n 386BSD sheji de falv wenti zhidao 1992nian hai meiyou jiejue ， NetBSD he FreeB SD shi 386BSD de houyi ， zaoyu Linux 。linnasi·tuowazi ceng shuo ， dangshi ruguo you keyong de 386BSD ， ta jiu keneng bu hui bianxie Linux 。\n \n M I NIX shi yige qingliang xiaoxing bing caiyong weinei he( Micro -Kernel) jiagou de lei Unix zuoye xitong ， shi andelu·situerte·taneng baomu wei zai diannao kexue yongzuo jiaoxue er sheji de 。\n \n 1991nian ， linnasi·tuowazi zai heerxinji daxue shangxue shi ， dui zuoye xitong hen haoqi 。ta dui MIN IX zhi yunxu zai jiaoyu shang shiyong hen buman （ zai dangshi M I NIX bu yunxu bei yongzuo renhe shangye shiyong ） ， yushi ta bian kaishi xie ta ziji de zuoye xitong ， zhejiu shi houlai de Linux hexin 。\n \n linnasi·tuowazi kaishi zai MIN IX shang kaifa Linux neihe ， wei MINI Xxie de ruanti ye keyi zai Linux nei heshang shiyong 。houlai shiyong GNU ruanti daiti M I NIX de ruanti ， yinwei shiyong cong GNU xitong lai de yuanshima keyi ziyou shiyong ， zhe dui Linux de fazhan shi youyi 。shiyong GNU GPL xieyi de yuanshima keyi bei qita xiangmu suo shiyong ， zhiyao zhexie xiangmu shiyong tongyang de xieyi fabu 。weile rang Linux keyi zai shangye shang shiyong ， linnasi·tuowazi jueding genggai ta yuanlai de xieyi （ zhege xieyihui xianzhi shangye shiyong ） ， yi GNU GPL xieyi lai daiti 。zhihou xuduo kaifazhe zhili ronghe GNU yuansu dao Linux zhong ， zuochu yige you wanzheng gongneng de 、 ziyou de zuoye xitong 。\n\nLinux de diyi ge banben zai 1991nian 9yue bei daxue FTP server guanliyuan - { Ari Lemmke} - fabu zai Internet shang ， zuichu Torvalds cheng zhege hexin de mingcheng wei \" Freax \" ， yisi shi ziyou （ \" free\" ） he qiyi （ \" freak\" ） de jiehe zi ， bingqie fushang \" X \" zhege changyong de zimu ， yi peihe suowei de lei Unix de xitong 。danshi FTP cifuqi guanliyuan xian yuanlai de mingming 「 Freax 」 de mingcheng bu haoting ， ba hexin de chenghu gaicheng 「 Linux 」 ， dangshi hexin wenjian suozai de ciqu ， bingbu juxianyu ext wenjian xitong ） 。\n \n jintian you Linus Torvalds dailing xia ， zhongduo kaifa gongtong canyu kaifa he weihu Linux neihe 。lichade·situoman lingdao zujian ， yiji qita xingshi de ruanjianbao guanli xitong ruanjian 。\n \n jiyu Linux de xitong shi yige mokuaihua de lei Unix caozuo xitong 。Linux caozuo xitong de dabufen sheji sixiang laiyuanyu 20 shiji 70niandai dao 80niandai de Unix caozuo xitong suo jianli de jiben sheji sixiang 。Linux xitong shiyong hongnei he ， you Linux neihe fuze chuli jincheng kongzhi 、 wangluo ， yiji waiwei shebei he \n\nLinux faxing banzhi de jiushi tongchang suo shuo de 「 Linux zuoye xitong 」 ， ta yiban shi you yixie zuzhi 、 tuanti 、 gongsi huozhe geren zhizuo bing faxing de 。Linux neihe zhuyao zuowei Linux xiaoshou 。\n \n \" Linux \" de zhuce shangbiao shi Linus Torvalds suoyou de 。zheshi youyu zai 1996nian ， yige mingzi jiaozuo William R .Della Croce de lvshi kaishi xiang gege Linux fabushang faxin ， shengming ta yongyou \" Linux \" shangbiao de suoyouquan ， bingqie yaoqiu gege fabushang zhifu banshui ， zhexie faxingshang jiti jinxing shangsu ， yaoqiu jiang gai zhuce shangbiao chongxin fenpei gei Linus Torvalds 。Linus Torvalds yizai shengming Linux shi ziyouqie mianfei de ， ta benren keyi maidiao ， dan Linux juebu neng mai 。\n \n “ GNU / Linux ” ci mingcheng shi GNU jihua de zhichizhe yu kaifazhe ， tebieshi qi chuanglizhe lichade·situoman duiyu Linux zuoye xitong de zhuzhang 。youyu cilei caozuo xitong shiyong le zhongduo GNU chengxu ， baohan Bash （ Shellchengshi ） 、 hanshi ku 、 bianyiqi dengdeng zuowei Linux hexin shang de xitong taojian ， lichade·situoman renwei yinggai jiang gai caozuo xitong chengwei 「 GNU / Linux 」 huo 「 GNU + Linux 」 jiaowei qiadang ， dan xianjin duoshu ren reng cheng qi wei Linux 。jiu 1997nian zhiqian de Linux laikan ， yi jian CD-ROM de gongyingshang suo tigong de ziliao xianshi zai tamen de “ Linux faxingban ” zhong ， GNU ruanjian suo zhan zui da de bizhong ， dayue zhan quan buyuan daima de 28% ， qie hai baokuo yixie guanjian de bujian ， ruguo meiyou zhexie bujian ， xitong jiu wufa gongzuo ， er Linux benshen zhan dayue 3% 。\n\nLinux shequn xitong mingcheng 。bingqie renwei Linux bingbu shuyu GNU jihua de yi bufen ， situoman zhidao 1990niandai zhongqi Linux kaishi liuxing hou cai yaoqiu gengming 。you bufen Linux taojian ， ru Debian ， caiyong le 「 GNU / Linux 」 de chenghu 。dan daduoshu shangye Linux taojian yiran jiang caozuo xitong chengwei Linux 。er youxie ren ze renwei 「 caozuo xitong 」 yi ci zhi de zhishi xitong de neihe (Kernel) ， qita chengxu dou zhineng suanshi yingyong ruanjian ， yiner ， gai caozuo xitong ying jiao Linux ， dan Linux xitong taojian shi zai Linux neihe de jichu shang jiaru gezhong GNU ruanjian taojian jihe er cheng de 。\n \n zai zhe liang ge zhuyao mingcheng zhiwai ， ye you qita mingcheng de tiyi 。1992nian ， Yggdrasil Linux zhuzhang mingming wei Linux / GNU / X ， yinwei chule GNU jihua ruanti zhiwai ， henduo Linux hai caiyong le Xshichuang xitong 。\n \n \n \n \n \n 
 GNU jihua \n \n GNU jihua （ ） ， you yiwei genu jihua ， shi yige ziyou ruanti jiti xiezuo jihua ， 1983nian 9yue 27ri you lichade·situoman zai masheng ligong xueyuan gongkai faqi 。ta de mubiao shi chuangjian yi tao wanquan ziyou de caozuo xitong ， chengwei GNU 。lichade·situoman zui zao zai net.unix - wizards xinwen zushang gongbu gai xiaoxi ， bing fudai yi fen 《 GNU xuanyan 》 deng jieshi weihe faqi gai jihua de wenzhang ， qizhong yige liyou jiushi yao “ chongxian dangnian ruanjianjie hezuo huzhu de tuanjie jingshen ” 。\n \n GNU shi “ GNU 's Not Unix ” de digui suoxie 。wei bimian yu dancignu （ feizhou niuling ， fayin yu 「new 」 xiangtong ） hunxiao ， situoman xuanbu GNU fayin ying wei 「 Guh - NOO 」 （ ） ， yu 「 canoe 」 fayin xiangsi 。qizhong ， Emacs jiushi you zhege jihua fuhua erchu 。\n \nUN IX shi yi zhong guangfan shiyong de shangye caozuo xitong de mingcheng 。youyu GNU jiangyao shixian UN IX xitong de jiekou biaozhun ， yinci GNU jihua keyi fenbie kaifa butong de caozuo xitong 。GNU jihua caiyong le bufen dangshi yijing ke ziyou shiyong de ruanjian ， liru TeX paiban xitong he X Window shichuang xitong deng 。buguo GNU jihua ye kaifa le dapi qita de ziyou ruanjian ， zhexie ruanjian ye bei yizhi dao qita caozuo xitong pingtai shang ， liru Micros of t Windows 、 BSD jiazu 、 Solaris ji Mac OS 。\n \n wei baozheng GNU ruanjian keyi ziyou di “ shiyong 、 fuzhi 、 xiugai he fabu ” ， suoyou GNU ruanjian dou baohan yi fen zai jinzhi qitaren tianjia renhe xianzhi de qingkuang xia ， shouquan suoyou quanli gei renhe ren de xieyi tiaokuan ， GNU tongyong gonggong xukezheng （ GNU General Public License ， GPL ） 。zhege jiushi bei chengwei “ gonggong banquan ” de gainian 。GNU ye zhendui butong changhe ， tigong GNU kuan tongyong gonggong xukezheng yu GNU ziyou wendang xukezheng zhe liang zhong xieyi tiaokuan 。\n \n 1985nian ， lichade·situoman chuangli le ziyou ruanjian jijinhui lai wei GNU jihua tigong jishu 、 falv yiji caizheng zhichi 。jinguan GNU jihua dabufen shihou shi you geren ziyuan wuchang gongxian ， dan FSF youshi haishi hui pinqing chengxuyuan bangzhu bianxie 。dang GNU jihua kaishi zhujian huode chenggong shi ， yixie shangye gongsi kaishi jieru kaifa he jishu - { zh - hans : zhichi ; zh - hant : zhiyuan ;} - 。dangzhong zui zhuming de jiushi zhihou bei Red Hat jianbing de Cygnus Solutions 。\n \n dao le 1990nian ， GNU jihua yijing kaifa chu de ruanjian baokuo le yige gongneng qiangda de wenzi bianjiqi Emacs 、 Cyuyan bianyiqi GCC yiji dabufen UN IX xitong de chengxuku he gongju 。weiyi yiran meiyou wancheng de zhongyao zujian ， jiushi caozuo xitong de neihe （ chengwei HURD ） 。\n \n 1991nian ， linnasi·tuowazi bianxie chu le yu UN IX jianrong de Linux caozuo xitong neihe bing zai GPL xia fabu 。Linux zhihou zai wangshang guangfan liuchuan 。1992nian ， Linux yu qita GNU ruanjian jiehe ， wanquan ziyou de caozuo xitong zhengshi dansheng 。xuduo chengxuyuan canyu le Linux de kaifa yu xiugai ， ye jingchang jiang Linux dangcheng kaifa GNU jihua ruanti de pingtai 。gai caozuo xitong wangwang bei chengwei “ GNU / Linux ” huo jiancheng Linux 。dan Linux benshen bu shuyu GNU jihua de yi bufen ， GNU jihua ziji de neiheHurd yiran zai kaifa zhong ， muqian yijing fabu Beta banben 。\n \n xuduo UN IX xitong shang ye anzhuang le GNU ruanjian ， yinwei GNU ruanjian de zhiliang bi zhiqian UN IX de ruanjian haiyao hao 。GNU gongju hai bei guangfan di yizhi dao Windows he Mac OS shang 。\n \n GNU gongcheng shiji nian yilai yijing chengwei yige dui ruanjian kaifa zhuyao de yingxiang liliang ， chuangzao le wushu de zhongyao de gongju ， liru ： qiangjian de bianyiqi ， youli de wenben bianjiqi ， shenzhi yige quan gongneng de caozuo xitong 。zhege gongcheng shi cong 1984nian masheng ligong xueyuan de chengxuyuan lichade·situoman de xiangfa de lai de ， ta xiangyao jianli yige ziyou de 、 he UN IX leisi de caozuo huanjing 。cong nashi kaishi ， xuduo chengxuyuan juji qilai kaishi kaifa yige ziyou de 、 gao zhiliang 、 yi lijie de ruanjian 。\n \n yixia shi GNU jihua de zhengshi fayanren ： \n\n \n 
 ziyou ruanjian yundong \n \n ziyou ruanjian yundong （ ， jiancheng FSM huo FOSSM ） shi yige tuiguang yonghu you shiyong 、 fuzhi 、 yanjiu 、 xiugai he fenfa ruanjian deng quanli de shehui yundong 。jiejin he xiangguan de yundong baokuo kaifang yuanma yundong ji ziyou ruanjian de kaifang yuanma yundong 。zhe yundong gen 1970niandai de heike wenhua you yuanyuan ， er lichade·situoman shi gai yundong de zhuyao faqiren yiji jingshen lingxiu 。\n \n ziyou ruanjian yundong renshi renwei ziyou ruanjian de jingshen yingdang guanche dao suoyou ruanjian ： tamen renwei jinzhi jisuanji yonghu xingshi zhezhong ziyou shi budaode de xingwei 。licha·maxiu·situoman renwei fanmai bu fu daiyuan daima de erjinzhi ruanjian shi budaode de ， yinwei zheyang zuzhi le ruanjian yonghu xuexi yiji bangzhu qitaren de quanli 。raner muqian hai meiyou ruhe shixian ziyou ruanjian yundong zuizhong mubiao de gongshi 。youxie ren renwei yingdang shiyong falv shouduan qiangzhi ruanjian gongyingshang tigong yuan daima ； youxie ze renwei yingdang tongguo dizhi zhuanyou ruanjian lai dadao mudi 。haiyou yixie ren ze renwei shijian jiang zhengming ， ziyou ruanjian zuizhong zai zhiliang shang yao bi zhuanyou ruanjian lveshengyichou ， bing hui zai ziyou shichang shang qude shengli 。\n \n bufen ziyou ruanjian yundong renshi ye renwei qita shou zhuanliquan baohu de chanpin ye yingdang ziyouhua 。haiyou yixie renshi ze renwei you bufen ziyuan bu yingdang bei ziyou genggai ， liru GNU tongyong gonggong xieyi zhengshu ， xiaoshuo deng 。\n \n zhege yundong de linian zaiyu diannao de shiyong bu yinggai zuai renji hezuo 。geng zhijie di shuo ， zhege yundong daibiao zhuju juezhuan you ruanti bing tuiguang ziyou ruanti 。ta de zhongji mubiao zaiyu jiefang wanglu shijie zhong de meige ren —— ji meige diannao shiyongzhe 。licha·situoman biaoming zhege xingdong zhizai tisheng er fei fangai keji de jinbu ， yinwei 「 zhe daibiao women keyi bimian chongfu wuyi de xitong biancheng ， er ba zhe fen jingli yong zai tuidong jishu gexin shangmian 。 」( \" It means that much wasteful duplication of system programming effort will be avoided .This effort can go instead in to advancing the state of the art .\" ) \n \n ziyou ruanti yundong de chengyuan xiangxin suoyou de ruanti shiyongzhe you xiangyou zhong lieju de ziyou 。xuduo chengyuan renwei jinzhi taren xiangyou zhexie ziyou shi budaode de ， ye xiangxin zai chuangzao yige shiyongzhe keyi huxiang bangzhu bing yongyou ziji duiyu diannao kongzhiquan de shehui ， zhexie ziyou shi bixu de 。\n \n raner ， you yixie ziyou ruanti shiyongzhe he chengshi shejishi bu yi zuowei tamen de lundian 。\n \n suiran shehui bianqian hui shi yige keji bianqian xia fei keyi zaocheng de fuchanwu ， xin keji de changyizhe jingchang xuanchuan zhexie xin jishu jiu shehui zhengmian yingxiang yige gongju 。shenghe xizhouli daxue de jiaoshou Joel West jieshi le xuduo ziyou yuanshima yundong de linian 。ruguo jiashe keji bujin dui shehui bianqian zaocheng yingxiang ， bing cong keji jinbu zhudao shehui bianqian de jiaodu lai kandai ， jinzhi teding renyuan shiyong zhexie keji shi daode de ma ？yinci —zong shi bu neng zaocheng like de gaibian — ziyou ruanti yundong haishi xiwang huanxing renmen zhege yundong suo neng zaocheng de yingxiang ， yinwei neng zaocheng dui xianshi shehui de yingxiang 。juli laishuo ： yu meiyou diannao shi xiangbi ， diannao gei le women geng duo ziyou ， dan zhexie keji meijie jiujing shi dailai ziyou 、 huo jin fuyu shaoshu ren tequan ？zheyang de daode zhenglun ruhe qu de yige zhezhong de banfa dui ziyou ruanti yundong shi ge nanti 。\n \n ziyou ruanti jijinhui jianxin suoyou de ruanti xuyao shuoming wenjian ， tebieshi zhoudao de gongchengshi ying zuodao neng gengxin shuomingshu yi fanying tamen dui ruanti de tiaozheng ， dan tamen renwei dui xiugai qita zhuzuo de ziyou benshen shi xiangduici yao de 。zai ziyou ruanti yundong zhong jijinhui tebie qiangdiao tigong cilei wenjian de mubiao 。ziyou ruanti yundong de chengyuan ye changyi ju shiji yongtu de ruanti yinggai ziyou de \n \n \n ziyou ruanjian yundong de hexin gongzuo zhuanzhuyu ruanjian kaifa 。ziyou ruanjian yundong ye fandui zhuanyou ruanjian ， jujue anzhuang bu jiyu ziyou quanli de ruanjian 。genju situoerman xushu ， “ zai ruanjian lingyu bi zhuanyou chengxu weijing shouquan de kaobei geng zaogao de weiyi yi jian shi ， jiushi siyou ruanjian de shouquan fuben 。yinwei zheyang zuo tongyang shanghai qi zhengge yonghu qunti 。ciwai ， tongchang kaifashang ， zhege xiee de fanzuiren ， jiu ke congzhong huoli 。\n ziyou ruanjian yundong de yixie zhichizhemen hui zhanyong gongzhong yanjiang ， huozhe zhuchi ruanjian xiangguan huiyi ， yi tigao ruanjian de ziyou yishi 。zhe bei shiwei xiangdang zhongyao ， yinwei jieshou mianfei ruanjian de renmen ， wangwang bu zhidao ta shi mianfei ruanjian 。shaohou bian keneng hui jieshou feimianfei genghuan ， huo jiang zengjia bushi mianfei ruanjian de fudai ruanjian 。\n magelite·S·ailiaote ， yige zai zai jiazhou daxue ouwen fenxiao de ruanjian yanjiuzhe 。bujin liechu le keneng laizi ziyou ruanjian yundong de xuduo haochu ， ta hai shengcheng ， ta benzhi shang shi yao jiyu meige ren pingdeng de jihui liyong hulianwang 。jiashe de 。genju xuduo tuidong youguan ziyou ruanjian yundong de xuezhe de renshi ， ruguo renmen xiangyao shengcun zai tongxin he quanqiu yuanzhu gengjia gongcun de shijie ， name quanqiu ziyou ruanjian gengjia yinggai zhengqu yige weizhi 。zhege you GNU tonghuo yinfa de xiangfa ， shi cujin yige lijie dangdi he quanqiu shequ de liyi ， suowei “ hezuo huanjing ” de yi zhong changshi 。\n \n daliang de dizhi ruanjian zhuanli he zhuzuo quanfa kuozhang de youshui gongzuo yijing wancheng 。qita youshui ze zhijie zhuanzhuyu zhengfu jigou he zhengfu zizhu de xiangmu zhong suo shiyong de ziyou ruanjian 。\n
