de puji 。\n \n \n 
 cailiao kexue \n \n - {T | zh - hans : cailiao kexue ; zh - hant : cailiao kexue ; zh -sg : wuzhi kexue} - \n cailiao kexue ， you ming wei cailiao gongcheng ， sheji wuzhi de xingzhi jiqi zai gege kexue he gongchengxue lingyu de zhenghe yingyong ， shi yige yanjiu cailiao de zhibei huo jiagong gongyi 、 cailiao de weiguan jiegou yu cailiao hongguan xingneng sanzhe zhijian de xianghu guanxi de kualingyu xueke 。sheji de lilun baokuo guti wulixue ， cailiao huaxue ， yingyong wuli he huaxue ， yiji huaxue gongcheng ， jixie gongcheng ， tumu gongcheng he dianji gongcheng 。yu dianzi gongcheng jiehe ， ze yan shengchu dianzi cailiao ， yu jixie jiehe ze yan shengchu jiegou cailiao ， yu shengwuxue jiehe ze yansheng chushengwu cailiao dengdeng 。suizhe jinnianlai meiti jiang zhuyili daliang jizhong zai nami kexue shang ， cailiao kexue zai kexue yu gongchengxue lingyu yuelaiyue guangweirenzhi 。ta ye shi jianshi kexue he pohuai fenxi zhong de yige zhongyao zucheng bufen ， yihouzhe wei li ， ta shi fenxi gezhong feihang yiwai de guanjian 。jinri xuduo keji shang de wenti shou xianyu cailiao nenggou rongxu de jixian ， ye yinci ， zai ci lingyu de tupo zai weilai keji juyou zhibiaoxing de yingxiang 。cailiao kexue youzhe guangfan de yingyong qianjing 。\n \n zai ge shidai shang cailiao de xuanze wangwang jueding le gai shidai de fazhan ， xiangshi shiqi shidai 、 qingtongqi shidai 、 tieqi shidai he gongye geming jiushi mingxian de lizi 。cailiao kexue shi zui gulao de yingyong kexue ji gongchengxue zhiyi ， qichu bei yindao laizi taoci de jiagong he yejinxue de yanshen 。xiandai cailiao kexue yanjin laiziyu yejinxue 。zai shijiu shiji wanqi yi wei meiguo kexuejia yuexiya·jibusi faxian cailiao zai butong xiangtai zhijian de relixue xingzhi ， shide zai lijie cailiao xingzhi shang you zhongdaxing de tupo 。cailiao kexue yu qita lingyu de hezuo fazhan gemingxing keji ， xiangshi sujiao 、 bandaoti he 。\n \n zai 1960niandai qian ， xuduo cailiao kexuexi dou bei chengwei kuang yexi 。1960 hou dangshi meiguo gaodeng yanjiu jihua shu( Advanced Research Projects Agency ) ， xian wei guofang gaodeng yanjiu jihua shu( Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency ) ， weile cailiao kexue de jichu yanjiu yiji xunlian de guojia jihua ( “ to expand the national program of basic research and training in the materials science ” ) zai 1960niandai chuangli yixilie daxue shiyanshi ， jianli le cailiao kexue 。ci lingyu baohan taoci 、 juhewu 、 bandaoti 、 cixing cailiao 、 、 nai mi cailiao 。\n \n xiangjian qing zhi cailiao kejishi \n \n \n \n \n \n 
 nuobeierjiang \n\n nuobeierjiang （ ， ） ， shi genju ruidian huaxuejia aerfuleide·nuobeier de yizhu yu 1901nian kaishi meinian banfa de wu ge jiangxiang ， baokuo ： wuli 、 huaxue 、 shenglixue huo yixue 、 wenxue he heping 。1968nian ， ruidian zhongyang yinhang sheli le ruidian yinhang jinian nuobeier jingji kexuejiang ， tongcheng “ nuobeier jingjixue jiang ” 。nuobeierjiang pubian bei renwei shi suo banjiang de lingyu nei zui zhongyao de jiangxiang 。\n \n nuobeier zhongsheng wei qu ， yi wuzi si 。zai qi shishi qian ， qinxiongdi ye zaoyibu qushi 。dan ta de gailiang —— zhayao ， qude le zhongduo de keyan chengguo ， ye chenggong sheli xuduo gongchang shengchan ， leiji juda caifu 。\n \n youyu nuobeier zhongsheng zhuzhang hepingzhuyi ， ye yinci ta duiyu ziji gailiang de zhayao zuowei pohuai ji zhanzheng de yongtu shizhong gandao tongxin 。zai jijiang cishi zhiji ， nuobeier lixia le yizhu ： “ qing jiang wo de caichan bianzuo jijin ， meinian yong zhege jijin de lixi zuowei jiangjin ， jiangli naxie zai qian yi nian wei renlei zuochu zhuoyue gongxian de ren 。 ”genju ta de zhege yizhu ， cong 1901nian kaishi ， juyou guojixing de nuobeierjiang chuangli le ， fenbie jiangli 5 ge lingyu ： wulixue 、 huaxue 、 shenglixue huo yixue 、 wenxue 、 heping 。\n \n 1969nian ， ruidian chuzi zengshe ruidian yinhang jingjixue jiang ， tongcheng 「 nuobeier jingjixue jiang 」 。jinguan yu qianshu 5 zhong jiangxiang 「 hecheng nuobeierjiang 」 ， dan shijishang bushi nuobeier yizhu zhong juanzhu de jiangxiang 。\n \n \n jin50 nian yilai ， nuobeier jijinhui mingwen guiding ， bulunshi gonggong changhe haishi siren changhe ， timing guocheng he renxuan dou yao yange baomi ， baokuo timingzhe renxuan he bei timing zhe renxuan 。henduo ren zai gezhong changhe shengcheng ziji ceng yin mou chengguo er huode nuobeierjiang de timing dan wei huojiang ， yingshu yaoyan 。\n \n jiezhi 2016nian ， gongyou 911 geren he zuzhi （ 836 nan 、 49 nvji 26 ge zuzhi ） huode le 579 ge nuobeierjiang yu ruidian yinhang jingjixue jiang 。jiezhi 2012nian ， dezhu pingjun nianling 59 sui 。duoci huojiangzhe gong 4 ren ， duoci huojiang de zuzhi gong 2 ming ， heji gong 6 wei duoci huojiang de zuzhi yu xuezhe 。\n \n genju guanfang shuju ， 2015nian huo hepingjiang de tunixiya quanguo duihua sifang jituan bei jisuan wei 「 4 ge 」 zuzhi 。\n \n biaolie 「 bili 」 jin quzhi xiaoshudian hou 2 wei ， bing caiwu tiaojian shequfa jilu zhi 。\n genju huojiang shiguoji yu chushengdi ， jiezhi 2016nian 10yue 14ri ， geguo ge jiangxiang dezhu renshu de shijie qian 5 qiang ： \n\n xiabiao zhanshi 1901nian zhi 2018nian shijie ge gaoxiao nuobeierjiang renshu fenbu （ zhi zhanshi qian 30 ming ） 。\n \n<nowiki> *: </nowiki> \n\n<nowiki> * *: </nowiki> \n\n<nowiki> *** </nowiki> \n \n xuezhe bufen \n \n \n zuzhi bufen \n \n \n \n \n \n nuobeierjiang yuanze shang jin neng shouyu zai shizhe ， dan you san ci liwai 。yi wei 1931nian nuobeier wenxuejiang dezhu ailike·akesaier·kaerfeierte ， erwei 1961nian nuobeier hepingjiang dezhu dage·hamasheerde ， san wei 2011nian nuobeier shenglixue huo yixue jiang dezhulaerfu·sitanman 。\n \n renmen dui nuobeierjiang de zhengyidian ， chule zai ge jiang dezhu bixu shi san ren yixia de xianzhi wai ， haiyou bu bangei yi guoshi de ren ， lingwai haiyou nuobeierjiang bu sheli zhongyao de shuxue jiang 。\n \n 1919nian de nuobeier wulixue jiang dezhu yuehannisi·sitake ceng wei zishen liyi wei xitelei xiaolao ， nuobeier jijinhui wuquan shi huojiangzhe gaibian ziji de kanfa 。\n \n nuobeierjiang de guiju ： dezhu bixu shi san ren yixia ， ye chansheng guo zhengyi ， gaijiang xiang zhishi biaozhang zai kexue lingyu zhong you zhongda tupo de geren he xiaotuandui de 。buguo ye you liwai de shi nuobeierjiang zhong de hepingjiang ， fenbie zai 1917nian ， 1944nian ， 1963nian banfa gei le hongshizi guoji weiyuanhui zuzhi ， 2012nian banfa gei le ouzhou lianmeng zuzhi 。2013nian ze banfa gei le jinzhi huaxue wuqi zuzhi ， 2015nian you banfa gei tunixiya quanguo duihua sifang jituan 。\n \n nuobeierjiang zai duiyu wulixue jiang ji huaxue jiang de banfa zai xueshujie youshi ye hui yinqi zhengyi ， qizhong zuiwei zhuming de lizi shi aiyinsitan meiyou yin xiangduilun huode nuobeier wulixue jiang er zai 12nian hou cai yin guangdian xiaoying huojiang 。\n \n guanyu nuobeier jijinhui bu sheli shuxue jiang ， qizhong you yige liuchuan jiao guang de minjian chuanshuo shi nuobeier de qizi yu yi wei mingjiao leifulei （ Mittag - Leffler ） de shuxuejia you waiyu ， suoyi nuobeier benren yizhu zhong bu shezhi nuobeier shuxue jiang 。buguo zhege shuofa xianran bu shi ， yinwei nuobeier genben meiyou jiehun ， jiao keneng de yinsu wei dang shidai ， shuxue jin wei shangwei xingcheng yi you gaibian renlei shenghuo keneng de xianxue 。\n suizhu shuxue ji jisuanji lingyu de fazhan ， shuxuejie de feierzi jiang ji jisuanjijie de tuling jiang bei chengwei gai lingyu de “ nuobeierjiang ” 。\n \n nuobeierjiang ye bei yixie nvquan tuanti piping ， yinwei xiangjiaoyu nanxing ， nvxing zai nuobeier dejiang de renshu mingxian pian di ， rang yixie funv he nvquan tuanti piping nuobeierjiang you xingbie qishi zhi xian 。zhi 2014nian weizhi muqian nvxing zai nuobeier huode zuiduo jiangxiang de yi nian wei 2009nian 。\n \n 1989nian kaishi ， tangsenlutou meiguo zongbu meinian fabu 「 tangsenlu touyin wenguiguan jiang 」 yi yuce weilai de nuobeierjiang dezhu 。\n \n \n \n \n \n
